## Importance of Diet and Lifestyle During the First 1000 Days of a Child's Life Including Pregnancy

Throughout  your  pregnancy,  you  will  be  experiencing  many  physiological  and  psychological changes, during which adequate nutrition is required for your health as well as that of your baby. ǼɄȳ ɭȳɰɇɣȯ ɴɻȝɰɻɇɞȿ ʋɇɻɄ ʑɣɿɰ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ȝɞȯ ɿɞɻɇɗ ɻɄȳ ȨȝȨʑ ɇɴ ɻʋɣ ʑȳȝɰɴ ɣɗȯ ˉɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ̷̶̶̶ ȯȝʑɴˊ plays an important role in ensuring your child's adequate development and overall health. Your diet and lifestyle during this period are therefore critical and deserve your utmost attention [1] .

This chapter addresses a few aspects related to your diet and lifestyle during pregnancy, such as  adequate  gestational  weight  gain  (GWG),  healthy  eating,  in  addition  to  other  factors  of importance (vitamin/mineral supplementation, dietary and lifestyle management of pregnancyrelated complications, physical activity, oral health, mental health, eating disorders, emotional eating, and food safety). The last part of the chapter focuses on pregnant women who developed gestational diabetes, which is a form of diabetes that appears during pregnancy.

Some of the recommendations presented in this chapter are based on pregnancy trimesters. As you may have learned from your physician, your nine months of pregnancy are divided into three ɻɰɇɝȳɴɻȳɰɴʳ Ȩȳȿɇɞɞɇɞȿ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ȯȝʑ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ɗȝɴɻ ɝȳɞɴɻɰɿȝɗ ȩʑȩɗȳʳ ȝɴ Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋɴʴ ̷ st trimester: 0-13 weeks; 2 nd trimester: 14-26 weeks and 3 rd trimester: 27-40 weeks.

![Picture 79](images/SRC013/picture-079.png)

## Weight Gain During Pregnancy 02

The amount of weight that you gain during your pregnancy, also termed gestational weight gain ˉǂȌǂʳˊ ɇɴ ɣɞȳ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ Ⱦȝȩɻɣɰɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ ȿɰȳȝɻɗʑ ɇɞʠɿȳɞȩȳ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɣɿɻȩɣɝȳɴ [ 1 ] . Mothers who gain excessive weight are at a higher risk of developing certain complications during their pregnancy, such as high blood pressure and high blood sugar. They may also deliver large (macrosomic) babies who may be at increased risk for obesity and chronic diseases later in life. On the other hand, mothers with very low GWG are more likely to have early delivery (preterm) and small ȨȝȨɇȳɴ ʋɄɣ ɝȝʑ ȝɗɴɣ ɴɿʜȳɰ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɇɞȩɰȳȝɴȳȯ ȯɇɴȳȝɴȳ ɰɇɴɕ ɻɄɰɣɿȿɄɣɿɻ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɗɇʊȳɴ [2] . Not only does ǂȌǂ ȝʜȳȩɻ ɻɄȳ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʳ Ȩɿɻ ɇɻ ȝɗɴɣ Ʉȝɴ ȝ ɝȝɒɣɰ ɇɝɭȝȩɻ ɣɞ ʑɣɿɰ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ȝɴ ʋȳɗɗʲ Studies showed that gaining excessive weight during your pregnancy will increase the amount of weight you retain after pregnancy. This will increase your risk of obesity, type II diabetes, and cardiovascular diseases [3] .

The amount of weight you should aim to gain during your pregnancy depends to a large extent on your weight status before pregnancy (i.e., whether you had a normal body mass index (BMI) before  your  pregnancy  or  whether  you  were  underweight,  overweight,  or  obese)  (Refer  to Ơɭɭȳɞȯɇʐ ̷ ɻɣ ɗȳȝɰɞ ɝɣɰȳ ȝȨɣɿɻ ɻɄȳ ƫǞǊ ȩɗȝɴɴɇʟȩȝɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ʋȳɇȿɄɻ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑˊʲ ǼɄȳ ȝɝɣɿɞɻ of weight you should gain during your pregnancy will also depend on whether you are pregnant with only one baby (singleton pregnancy) or with twins (check tables 1 and 2, respectively).

As such, the recommended amount of weight gain during pregnancy is the highest for women who were underweight before pregnancy (BMI &lt;18.5 kg/m2). In contrast, the recommended amount  of  weight  gain  during  pregnancy  is  the  lowest  for  women  who  were  obese  before ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ˉƫǞǊ ˹ ̶̹ ɕȿʿɝ̸ˊʲ  Ǌɞ ɣɻɄȳɰ ʋɣɰȯɴʳ ɣȨȳɴȳ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ȝɰȳ ȝȯʊɇɴȳȯ ɻɣ ȿȝɇɞ ɗȳɴɴ ʋȳɇȿɄɻ throughout their pregnancy compared to women with a lower BMI. It is important to note that weight loss is not recommended during pregnancy, unless medically indicated. Instead, overweight and obese women are recommended to lose the excess weight before getting pregnant (never during the pregnancy itself).

If you are pregnant with one baby (singleton pregnancy), refer to T able 1, which provides you with weight gain recommendations based on your pre-pregnancy BMI. If you are pregnant with twins, refer to T able 2. In all cases, make sure to consult a dietitian to help you plan for your weight gain and diet during pregnancy.

![Picture 80](images/SRC013/picture-080.png)

Table 1. Recommendations for Gestational Weight Gain (GWG) for a singleton pregnancy [4, 5]

| Pre-pregnancy BMI category        | Total weight gain during pregnancy (kg)   | Average rate of weight gain during the 2nd and 3rd trimesters in g/week   |
|-----------------------------------|-------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Underweight (<18.5 kg/m 2 )       | 12.5 - 18 kg                              | ~ 510 g/week                                                              |
| Normal weight (18.5-24.9 kg/m 2 ) | 11.5 - 16 kg                              | ~ 420 g/week                                                              |
| Overweight (25.0-29.9 kg/m 2 )    | 7 - 11.5 kg                               | ~ 280 g/week                                                              |
| ǤȨȳɴȳ ˉ˹̶̹ʲ̶ ɕȿʿɝ 2 )                | 5 - 9 kg                                  | ~ 220 g/week                                                              |

Table 2. Recommendations for Gestational Weight Gain (GWG) for a twin pregnancy [4, 5]

| Pre-pregnancy BMI category        | Total weight gain during pregnancy       | Average rate of weight gain during the 2nd trimester   | Average rates of weight gain during the 3rd trimester   |
|-----------------------------------|------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------|
| Underweight (<18.5 kg/m 2 )       | ǟɣ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞ ȯɿȳ ɻɣ ɇɞɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ȯȝɻȝ | ǟɣ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞ ȯɿȳ ɻɣ ɇɞɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ȯȝɻȝ               | ǟɣ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞ ȯɿȳ ɻɣ ɇɞɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ȯȝɻȝ                |
| Normal weight (18.5-24.9 kg/m 2 ) | 16.8 - 24.5 kg                           | ~ 770 g/week                                           | ~ 670 g/week                                            |
| Overweight (25.0-29.9 kg/m 2 )    | 14.1 - 22.7 kg                           | ~ 720 g/week                                           | ~ 610g/week                                             |
| ǤȨȳɴȳ ˉ˹̶̹ʲ̶ ɕȿʿɝ 2 )                | 11.4 - 19.1 kg                           | ~ 450 g/week                                           | ~ 580 g/week                                            |

If you are pregnant with triplets or other higher-order multiples, consult with your doctor and dietitian for advice on your weight gain.

In  all  cases,  it  is  important  that  you  work  closely  with  your  dietitian  to  maintain  your  GWG within  the  recommended  range.

![Picture 81](images/SRC013/picture-081.png)

## Dietary Recommendations During Pregnancy

### 3.1. Consume a balanced and diverse diet

The dietary intake recommendations for non-pregnant women are shown in Box 1.  The same ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴ ȝɭɭɗʑ ʋɄȳɞ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞɻ ȝɴ ʋȳɗɗʲ ǼɄȳ ɣɞɗʑ ɻɄɇɞȿ ɻɄȝɻ ɇɴ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ɇɴ ɻɄȳ fact that you will need to take additional energy and protein as compared to when you were not pregnant (refer to section 3.3 for recommendations regarding your energy intake).

Eating a variety of foods from the six food groups every day is the ideal way to provide all the essential nutrients to your body as well as to your baby. The six food groups include (Vegetables, Fruits,  Cereals  and  starchy  vegetables,  Legumes,  Milk,  dairy  products  &amp;  alternatives,  Fish, poultry, meat &amp; alternatives). To achieve a healthy and balanced diet, it is also recommended that you limit your consumption of foods that are high in sugar, salt, and unhealthy fats such as commercially prepared foods and snacks. These foods are high in calories and hence will make you gain excessive weight. These foods are also unhealthy for your baby and can increase your baby's risk for obesity and chronic disease later in life. It is important to note that many of the ȝȯʊȳɰɴȳ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ɣȾ ȝɞ ɿɞɄȳȝɗɻɄʑ ȯɇȳɻ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ʋɇɗɗ ɞɣɻ ȝɭɭȳȝɰ ɇɝɝȳȯɇȝɻȳɗʑ ɣɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ˉɇʲȳʲʳ ȝɻ ȨɇɰɻɄˊʲ Ǥɞ ɻɄȳ ȩɣɞɻɰȝɰʑʳ ɝȝɞʑ ɣȾ ɻɄȳɴȳ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ʋɇɗɗ ɻȝɕȳ ʑȳȝɰɴ ɻɣ Ȩȳ ɴȳȳɞ ȝɞȯ ʋɇɗɗ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ manifested until later in the child's life.

Box 1 provides you with some general dietary recommendations [6-12] , make sure to consult with your dietitian Ⱦɣɰ ȾɿɰɻɄȳɰ ɻȝɇɗɣɰɇɞȿ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɞȳȳȯɴʲ

![Picture 82](images/SRC013/picture-082.png)

#### Box  1.  General  recommendations,  serving  examples,  and  practical  tips  for  an  adequate  and balanced  diet

##### VEGETABLES

###### Aim for 3-5 servings of vegetables a day

![Picture 83](images/SRC013/picture-083.png)

###### Examples of one serving of vegetable:

- 1 large carrot
- 1 medium tomato
- ½ cup of cooked green or colored vegetables (cabbage, broccoli, eggplant)
- 1 cup of raw green leafy vegetables (lettuce, spinach, arugula, purslane)
- ́ ȩɿɭ ̷̶̶̉ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳ ɒɿɇȩȳʳ ɗɣʋ ɴɣȯɇɿɝ

###### Practical tips:

- Choose a wide variety and color of vegetables.
- Eat vegetables with most meals, including snacks.
- Favor fresh vegetables in season.
- Choose vegetables prepared with little or no added salt, oil or fat.
- Eat adequate amounts daily since vegetables help you feel full and are low in calories.
- Cook  side  vegetables  (broccoli,  carrots,  zucchini)  by  lightly  steaming  or  stir-frying  to  preserve nutrients.
- Eat  more  greens  and  leafy  vegetables  (fattouch,  tabbouleh,  green  thyme,  arugula,  cabbage,  or spinach  salad).
- In restaurants, order salad dressing separately and limit how much you add.
- Eat raw vegetables as snacks with low-fat dip.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ȿɰɇɗɗȳȯ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳɴ ˉɻɣɝȝɻɣȳɴʳ ɣɞɇɣɞɴʳ ɝɿɴɄɰɣɣɝɴʳ ȿɰȳȳɞ ɭȳɭɭȳɰɴˊʲ
- Eat more vegetable-based dishes such as saloona (traditional stew).
- When eating out, choose plain vegetables instead of breaded or deep fried.
- Avoid adding butter or margarine and rich sauces to vegetables. Use fresh or dried spices, herbs, or ɗȳɝɣɞ ɒɿɇȩȳ ɇɞɴɻȳȝȯʲ
- Favor fresh vegetables over canned ones. When choosing canned vegetables, make sure to rinse them with water to lower the salt content.
- Add a plate of fresh cut vegetables with your main meals.

![Picture 84](images/SRC013/picture-084.png)

##### CEREALS AND STARCHY VEGETABLES

ǵɿȨɴɻɇɻɿɻȳ ɰȳʟɞȳȯ ȿɰȝɇɞɴ ˉȳʲȿʲʳ ʋɄɇɻȳ Ȩɰȳȝȯˊ ʋɇɻɄ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ Ȩɰȳȝȯɴ ȝɞȯ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ General recommendations are 5-6 servings per day

![Picture 85](images/SRC013/picture-085.png)

1 Serving = ½ cup

![Picture 86](images/SRC013/picture-086.png)

###### Example of one serving [9] :

- ½ cup of cooked brown rice or pasta
- ½ cup of cooked bulgur, oats, harees wheat, quinoa or buckwheat
- 1 medium slice of whole grain bread
- ̷ ȩɿɭ ɣȾ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ ȩɣɰɞʠȝɕȳɴ
- 3 cups of plain popcorn
- ½ medium potato, baked or boiled
- ½ cup of mashed potato; ½ large, sweet potato, baked; ½ cup of cooked sweet potato (sliced or mashed)
- ½ cup of corn kernels, fresh or frozen

###### Practical tips:

- ǵɿȨɴɻɇɻɿɻȳ ɰȳʟɞȳȯ ȿɰȝɇɞɴ ˉȳʲȿʲʳ ʋɄɇɻȳ Ȩɰȳȝȯˊ Ȩʑ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ Ȩɰȳȝȯɴ ȝɞȯ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴʲ
- Make most of your choices whole grain such as (brown rice, whole wheat pasta and whole grain bread).
- ȌɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ ʋɇɗɗ ɕȳȳɭ ʑɣɿ Ⱦɿɗɗ ɗɣɞȿȳɰ ɻɄȝɞ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɝȝȯȳ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɰȳʟɞȳȯ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴʲ
- Make sandwiches using whole grain breads.
- ǖȳȳɭ ɝɣȯȳɰȝɻȳ ɭɣɰɻɇɣɞ ɴɇʗȳɴ ˆ ȳɴɭȳȩɇȝɗɗʑ Ⱦɣɰ ɰȳʟɞȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɗɇɕȳ ɭȝɴɻȝ ȝɞȯ ʋɄɇɻȳ ɰɇȩȳʲ
- When eating out, order pasta with a tomato-based sauce rather than cream-based sauce.
- Ǯɰȳɭȝɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȩȳɰȳȝɗ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ ȯɇɴɄȳɴ ʋɇɻɄ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞɴ ɗɇɕȳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ʋɄȳȝɻ ʠɣɿɰʳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ʋɄȳȝɻ ȿɰȝɇɞɴʳ Ȩɰɣʋɞ ɰɇȩȳʳ ɒȝɰȳȳɴɄ ˉȩɰɿɴɄȳȯ ʋɄȳȝɻˊʳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ɣȝɻɴ ɣɰ ɣȝɻɝȳȝɗʳ Ȩȝɰɗȳʑʳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ʋɄȳȝɻ ɭȝɴɻȝʲ
- Start your day with a bowl of oatmeal, whole grain cereal or a whole wheat toast instead of eating ȝ Ⱦȝɻȝʑȳɰʳ ȩɰɣɇɴɴȝɞɻ ɣɰ ɝɿʝɞʲ
- Choose cereals prepared with little or no added fats, oils, sugar , and salt.
- Keep biscuits, cakes, pastries, and pies for special occasions.
- Have a baked or boiled potato, sweet potato, or salad instead of French fries.
- Limit  fried  breads  (paratha,  puri)  and  bakery  products  that  contain  a  lot  of  fat  and  oil  (such  as croissant, fatayer).
- The daily consumption of whole grains is associated with reduced risk of weight gain.
- Ǳȳȝȯ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɗȝȨȳɗɴ ɻɣ ȩɄɣɣɴȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ʋɇɻɄ ɄɇȿɄ ʟȨȳɰ ȝɞȯ ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ȩɣɞɻȳɞɻ ȝɞȯ ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ Ʉʑȯɰɣȿȳɞȝɻȳȯ or trans-fat.
- Ǳȳȝȯ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɗȝȨȳɗɴ ɻɣ ɝȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ ɣɰ ʋɄɣɗȳ ʋɄȳȝɻ ɇɴ ʟɰɴɻ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ɗɇɴɻ ɣȾ ɇɞȿɰȳȯɇȳɞɻɴʲ
- Avoid cereal-based products that contain partially hydrogenated oils or trans-fats (such as crackers, biscuits and baked products).

![Picture 87](images/SRC013/picture-087.png)

1 Serving = ½ Medium Potato

![Picture 88](images/SRC013/picture-088.png)

##### LEGUMES

###### Eat legumes daily. Legumes are rich in protein

![Picture 89](images/SRC013/picture-089.png)

Maintain a daily consumption of protein foods which include legumes, unsalted and raw nuts and seeds, ȝɞȯʿɣɰ ȝɞɇɝȝɗ˅ Ȩȝɴȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ˉʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ɝȳȝɻʳ ȝɞȯ ȳȿȿɴˊʲ ǱȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ ƫɣʐ ̸ Ⱦɣɰ ɝɣɰȳ ȯȳɻȝɇɗɴ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ number of servings and serving sizes.

###### Practical tips:

- Make legumes (lentils, beans, chickpeas) one of your main protein sources.
- Choose legumes that are prepared with little or no added fats or oils.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɻɰȝȯɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ƠɰȝȨɇȩ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ˉȾɣɿɗ ɝɿȯȝɝɝȳɴʳ Ʉɿɝɝɿɴʳ Ȩȝɒȳɗȝ ˉȾȝʊȝ Ȩȳȝɞɴˊʳ ɞȝɕɄɇ ˉȩɄɇȩɕɭȳȝɴˊʲ
- Add beans, lentils or chickpeas to soups, stews, and casseroles.
- Top a salad with beans, unsalted, raw nuts or seeds.
- For lunch at work, try cooked beans, dahl, or hummus.
- Try vegetarian dishes from other cultures such as bean burritos and dahl.
- Rinse canned beans with water before using to decrease salt content.
- Include foods rich in vitamin C (tomatoes, peppers, lemon) with meals to enhance the absorption of iron and zinc from legumes.
- Wait for at least one hour after meals before drinking tea to allow the absorption of iron from foods.
- Cooking dry legumes instead of canned varieties is cheaper and decreases packaging waste, and exposure to chemicals from cans.

![Picture 90](images/SRC013/picture-090.png)

### MILK, DAIRY PRODUCTS AND ALTERNATIVES

Maintain a daily consumption of low-fat milk and dairy products or milk alternatives General recommendations are 3 servings per day

![Picture 91](images/SRC013/picture-091.png)

#### Examples of one serving [13] :

- 1 cup of low-fat milk
- 3 tablespoons of low-fat powdered milk
- ̷ ȩɿɭ ɣȾ ȩȝɗȩɇɿɝ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɴɣʑ ɝɇɗɕ
- 1 cup of yogurt (low-fat)
- 2 tablespoons of labneh
- 50 g of white cheese (i.e., a size equivalent to 2 thumbs - taking the tip of the thumb to the base).

#### Practical tips:

- Include a cup of low-fat milk, laban, or yogurt with your meals.
- Use low-fat milk or dairy products when cooking.
- ǁȝʊɣɰ ɭɗȝɇɞ ɗɣʋ˅Ⱦȝɻ ȯȝɇɰʑ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ɗɇɕȳ ɝɇɗɕʳ ɗȝȨȝɞʳ ȝɞȯ ʑɣȿɿɰɻ ɣʊȳɰ ɴʋȳȳɻȳɞȳȯ ȝɞȯ ʠȝʊɣɰȳȯ ɣɞȳɴʲ Add your own fruit when desired.
- Maintain a daily consumption of skimmed or low-fat milk and dairy products.
- ƬɄɣɣɴȳ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɝɇɗɕ ˉɗɣʋ˅Ⱦȝɻˊʲ
- When drinking karak or other hot drinks (lattés and cappuccinos) choose low-fat options and add only a small amount of sugar (or without sugar if possible).
- Prepare your milk-based desserts (Umm Ali, muhallabiya) with low-fat milk and less sugar.
- Consume low-salt white cheeses instead of yellow cheeses (which are higher in fat).
- Choose low-fat types of halloumi, mozzarella, feta or other cheese for cooking.
- Limit your intake of processed cheese (spreadable).
- Ǟȝɕȳ ɴɄȝɕȳɴ ɣɰ ɴɝɣɣɻɄɇȳɴ Ȩʑ Ȩɗȳɞȯɇɞȿ ɗɣʋ˅Ⱦȝɻ ɣɰ ɴɕɇɝɝȳȯ ɗȝȨȝɞʳ ʑɣȿɿɰɻʳ ɝɇɗɕ ɣɰ ȝ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɝɇɗɕ alternative such as soy beverage with a combination of fresh or frozen fruits.
- If you do not drink enough milk or eat enough dairy products, choose other calcium and vitamin-D ɰɇȩɄ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ˉȳʲȿʲ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɴɣʑ ȯɰɇɞɕɴʳ ȝɗɝɣɞȯɴʳ ȩɄɇȩɕɭȳȝɴˊʲ
- Ʋɰɇɞɕ ɗȝȩɻɣɴȳ˅Ⱦɰȳȳ ɝɇɗɕ ɣɰ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɴɣʑ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ ɇȾ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɗȝȩɻɣɴȳ ɇɞɻɣɗȳɰȝɞɻʲ

![Picture 92](images/SRC013/picture-092.png)

### FISH, POULTRY, MEAT AND ALTERNATIVES

These foods are rich sources of protein

![Picture 93](images/SRC013/picture-093.png)

Maintain a daily consumption of protein foods which include legumes, nuts and seeds and/or animalȨȝɴȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ˉʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ɝȳȝɻ ȝɞȯ ȳȿȿɴˊʲ ǱȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ ƫɣʐ ̸ Ⱦɣɰ ɝɣɰȳ ȯȳɻȝɇɗɴ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ɞɿɝȨȳɰ ɣȾ ɴȳɰʊɇɞȿɴ and serving sizes.

#### ǁɇɴɄʴ Ƭɣɞɴɿɝȳ ʟɴɄ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɻʋɇȩȳ ȝ ʋȳȳɕʴ

- Ơɇɝ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ȝ ʊȝɰɇȳɻʑ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɻʋɇȩȳ ɭȳɰ ʋȳȳɕʵ ȳʐȝɝɭɗȳɴ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳ ɴȝɗɝɣɞʳ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳɴʳ ɻɿɞȝ (light), and zobaidy (malabar cavalla).
- ǘɇɝɇɻ ȳʐȩȳɴɴɇʊȳ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ɣȾ ɗȝɰȿȳ ʟɴɄ ˉɴʋɣɰȯʟɴɄʳ ɕɇɞȿ ɝȝȩɕȳɰȳɗʳ ɝȝɰɗɇɞʳ ȝɞȯ ɻɿɞȝ˅Ȩɇȿȳʑȳˊ Ȩȳȩȝɿɴȳ ɻɄȳʑ may contain some contaminants like mercury.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɴȳȝȾɣɣȯ Ȩɿɻ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȯȳȳɭ Ⱦɰɇȳȯ ȩɄɣɇȩȳɴʲ
- ƫȝɕȳ ɣɰ ȿɰɇɗɗ ʟɴɄ ɇɞɴɻȳȝȯ ɣȾ Ⱦɰʑɇɞȿʲ
- ƫɿʑ ȾɰȳɴɄ ɣɰ Ⱦɰɣʗȳɞ ʟɴɄ ɻɄȝɻ Ʉȝɴ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳȳɞ Ȩɰȳȝȯȳȯʳ Ȩȝɻɻȳɰȳȯʳ ɣɰ ȯȳȳɭ˅Ⱦɰɇȳȯʲ
- Ǯɰȳɭȝɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ ʟɴɄ ʋɇɻɄɣɿɻ ȩɣȝɻɇɞȿ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ Ȩɰȳȝȯȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴˊ ȝɞȯ ɗɇɝɇɻ ɭɰȳ˅ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳȯ Ȩɰȳȝȯȳȯ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʟɴɄ ʟɞȿȳɰɴʲ
- Ǯɇȩɕ ȩȝɞɞȳȯ ʟɴɄ ɭȝȩɕȳȯ ɇɞ ʋȝɻȳɰ ɰȝɻɄȳɰ ɻɄȝɞ ɣɇɗʲ
- ȌɄȳɞ ȯɇɞɇɞȿ ɣɿɻʳ ȩɄɣɣɴȳ ʟɴɄ ɴȳȝɴɣɞȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ɄȳɰȨɴ ȝɞȯ ɗȳɝɣɞ ɇɞɴɻȳȝȯ ɣȾ ȝ ɄɇȿɄ˅Ⱦȝɻ ɴȝɿȩȳʲ
- Ȍɰȝɭ ȝ ʟɴɄ ʟɗɗȳɻ ȝɗɣɞȿ ʋɇɻɄ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳɴ ȝɞȯ ɄȳɰȨɴ ɇɞ ȝ ɭȝɰȩɄɝȳɞɻ ɭȝɭȳɰ ȝɞȯ Ȩȝɕȳ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ɣʊȳɞʲ

##### Poultry and meat: Choose skinless poultry and lean cuts of meat:

- Remove skin from poultry before cooking or buy skinless pieces.
- Limit your consumption of red meat to no more than 500 g per week [14] .
- Limit your consumption of processed luncheon and deli meats such as corned beef, hot dogs, sausages, pepperoni, salami, and smoked meat, as they are high in salt and nitrates (cancer-causing constituents). Make sandwiches with lower fat, unprocessed options such as roast beef, turkey, or chicken.
- Choose less fatty cuts of meat such as leg of lamb (after removing visible fat), lean ground beef, and beef tenderloin.
- Tenderize lean cuts of meat by using a marinade or a slow cooking method such as stewing or braising.
- Ǽɰɇɝ ɣʜ ȝɗɗ ʊɇɴɇȨɗȳ Ⱦȝɻɴ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɝȳȝɻɴʲ Ʋɇɴȩȝɰȯ Ⱦȝɻ ȯɰɇɭɭɇɞȿɴ Ⱦɰɣɝ ȩɣɣɕȳȯ ɝȳȝɻʲ
- Broil, grill, roast, poach or boil poultry and meat instead of frying.
- If frying meat, use little oil.
- Prepare your foods without coating (such as breaded foods); avoid rich sauces and gravies.
- Limit pre-prepared breaded foods such as nuggets.

##### Eggs:

- Limit raw or partially cooked eggs or foods containing raw eggs.
- Boiled eggs are nutritious and great to have for breakfast or dinner.

##### Nuts and seeds:

- Aim for unsalted, raw nuts and seeds, rather than fried ones.
- Choose unsalted, raw nuts and seeds, as part of a healthy snack and in moderate quantities (¼ cup).
- Top your salad with unsalted, raw nuts or seeds.
- Add some unsalted, raw nuts to your yogurt or oatmeal in the morning.

'For more information on alternatives for animal-based protein foods, see Box 8. Dietary recommendations for vegetarian and vegan women.'

### Box 2:  PROTEIN FOODS

![Picture 94](images/SRC013/picture-094.png)

Ǟȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞ ɰɇȩɄ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȯȝɇɗʑ ȯɇȳɻʲ ǼɄȳɴȳ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳ ɗȳȿɿɝȳɴʳ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ɗȳȝɞ meat, eggs, as well as unsalted, raw nuts and seeds.

General recommendations for protein foods are 5-5.5 servings per day. Examples of one serving include [11] :

- ¼ cup cooked beans, peas, and lentils
- 1 ounce (30 g) of cooked seafood, skinless chicken, and lean meats
- 1 egg or 1½ egg whites
- ½ ounce (15 g) raw, unsalted nuts or seeds (such as 12 almonds or 7 walnut halves or ¼ cup of seeds)
- 2 tablespoons of Hummus
- 1 tablespoon of peanut butter

#### ̹ʲ̸ʲ Ǟɣɰȳ ȝȨɣɿɻ ʟɴɄ

Fish is an important source of high-quality protein and omega-3 fatty acids (which are healthy ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ Ⱦȝɻˊ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ Ǥɇɗʑ ʟɴɄ Ʉȝɴ ɻɄȳ ɄɇȿɄȳɴɻ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ɣɝȳȿȝ˅̹ Ⱦȝɻɻʑ ȝȩɇȯɴʲ ǼɄɇɴ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳɴ ʟɴɄ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳɴʳ ɴȝɗɝɣɞʳ ɣʑɴɻȳɰɴ ȝɞȯ ɴɣɝȳ ʊȝɰɇȳɻɇȳɴ ɣȾ ȩȝɞɞȳȯ ɻɿɞȝ ˉȩȝɞɞȳȯ ɇɞ water, light) [13] ʲ ȘɣȨȝɇȯʑ ˉɝȝɗȝȨȝɰ ȩȝʊȝɗɗȝˊ ȝɞȯ ȿɿȨȿɿȨ ˉɴȳȝ ȩɰȝȨˊ ȝɰȳ ȝɗɴɣ ɗɣȩȝɗ ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɻɄȝɻ contain some omega-3 fatty acids.

ȌɄɇɗȳ ʟɴɄ ɇɴ ʊȳɰʑ ɄȳȝɗɻɄʑʳ ɴɣɝȳ ɗȝɰȿȳɰ ʋɇɗȯ ʟɴɄ ˉȳʲȿʲʳ ȿɰɣɿɭȳɰʳ ɕɇɞȿ ɝȝȩɕȳɰȳɗʳ ɻɿɞȝˊ ɝȝʑ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ȩɣɞɻȝɝɇɞȝɞɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑʲ ǘɇɝɇɻȳȯ ȯȝɻȝ ȳʐɇɴɻɴ ȝȨɣɿɻ ɻɄȳ ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑ ȩɣɞɻȳɞɻ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ƠɰȝȨɇȝɞ ǂɿɗȾʲ ǵɣɝȳ Ⱦȝɰɝȳȯ ʟɴɄ ȩȝɞ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ɄȝɰɝȾɿɗ ȩɄȳɝɇȩȝɗɴʲ ǱȳɴȳȝɰȩɄ ɴɿȿȿȳɴɻɴ ɻɄȳ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɣɿɻʋȳɇȿɄ ɻɄȳ ɰɇɴɕɴ [15] .

##### ǼɄȳ Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋɇɞȿ ȝɰȳ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴ ɰȳɗȝɻȳȯ ɻɣ ʟɴɄ [16] :

- ƶȝɻ ȝ ʊȝɰɇȳɻʑ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ȝɴ ɻɄɇɴ ʋɇɗɗ ɝɇɞɇɝɇʗȳ ʑɣɿɰ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ȳʐɭɣɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɄȝɰɝȾɿɗ ȩɄȳɝɇȩȝɗɴʲ
- Ơɇɝ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ƫȳɴɻ ƬɄɣɇȩȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ˉɗɇɴɻȳȯ ɇɞ ƫɣʐ ̹ˊʴ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ȝ ʊȝɰɇȳɻʑ ɣȾ ɻɄȳɴȳ ʟɴɄ ȝɻ least twice a week.
- ǁɣɰ ɻɄȳ ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɗɇɴɻȳȯ ɿɞȯȳɰ ǂɣɣȯ ƬɄɣɇȩȳɴʴ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ɻɄȳɴȳ ɣɞɗʑ ɣɞȩȳ ɭȳɰ ʋȳȳɕʲ
- ƫɣʐ ̹ ȝɗɴɣ ɗɇɴɻɴ ɻɄȳ ɻʑɭȳ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɻɣ ɗɇɝɇɻʲ

### 3.3. Energy intake during pregnancy

ǵɄɣɿɗȯ Ǌ ɇɞȩɰȳȝɴȳ ɝʑ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻɰɇɝȳɴɻȳɰ ɣȾ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʹ

ǊȾ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞɻʳ ʑɣɿ ɞȳȳȯ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɗɻ ʋɇɻɄ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɇȳɻɇɻɇȝɞ ɻɣ ȯȳɻȳɰɝɇɞȳ ʑɣɿɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ recommendations. In general, ɻɄȳɰȳ ɇɴ ɞɣ ɞȳȳȯ ɻɣ ɇɞȩɰȳȝɴȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ trimester of your pregnancy.

In other words, if your usual energy intake was 1800 kcal per day before pregnancy, then you should ȩɣɞɻɇɞɿȳ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ɻɄȳ ɴȝɝȳ ɯɿȝɞɻɇɻʑ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻɰɇɝȳɴɻȳɰ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʲ

ȌɄȝɻ ȝȨɣɿɻ ɻɄȳ ɴȳȩɣɞȯ ȝɞȯ ɻɄɇɰȯ ɻɰɇɝȳɴɻȳɰɴ ɣȾ ɝʑ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʹ

In general, you need to increase your energy intake by 340 kcal/ day in the second trimester and by 452 kcal/day in the third (Box 4). These recommendations apply to you if you have started your pregnancy with a normal body weight (i.e. BMI within the normal range) [5, 17] . If you were overweight, obese or underweight at the start  of  your  pregnancy,  the  recommendations  shown  in  Box  4 may not apply to you. You will need to consult with your dietitian ɻɣ ȩȝɗȩɿɗȝɻȳ ʑɣɿɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ ɞȳȳȯɴ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʲ

#### GOOD CHOICES:

- Bass
- Grouper
- Halibut
- Mackerel (Spanish) 'khanad'
- Mahi Mahi
- Snapper
- Tuna (white/albacore)

![Picture 97](images/SRC013/picture-097.png)

#### TO LIMIT:

- Mackerel (King)
- Marlin
- ǵʋɣɰȯʟɴɄ
- ǼɇɗȳʟɴɄ
- Tuna (Bigeye)

![Picture 98](images/SRC013/picture-098.png)

![Picture 99](images/SRC013/picture-099.png)

### Box 4. Energy requirements during pregnancy if you have started your pregnancy with a normal body weight

If  you are starting your pregnancy with a healthy weight, you do not need to increase your energy intake  until  the  second  and  third  trimesters.

- First trimester: No need to increase your caloric intake. However, it is important that you choose nutritious foods to help support your baby's growth and development.
- Second trimester: You need to add 340 kcal to your daily energy intake.
- Third trimester: You need to add 452 kcal to your daily energy intake.
- Twin pregnancies: If you are pregnant with twins, you will need to add 600 kcal per day during the second and third trimesters

As you may probably realize, there is no need to eat twice as much food to meet your caloric needs during pregnancy. You can meet your requirements by simply adding a healthy snack or a small meal. Examples of snacks/meals that could be added to your diet to meet the additional calorie needs are presented in Box 5. Snacks that contain some protein (such as unsalted, raw nuts, legumes, yogurt, cheese) are important for you since your protein needs increase a bit during the second and third trimesters of pregnancy.

![Picture 100](images/SRC013/picture-100.png)

### Box 5. Examples of snacks/meals that could be added to the diet to meet the additional calorie needs during pregnancy

#### Second trimester (+340 kcal/day)

##### Example 1:

- ́ ȝ ȩɿɭ ɣȾ ȯɰɇȳȯ ʟȿɴ
- 10 whole almonds
- 7 walnuts, halves

##### Example 2:

- 1  ½  medium  sliced  whole  wheat  bread toasted
- 2 ounces (60 g) of low-fat labneh with 1 teaspoon of olive oil
- 2 small tomatoes

##### Example 3:

- 4 whole wheat crackers
- 2 tablespoons of peanut butter
- ½ a large apple

#### Third trimester (+452 kcal/day)

##### Example 1:

- ¾ cup of hummus dip
- 2 medium carrots, sliced
- 2 medium cucumbers, slices

##### Example 2:

-  ѿ cup of oats
- 1 cup of plain low-fat yogurt
- ½ cup of chopped banana
- 5 almonds

##### Example 3:

- 1 medium slice of whole wheat pita bread
- 2 ounces (60 g) of Akkawi cheese
- 1 cup of fresh cut fruit

It is important that you work closely with your dietitian to monitor your diet and weight gain during pregnancy. Your dietitian may consider adjusting your caloric intake based on your weight gain or other parameters.

![Picture 101](images/SRC013/picture-101.png)

### 3.4. Importance of hydration

Ʋɿɰɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʳ ȝȯȳɯɿȝɻȳ ʠɿɇȯ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ɇɴ ȳɴɴȳɞɻɇȝɗ ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȯȳɄʑȯɰȝɻɇɣɞ ˉʋɄɇȩɄ Ʉȝɴ ɞȳȿȝɻɇʊȳ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ɣɞ ʑɣɿɰ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȝɻ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ ȨȝȨʑˊ [18] . Dehydration may lead to constipation, headache and dizziness in the pregnant women and may lead to early labor and poor development of the ȨȝȨʑʲ ǼɄȳɰȳȾɣɰȳʳ ɇɻ ɇɴ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȳȯ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿ ȯɰɇɞɕ ̷̶˅̷̸ ȩɿɭɴ ɣȾ ʠɿɇȯɴ ɭȳɰ ȯȝʑ ˉɇʲȳʲʳ ̸ʲ̻ ˅ ̹ ǘˊ [19, 20] ʲ ǼɄɇɴ ɻɣɻȝɗ ȝɝɣɿɞɻ ɣȾ ʠɿɇȯɴ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳɴ ȝɗɗ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴʳ ɇɞȩɗɿȯɇɞȿ ȯɰɇɞɕɇɞȿ ʋȝɻȳɰʲ ǼɄȳ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ɣȾ water is critical in countries with hot and humid weather, such as that in the State of Qatar.

You may want to watch out for early signs of dehydration, such as:

- Feeling of thirst
- Dark-colored urine
- Tiredness
- Dizziness
- Dry mouth
- Headache
- Infrequent urination

If you experience any of those symptoms, try to rest and drink water and other healthy beverages ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȾɰȳɴɄ ɗɣʋ˅ɴȝɗɻ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳ ɒɿɇȩȳʲ Ƭɣɞɴɇȯȳɰ ȩɣɞɻȝȩɻɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ɇȾ ɻɄȳ ɴʑɝɭɻɣɝɴ ɭȳɰɴɇɴɻʲ ǱȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ ƫɣʐ ̼ Ȩȳɗɣʋ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɇɭɴ ɣɞ Ʉɣʋ ɻɣ ɝȳȳɻ ʑɣɿɰ ʠɿɇȯ ɞȳȳȯɴʲ

#### * 1 cup = 250 mL

### Box 6. Tips to meet your water needs

- Ǟȝɕȳ ʋȝɻȳɰ ʑɣɿɰ ɝȝɇɞ ɴɣɿɰȩȳ ɣȾ ʠɿɇȯɴ ɭȳɰ ȯȝʑʲ
- Choose water more often than other types of beverages.
- If you do not like water, add a wedge of lime or lemon or any other vegetable or fruit to enhance the taste.
- Choose water as a beverage to drink with meals, especially when eating out. This will help reduce your caloric intake.
- Carry a reusable water bottle everywhere you go.
- Choose water instead of sugar-sweetened beverages to help maintain your weight and the health of your teeth.
- Drink more water in hot weather and when physically active (before, during and after exercise).
- Set reminders on your phone for drinking water or use a water drinking application on your smart phone.

![Picture 102](images/SRC013/picture-102.png)

### 3.5. Supplementation during pregnancy

It is important for you to consume adequate amounts of all the essential vitamins and minerals in order to have a normal pregnancy with lower risk of complications. In addition, these nutrients are vital for your baby's development and growth.

Following a varied, balanced healthy diet during your pregnancy will most likely provide you with the needed vitamins and minerals. That said, there are a few vitamins and minerals that deserve special attention and for which you may need to take supplements. These include iron, folic acid, vitamin D and calcium. However, before taking any supplements, it is recommended that you ȯɇɴȩɿɴɴ ʑɣɿɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɞȳȳȯɴ ʋɇɻɄ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰʲ

![Picture 103](images/SRC013/picture-103.png)

#### Iron:

You need more iron during pregnancy, to meet your own needs as well as those of your baby. In Ⱦȝȩɻʳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʳ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ˔ɴ ɇɰɣɞ ɴɻɣɰȳɴ ȝɰȳ Ⱦɣɰɝȳȯʲ ǊȾ ʑɣɿ Ʉȝʊȳ ȝɞ ɇɰɣɞ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞɻ ȯɇȳɻʳ ʑɣɿ will develop anemia, a condition that can result in health complications for you and your baby. Ơɞȳɝɇȝ ȩȝɞ ȝɗɴɣ ȩȝɿɴȳ Ⱦȝɻɇȿɿȳ ȝɞȯ ɴɄɣɰɻɞȳɴɴ ɣȾ ȨɰȳȝɻɄ ʋɄȳɞ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɝȝɕɇɞȿ ȝ ɭɄʑɴɇȩȝɗ ȳʜɣɰɻʲ Adequate iron intake during pregnancy can reduce your risk of having a low-birth weight baby (i.e., a very small baby), while also reducing the risk of early birth (preterm) and infant mortality. Ơɞȳɝɇȝ ȝɞȯ ɇɰɣɞ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩʑ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȯȳɻȳȩɻȳȯ Ȩʑ ȝ Ȩɗɣɣȯ ɻȳɴɻ [21, 22] .

The  WHO  recommends  daily  oral  iron  supplementation  with  30-60  mg  of  iron  for pregnant women [23] . If you had anemia before getting pregnant, make sure to discuss this with your doctor as you may require higher doses of iron supplementation.

In addition to supplementation, it is important to include iron-rich foods in your daily diet. Refer to Tables 3 and 4 for examples of animal-based iron-rich foods as well as plant-based foods that contain iron, respectively. It is important to note that iron from animal sources (heme-iron) is more easily absorbed by the body compared to iron from plant sources (non-heme iron).

##### Table 3. Animal sources of iron

##### Excellent sources of Iron:

- Spleen
- Octopus
- Oysters
- Mussels
- Heart

##### Good Sources of Iron :

- Goat
- Sardines
- Beef
- Lamb
- Shrimp

##### Table 4. Plant based iron sources

##### Excellent sources of Iron:

- Dried apricots
- Large white beans, cooked
- Kidney beans, cooked
- Lentils, cooked
- Spinach, cooked
- Chard, cooked

##### Adequate Sources of Iron:

- Leg and thigh of chicken or turkey
- Tuna (light)
- Breast of chicken or turkey

##### Good Sources of Iron :

- Ǌɰɣɞ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ȨɰȳȝɕȾȝɴɻ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ ˉɿɞɴʋȳȳɻȳɞȳȯˊ
- Quinoa
- Mushrooms, cooked
- Squash and pumpkin seeds
- Broccoli
- Cashews
- Leeks

![Picture 104](images/SRC013/picture-104.png)

#### In order to maximize iron absorption from your foods, it is advisable to:

- Add a source of vitamin C to your meal, such as tomatoes, peppers, broccoli, strawberries, and  oranges,  as  well  as  other  citrus  fruits.  This  is  particularly  important  when  you  are consuming legumes or other plant-based sources of iron.
- ǘɇɝɇɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɇɞȿ ɻȳȝ ɣɰ ȩɣʜȳȳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ȝ ɝȳȝɗ ɣɰ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɣɞȳ Ʉɣɿɰ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ɣɰ ȝȾɻȳɰ ȝ ɝȳȝɗʳ ȝɴ these beverages contain substances that decrease the absorption of iron (and calcium).

#### Folic Acid:

You have probably been taking folic acid supplements before your pregnancy. It is important that you continue taking your folic acid supplements during your pregnancy too. An adequate amount of folic acid is needed in order to decrease the risk of early birth (preterm), or birth defects such as neural tube defects (i.e., improper development of the baby's brain or spinal cord) [24] .

You  are  therefore  expected  to  continue  with  your  folic  acid  supplementation  (400 ɝɇȩɰɣȿɰȝɝɴʿȯȝɇɗʑˊ  ɻɄɰɣɿȿɄɣɿɻ  ɻɄȳ  ʟɰɴɻ  ̷̸  ʋȳȳɕɴ  ɣȾ  ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ [25] .  In  some  cases,  and depending on your health condition, your doctor may recommend that folic acid supplementation be continued throughout the entire pregnancy [24] , or he/she may recommend higher doses. Your doctor will advise you on the right dose for you.

In addition to folic acid supplementation, it is also important that you consume a diet rich in folate (i.e., folic acid). T able 5 provides tips on what food options are rich sources of folate.

![Picture 105](images/SRC013/picture-105.png)

![Picture 106](images/SRC013/picture-106.png)

#### Vitamin D:

Even though you can meet part of your vitamin D requirement through sunlight exposure, it is also important that you consume foods that are rich in vitamin D. Few foods are naturally rich ɇɞ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋʲ ǼɄȳ Ȩȳɴɻ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ ȝɰȳ Ⱦȝɻɻʑ ʟɴɄ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɴȝɗɝɣɞ ȝɞȯ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳɴʲ ƶȿȿ ʑɣɗɕɴʳ ȩɄȳȳɴȳ ȝɞȯ beef liver also contain vitamin D. However, you are advised to limit the consumption of liver and liver products when you are pregnant, since they contain very high amounts of vitamin A that ȩȝɞ Ʉȝɰɝ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ Ǟȝɞʑ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȝɰȳ ȝɗɴɣ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋ ɗɇɕȳ ȯȝɇɰʑ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ȝɞȯ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴʲ Below are examples of foods that are considered good sources of vitamin D [26] :

- ǁȝɻɻʑ ʟɴɄ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɴȝɗɝɣɞʳ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳʳ ȝɞȯ ɝȝȩɕȳɰȳɗ ˉɭɰȳȾȳɰȝȨɗʑ ǵɭȝɞɇɴɄ ɝȝȩɕȳɰȳɗʳ ȝɗɴɣ ɕɞɣʋɞ as 'khanad' in Qatar)
- Ǽɿɞȝ ʟɴɄ ˉɗɇɝɇɻ ɻɄȳ ȩɣɞɴɿɝɭɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ʋɄɇɻȳ ˉȝɗȨȝȩɣɰȳˊ ɻɿɞȝ ɻɣ ɣɞȩȳ ɭȳɰ ʋȳȳɕ [27] , since it may contain contaminants such as mercury)
- Ʋȝɇɰʑ ȝɞȯ ɭɗȝɞɻ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ ɝɇɗɕɴ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋ
- Egg yolk
- Ȁɞɴʋȳȳɻȳɞȳȯ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋ

In addition to the consumption of foods rich in vitamin D, it is advisable that you get some sun exposure. Some vitamin D researchers in the UK and USA suggest that approximately 5 - 30 minutes of sun exposure between 10 AM and 3 PM at least twice a week to the face, arms, legs, or back without sunscreen is usually enough [13, 28] . Data for estimates are not available in the Middle East, but required exposure time for Qatar is likely less than these estimates [13, 28] . Season, time of day, length of day, cloud cover, smog, skin melanin content (how dark your ɴɕɇɞ ɇɴˊʳ ȝɞȯ ɴɿɞɴȩɰȳȳɞ ȝɰȳ ȝɝɣɞȿ ɻɄȳ Ⱦȝȩɻɣɰɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȝʜȳȩɻ Ȁȋ ɰȝȯɇȝɻɇɣɞ ȳʐɭɣɴɿɰȳ ȝɞȯ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ʋ synthesis.

Remember

You are advised to limit the consumption of liver and liver products when you are pregnant, since they contain very high amounts of vitamin A that can harm your baby

#### Calcium:

The recommendations for calcium intake do not increase during pregnancy. Hence, if you have an adequate dietary intake of calcium, you do not need to take calcium supplements when you are  pregnant.  Supplementation  is  recommended  only  for  women  who  do  not  consume  milk and dairy products, and in certain special cases. That said, it is important that you obtain the recommended 1000 mg/day of calcium from dietary sources. Milk and dairy products are the richest sources of dietary calcium as shown in T able 6.

Table 6. What is equivalent to the calcium in 1 cup milk (300 mg calcium)?

- 1 cup yogurt (low fat or skimmed)
- 50 grams of white low salt cheese

![Picture 107](images/SRC013/picture-107.png)

ǼɄȳɰȳ ȝɰȳ ȝɗɴɣ ɣɻɄȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɇɻȳɝɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ ȩɣɞɻɰɇȨɿɻȳ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȩȝɗȩɇɿɝ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɒɿɇȩȳɴʳ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳɴʳ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɴɣʑ ɝɇɗɕʳ ȯɰɇȳȯ ʟȿɴʳ ȯȝɻȳɴʳ ȝɞȯ ɗȳȝȾʑ ȿɰȳȳɞɴʳ ȝɝɣɞȿ ɣɻɄȳɰɴ [29-32] . Refer to T able 7 to learn about the calcium content of selected food items.

#### Box 7 includes a few tips to assist you in consuming an adequate amount of calcium [10] .

### Box 7. Tips for consuming an adequate intake of calcium

- Ʋɰɇɞɕ ɝɇɗɕʳ ʑɣȿɿɰɻ ɣɰ ȩȝɗȩɇɿɝ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ ʋɇɻɄ ȳȝȩɄ ɝȳȝɗ ˉȝɗʋȝʑɴ ȩɄɣɣɴȳ ɗɣʋ˅Ⱦȝɻ ɝɇɗɕ ȝɞȯ yogurt).
- Use milk to prepare cream soups.
- Add white cheese to your salads.
- Use milk to prepare hot unsweetened oatmeal or unsweetened breakfast cereals.
- Ȁɴȳ ɗɣʋ˅Ⱦȝɻ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɣ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴʳ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɻȳȝ ɣɰ ȩɣʜȳȳʲ
- Eat yogurt or white cheese for a calcium-rich snack.
- Use yogurt as a dressing for salads or a topping for a baked potato, or try it mixed with fruit.
- Avoid the consumption of raw (unpasteurized) milk or products made from raw milk, as they may carry harmful bacteria.
- Refrigerate  dairy  products  promptly.  If  dairy  products  have  been  left  at  temperatures  between 4.5°C and 60°C for more than two hours, discard them.

If you are lactose intolerant, you may choose lactose-free dairy alternatives that are available in ɻɄȳ ɝȝɰɕȳɻ ɣɰ ȩɄɣɣɴȳ ɴɣʑ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɄȝɻ ȝɰȳ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ȩȝɗȩɇɿɝʲ

![Picture 108](images/SRC013/picture-108.png)

#### Other vitamins and minerals:

In addition to iron, folic acid, vitamin D and calcium, your doctor may recommend supplementation with other vitamins and minerals [33] . Although vitamin A is important for the healthy development of your baby, large amounts may cause malformations and birth defects. It is therefore important that  you avoid any supplements containing vitamin A, retinol, as well as supplements ʋɇɻɄ ʟɴɄ ɗɇʊȳɰ ɣɇɗ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȩɣȯ ɣɇɗˊ . Moreover, you are advised to limit the consumption of liver and liver products due to their very high vitamin A content. Your doctor should be consulted before considering vitamin A supplementation.

#### Omega-3 fatty acids:

Omega-3 fatty acids are a type of fat that your body cannot make on its own. While these fats are important to be part of everyone's diet, they are particularly important for you and your baby. Adequate consumption of omega-3 fatty acids provides the building blocks of your baby's brain and nervous system, and plays a role in preventing maternal depression after childbirth [34] . Ǥɇɗʑ ʟɴɄ Ʉȝɴ ɻɄȳ ɄɇȿɄȳɴɻ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ɣɝȳȿȝ ̹ Ⱦȝɻɻʑ ȝȩɇȯɴʲ ǼɄɇɴ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳɴ ɴȝɰȯɇɞȳɴʳ ɴȝɗɝɣɞʳ ɣʑɴɻȳɰɴ and some varieties of canned tuna (canned, light) [13] . Zobaidy (malabar cavalla) and gubgub (sea ȩɰȝȨˊ ȝɰȳ ȝɗɴɣ ɗɣȩȝɗ ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɻɄȝɻ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ɴɣɝȳ ɣɝȳȿȝ ̹ Ⱦȝɻɻʑ ȝȩɇȯɴʲ

Ȓɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȳȯ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ɣɇɗʑ ʟɴɄ ɣɞȳ ɻɣ ɻʋɣ ɻɇɝȳɴ ɭȳɰ ʋȳȳɕʲ

ȌɄɇɗȳ ʟɴɄ ɇɴ ʊȳɰʑ ɄȳȝɗɻɄʑ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʳ ɴɣɝȳ ɗȝɰȿȳɰ ʋɇɗȯ ʟɴɄ ȩȝɞ ȝȩȩɿɝɿɗȝɻȳ ɄɇȿɄ levels of contaminants such as mercury. For this reason, limit the consumption of king mackerel, ɝȝɰɗɇɞʳ  ɴʋɣɰȯʟɴɄʳ  ɻɇɗȳʟɴɄʳ  ȝɞȯ  ɻɿɞȝ  Ȩɇȿȳʑȳʲ  ǱȳȾȳɰ  ɻɣ  ɴȳȩɻɇɣɞ  ̹ʲ̸  ȝȨɣʊȳ  Ⱦɣɰ  ɝɣɰȳ  ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ɣɰ ɻɣ ɗɇɝɇɻʲ

Ǌɞ ȝȯȯɇɻɇɣɞʳ ȝɗɻɄɣɿȿɄ ɣɇɗʑ ʟɴɄ ɇɴ ɻɄȳ ɰɇȩɄȳɴɻ ɴɣɿɰȩȳ ɣȾ ɣɝȳȿȝ˅̹ Ⱦȝɻɻʑ ȝȩɇȯɴʳ ɻɄȳɰȳ ȝɰȳ ɴɣɝȳ ɭɗȝɞɻ˅ based foods that contain some omega-3 fats. These include walnuts, pumpkin seeds, and other ɴȳȳȯɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʠȝʐɴȳȳȯʳ ɇɞ ȝȯȯɇɻɇɣɞ ɻɣ ȩȝɞɣɗȝ ɣɇɗʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ ȝʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɰȳɴȳȝɰȩɄ ɇɞȯɇȩȝɻȳɴ ɻɄȝɻ ɻɄȳɴȳ ȝɰȳ ɞɣɻ ȝɴ ʋȳɗɗ ɿɻɇɗɇʗȳȯ Ȩʑ ɻɄȳ Ȩɣȯʑ ȝɴ ʟɴɄ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ [13, 15] .

In case an adequate dietary intake of omega-3 fatty acids is not achieved, then your doctor may recommend that you take supplements. Always check with your doctor before taking any supplements.

![Picture 109](images/SRC013/picture-109.png)

### 3.6. Special population groups: vegan and vegetarian women

ǵɣɝȳ  ʋɣɝȳɞ  ȩɄɣɣɴȳ  ɻɣ  Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋ  ȝ  ʊȳȿȳɻȝɰɇȝɞ  ɣɰ  ʊȳȿȝɞ  ȯɇȳɻʲ  ǼɄȳɰȳ  ɇɴ  ȝ  ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞȩȳ  Ȩȳɻʋȳȳɞ vegetarian  and  vegan  diets,  as  follows:

- Vegetarian diet: this is in general characterized by the exclusion of animal-based products ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɻ Ȩɿɻ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ȝɞɇɝȝɗ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ Ȩʑɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɝɇɗɕ and dairy products, honey, and eggs.
- Vegan diet: ɻɄɇɴ ɇɴ ȩɄȝɰȝȩɻȳɰɇʗȳȯ Ȩʑ ɻɄȳ ȳʐȩɗɿɴɇɣɞ ɣȾ ȝɗɗ ȝɞɇɝȝɗ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ˉʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ meat, milk, dairy products, honey, or eggs).

If you are following a vegetarian or vegan diet, which restricts or completely excludes animalȨȝɴȳȯ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴʳ ɰȳɴɭȳȩɻɇʊȳɗʑʳ ʑɣɿ ɝȝʑ Ȩȳ ȝɻ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɇɞȿ ɴȳʊȳɰȝɗ ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ ɴɿȩɄ as proteins, vitamin B12, iron, and zinc.

It is therefore important to consult with a dietitian for advice on how to construct a balanced and adequate vegetarian or vegan diet that meets the requirements for the various nutrients. In general, a vegan diet requires a closer monitoring by a dietitian and a doctor since the risk ɣȾ  ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ  ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ  ɇɴ  ɄɇȿɄȳɰ  ʋɇɻɄ  ɻɄɇɴ  ɻʑɭȳ  ɣȾ  ȯɇȳɻʲ  Ƭɣɞɴɿɗɻ  ʋɇɻɄ  ʑɣɿɰ  ȯɣȩɻɣɰ  ɰȳȿȝɰȯɇɞȿ your need for supplementation during pregnancy. All vegan women should take vitamin B12 supplements  during  their  pregnancy.

Box 8 outlines provides you with some useful recommendations if you are following a vegetarian or vegan diet.

### Box 8. Dietary recommendations for vegetarian and vegan women

- Consume a variety of plant-based foods (beans, lentils, tofu, soy-based meat substitutes, unsalted, raw nuts, and seeds) to help you meet your daily recommendation of protein, iron, and zinc.
- Combine legumes with whole grain cereals in your meals. This will improve the quality of the protein you are consuming.
- Ơȯȯ  ɴɣɝȳ  ɴɣɿɰȩȳ  ɣȾ  ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ  Ƭ  ˉɗȳɝɣɞ  ɒɿɇȩȳʳ  ɻɣɝȝɻɣȳɴʳ  ɭȳɭɭȳɰɴˊ  ɻɣ  ʑɣɿɰ  ɝȳȝɗɴ  ɻɣ  Ȩɣɣɴɻ  ɻɄȳ absorption  of  iron  from  plant-based  foods.
- Ǳȳɴɻɰɇȩɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɇɞȿ ɻȳȝ ɣɰ ȩɣʜȳȳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ȝ ɝȳȝɗ ɣɰ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɣɞȳ Ʉɣɿɰ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ɣɰ ȝȾɻȳɰ ȝ ɝȳȝɗʳ ȝɴ ɻɄȳɴȳ beverages contain substances that decrease iron and calcium absorption.
- If you are following a vegan diet, make sure to include foods that are rich in calcium in your diet. ǼɄȳɴȳ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳ ȩȝɗȩɇɿɝ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɣɰȝɞȿȳ ɒɿɇȩȳʳ ɴɣʑ ɝɇɗɕʳ ɝɿɗɿɕɄɇʑȝ ˉɒɿɻȳ ɗȳȝʊȳɴˊʳ ɴʋɇɴɴ ȩɄȝɰȯʳ ȯɰɇȳȯ ʟȿɴʳ ɻȝɄɇɞɇʳ ȯɰɇȳȯ ȝɭɰɇȩɣɻɴʳ ȝɗɝɣɞȯɴʳ ȝɞȯ Ȩɰɣȩȩɣɗɇ ˉɰȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ Ǽ ȝȨɗȳ ̽ˊʲ
- Consult your doctor regarding your need to take vitamin B12 supplements.
- Consult with a dietitian to help you develop a well-planned diet.
- Consult with a doctor regarding other needed supplements

### 3.8. Use of herbal supplements/teas during pregnancy

![Picture 114](images/SRC013/picture-114.png)

Taking herbal supplements or herbal teas to prevent or treat certain health conditions has long been part of our traditions. However, it is important that you watch out for these supplements or herbal teas during your pregnancy. Even if these products contain natural ingredients, this does not directly mean that they are safe. Some of these herbal supplements or herbal teas may have ingredients that are not listed on the label, and which could pass on to your baby. They may also interfere with other medicines or supplements that you are taking.

ǇȳɰȨȝɗ  ɴɿɭɭɗȳɝȳɞɻɴ  ȝɞȯ  ɄȳɰȨȝɗ  ɻȳȝɴ  Ʉȝʊȳ  ɞɣɻ  Ȩȳȳɞ  ɴȩɇȳɞɻɇʟȩȝɗɗʑ  ɴɻɿȯɇȳȯ  ȳɞɣɿȿɄ  ɗɇɕȳ  ɣɻɄȳɰ medicinal products. Be cautious when consuming these herbal supplements/teas. As a general rule,  it  is  better  to  choose  herbs  that  are  usually  used in cooking and teas made from fruits. Avoid making your own herbal tea from plants you have collected yourself. Large amounts of some herbs may possibly initiate contractions and increase your risk of early labor, or they may ȝʜȳȩɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ Ơɗʋȝʑɴ ȯɇɴȩɿɴɴ ʋɇɻɄ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ɻɄȳ ɻʑɭȳ ȝɞȯ ȝɝɣɿɞɻ ɣȾ ɄȳɰȨȝɗ ɻȳȝ ʑɣɿ ɇɞɻȳɞȯ to drink.

Box 10 contains a list of the commonly used herbal teas and their indications /contraindications during pregnancy (Box 10) [39, 40] .

#### ̹ʲ̿ʲ Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳ ȩɣɞɴɿɝɭɻɇɣɞ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ

ǊȾ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ȝ Ʉȳȝʊʑ ȯɰɇɞɕȳɰ ɣȾ ȩɣʜȳȳʳ ʑɣɿ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɻɰʑ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɇȯȳɰ ȩɿɻɻɇɞȿ ȯɣʋɞʲ ǱȳɴȳȝɰȩɄ ɴɄɣʋɴ ɻɄȝɻ ɄɇȿɄ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ˉɝɣɰȳ ɻɄȝɞ ̸̶̶ɝȿ ȝ ȯȝʑˊ ɝȝʑ ɇɞȩɰȳȝɴȳ ɻɄȳ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɗɣɴɴ ɣɰ ɗɣʋ˅ birth weight babies. For this reason, it is important that you follow the below recommendation:

- ǘɇɝɇɻ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ɻɣ ̸̶̶ɝȿ ɭȳɰ ȯȝʑ [41-43] ʳ Ⱦɰɣɝ ȝɗɗ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ ˉɻȳȝʳ ȩɣʜȳȳʳ ȩȝɰȨɣɞȝɻȳȯ ɴɣȾɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɴʳ  ȩɄɣȩɣɗȝɻȳɴ  ȝɞȯ  ɴɣɝȳ  ɣʊȳɰ˅ɻɄȳ˅ȩɣɿɞɻȳɰ  ɝȳȯɇȩɇɞȳɴˊʲ  Ǽ ȝȨɗȳ  ̾  ȯɇɴɭɗȝʑɴ  ɻɄȳ  ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ content of commonly consumed beverages [ 44] .

#### ǼȝȨɗȳ ̾ʲ Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳ ȩɣɞɻȳɞɻ ɣȾ ȩɣɝɝɣɞɗʑ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳȯ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ

Almost every pregnant woman will face a decision about taking medications during her pregnancy. However, it is important to know that not all medications are safe to take during this period. Some medications  may  cause  birth  defects,  pregnancy  loss,  premature  birth,  developmental problems or even infant death [45] .

![Picture 118](images/SRC013/picture-118.png)

### Avoiding Harmful Substances

During your pregnancy, it is very important to stay away from certain harmful substances that may cause health risks for you or your baby. Among those substances are smoking and energy drinks.

#### 5.1. Smoking

Smoking decreases the amount of oxygen that reaches your baby and exposes the fetus to chemicals that may cause cancer. It also leads to a greater risk of early birth (preterm birth), miscarriages, having a small baby (low birth weight), or even death.

Smoking increases  your  risk  of  developing  diabetes  during  pregnancy  (gestational  diabetes). ǼɄȳ ɞȳȿȝɻɇʊȳ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ɣȾ ɴɝɣɕɇɞȿ ȝɰȳ ɣȨɴȳɰʊȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ȨɣɻɄ ʟɰɴɻ ȝɞȯ ɴȳȩɣɞȯɄȝɞȯ ɴɝɣɕɇɞȿ (whether you were the one smoking or you were inhaling the smoke from someone else who is smoking).

- Cigarette smoking is therefore not safe during pregnancy as it contains nicotine. Nicotine can  increase  the  baby's  heart  rate  and  respiratory  infections,  delay  his/her  growth  and damage his/her brain and lungs.
- Shisha is not safe to use during pregnancy since it also contains nicotine.
- E-cigarettes, vapes and other tobacco products containing nicotine are also not safe to use ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʲ Ǟɣɰȳɣʊȳɰʳ ɴɣɝȳ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ ȩɣɝɝɣɞɗʑ ɿɴȳȯ ʠȝʊɣɰɇɞȿɴ ɇɞ ȳ˅ȩɇȿȝɰȳɻɻȳɴ ɝȝʑ Ȩȳ harmful to the developing baby.

You are therefore strongly advised to avoid all tobacco-containing products whether through ʟɰɴɻ ɣɰ ɴȳȩɣɞȯ˅Ʉȝɞȯ ɴɝɣɕɇɞȿʲ Ǌɻ ɇɴ ȝɗɴɣ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȳɞʊɇɰɣɞɝȳɞɻʳ ɇɞȩɗɿȯɇɞȿ ɭȳɣɭɗȳ ʋɄɣ are living with you in the same household, are aware of the risks of smoking. Box 11 presents a few key points with regards to smoking and pregnancy [46] .

![Picture 119](images/SRC013/picture-119.png)

### Box 11. Key points with regards to smoking and pregnancy

- Smoking during pregnancy is harmful to you and your baby.
- Passive smoking (breathing in other people's tobacco smoke) can also harm you and your baby.
- A baby that is born too small due to smoking is not a healthy baby.
- If you smoke, the best thing you can do is stop. Stopping at any time in pregnancy will Ʉȳɗɭʳ  ɻɄɣɿȿɄ  ɻɄȳ  ɴɣɣɞȳɰ  ɻɄȳ  Ȩȳɻɻȳɰʲ  Ȓ ɣɿ  ɴɄɣɿɗȯ  ɴɻɣɭ  ȩɣɝɭɗȳɻȳɗʑ  ˉɰȝɻɄȳɰ  ɻɄȝɞ  ɒɿɴɻ  ȩɿɻ down),  ideally  before  getting  pregnant.
- Shisha smoking is not safe during pregnancy.
- E-smoking and any tobacco containing substance are not safe during pregnancy.
- You and your husband are advised to seek help, advice, and support to stop smoking.
- Nicotine replacement therapy (NRT) is safe to use in pregnancy.

#### 5.2. Energy Drinks

ƶɞȳɰȿʑ ȯɰɇɞɕɴ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ɄɇȿɄ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ɇɞ ȝȯȯɇɻɇɣɞ ɻɣ ɣɻɄȳɰ ɴɻɇɝɿɗȝɞɻɴ ɻɄȝɻ ɝȝʑ ȩȝɿɴȳ dehydration, insomnia, as well as increased blood pressure and heart rate [ 47] .  This may cause health problems for you and your baby [41-43] . Y ou should not consume energy drinks during your pregnancy.

![Picture 120](images/SRC013/picture-120.png)

![Picture 121](images/SRC013/picture-121.png)

It  is  not  uncommon  that  you  experience  gastrointestinal  (GI)  issues  during  your  pregnancy. As the baby grows, less space is available in the abdomen for your intestines, stomach, and ȳɴɣɭɄȝȿɿɴʲ Ơȯȯɇɻɇɣɞȝɗɗʑʳ ɻɄȳ ȩɄȝɞȿȳɴ ɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ Ʉɣɰɝɣɞȳɴ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɝȝʑ ȝʜȳȩɻ ȯɇȿȳɴɻɇɣɞ ȝɞȯ ɣɻɄȳɰ ǂǊ Ⱦɿɞȩɻɇɣɞɴʲ ǼɄȳ ɝȝɒɣɰɇɻʑ ɣȾ ǂǊ ȩɣɞȩȳɰɞɴ ɭȝɴɴ ɰȳɗȝɻɇʊȳɗʑ ɯɿɇȩɕɗʑ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ȝɞȯ are resolved after delivery. The most common pregnancy-related health concerns are nausea, vomiting,  constipation,  and  heartburn.

### 6.1. Nausea and vomiting

During your early pregnancy, you may be experiencing episodes of nausea and vomiting, often known as morning sickness. The common perception is that morning sickness happens only in the morning; however, it can happen at any time of the day or night or could last for the whole day. Ǟɣɰɞɇɞȿ ɴɇȩɕɞȳɴɴ ɇɴ ɿɞɭɗȳȝɴȝɞɻ ȝɞȯ ȩȝɞ ɴɇȿɞɇʟȩȝɞɻɗʑ ȝʜȳȩɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȯȝʑ˅ɻɣ˅ȯȝʑ ɗɇȾȳʲ ƫɿɻ ɇɻɴ Ⱦɰȳɯɿȳɞȩʑ and  severity  usually  decline  by  weeks  16  to  20  of  your  pregnancy.  The  recommendations described in Box 12 can help you manage nausea and vomiting [48-50] .

### Box 12. Tips to help manage nausea and vomiting during pregnancy

- Have small, frequent meals every 1-2 hours.
- Limit drinking during your meals.
- Drink small sips of water to stay hydrated and minimize nausea.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɴɣɝȳ ȯɰʑ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɰɇȩȳ ȩȝɕȳɴʳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ȿɰȝɇɞ ɻɣȝɴɻȳȯ Ȩɰȳȝȯʳ ȩɰȝȩɕȳɰɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȯɣ not contain hydrogenated oils, etc.), high protein foods (boiled egg, turkey slices) or plain yogurt.
- Restrict the consumption of foods that have strong odors.
- Limit the consumption fatty and spicy foods.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɴɣɝȳ ȿɇɞȿȳɰ˅ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɣɰ ȯɰɇɞɕɴʳ ɣɰ ȩɄȝɝɣɝɇɗȳʲ
- Ask your doctor if you can take vitamin B6 supplements or other antiemetic medications (drugs that treat nausea and vomiting).
- If symptoms persist, discuss your symptoms with a doctor.

![Picture 122](images/SRC013/picture-122.png)

### 6.2. Constipation

During your pregnancy, you may experience more frequent constipation episodes. Constipation means having fewer than 3 bowel motions per week and having stools that are hard to pass. However, constipation will often resolve itself as pregnancy progresses and after delivery. Your ȩɣɞɴɻɇɭȝɻɇɣɞ ȯɣȳɴ ɞɣɻ ȝʜȳȩɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʳ ɻɄȳ ȯɇɴȩɣɝȾɣɰɻ ɣȩȩɿɰɴ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ɝɣɻɄȳɰ˔ɴ ȿɿɻ ȝɞȯ Ȩɣʋȳɗɴ and is not passed on to the baby. However, constipation may reduce your quality of life and perception of your health as well as increase the risk of haemorrhoids [51] . Box 13 lists a few tips for you to prevent constipation and reduce its symptoms [48, 52-54] .

### Box 13. Tips to help manage constipation during pregnancy

- Ǟȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ȯɰɇɞɕ ȳɞɣɿȿɄ ʠɿɇȯɴ ȯȝɇɗʑʲ
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ȾɰȳɴɄʳ ʋɄɣɗȳ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳɴ ȝɞȯ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴ ˉȩȝɰɰɣɻɴʳ Ȩɰɣȩȩɣɗɇʳ ȿɰȳȳɞ ɭȳȝɴʳ ɭɰɿɞȳɴʳ ȝɭɭɗȳɴʳ ɕɇʋɇʳ ɣɰȝɞȿȳɴʳ Ȩȳɰɰɇȳɴˊʳ ȝɴ ʋȳɗɗ ȝɴ Ȩɰȝɞʳ ȝɴ ɻɄȳʑ ȝɰȳ ɰɇȩɄ ɇɞ ʟȨȳɰʲ
- Ƭɣɞɴɇȯȳɰ ȝȯȯɇɞȿ ʊȝɰɇɣɿɴ ɕɇɞȯɴ ɣȾ ɗȳȿɿɝȳɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɇȳɻʳ ȝɴ ɻɄȳʑ ȝɰȳ ɰɇȩɄ ɇɞ ʟȨȳɰ ȝɴ ʋȳɗɗ ȝɴ protein.
- Do some light physical activity to help enhance the bowel movement.
- If symptoms persist, discuss your symptoms with a healthcare provider.

### 6.3. Heartburn

Heartburn is very common during pregnancy [55] .  It  rarely  leads  to  serious  complications,  and it  usually  resolves  soon  after  delivery.  Y our  doctor  may  recommend  that  you  take  certain medications  that  decrease  the  acidity  in  the  stomach  (antacids).  In  addition,  the  following recommendations may help you reduce the discomfort and symptoms of heartburn (Box 14) [48, 49,  52] .

### Box 14. Tips to help decrease heartburn during pregnancy

- Have small, frequent meals.
- ǘɇɝɇɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɇɞȿ ʠɿɇȯɴ ʋɄɇɗȳ ȳȝɻɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ɝȳȝɗɴʲ
- Eat and chew slowly.
- Limit the consumption of very spicy foods.
- ǘɇɝɇɻ ȩȝɰȨɣɞȝɻȳȯ ȝɞȯ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ˅ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴʲ
- Limit fried and greasy foods.
- Limit citrus foods, tomatoes and mint.
- Do not lay down immediately after eating.
- Use more pillows to raise your head and shoulders when lying down.
- If symptoms persist, discuss your symptoms with a healthcare provider.

![Picture 123](images/SRC013/picture-123.png)

### Physical Activity Recommendations During Pregnancy

#### 7.1. Pregnancy and Physical Activity - Is it safe?

Once you announce your pregnancy and your intention to be physically active, you might face ɴɣɝȳ ɣɿɻȯȝɻȳȯ ɭɰȳɒɿȯɇȩȳɴʴ ˑƲɣɞ˔ɻ ɴɻȝɰɻ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴɇɞȿ ɞɣʋʷ˒ʳ ˑǱɿɞɞɇɞȿ ʋɇɗɗ Ʉɿɰɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ˒ʳ ˑǱȳɴɻ ɇɴ the most important' or 'exercise will not leave enough nutrients for the baby.'

The  above  fears  are  passed  on  from  generation  to  generation  and  are  based  on  outdated guidelines from the 1950s and earlier [56] . Ever since the 1980s, science has debunked the myths with  facts.

Modern science is taking your side. 'Physical activity and exercise in pregnancy are associated ʋɇɻɄ ɝɇɞɇɝȝɗ ɰɇɴɕɴ ȝɞȯ Ʉȝʊȳ Ȩȳȳɞ ɴɄɣʋɞ ɻɣ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻ ɝɣɴɻ ʋɣɝȳɞʳ ȝɗɻɄɣɿȿɄ ɴɣɝȳ ɝɣȯɇʟȩȝɻɇɣɞ to exercise routines may be necessary because of normal anatomic and physiologic changes and fetal requirements.' [57]

It is safe to be physically active throughout a healthy pregnancy, however, any intense exercise regime should be discussed with your family doctor. For more information refer to section 7.3.

![Picture 124](images/SRC013/picture-124.png)

##### ̽ʲ̸ʲ ƫȳɞȳʟɻɴ

Despite  misconceptions,  it  is  important  to  know  that  physical  activity  during  pregnancy  not ɣɞɗʑ Ʉȝɴ ɝɇɞɇɝȝɗ ɰɇɴɕɴ Ȩɿɻ ȝɗɴɣ ɗȳȝȯɴ ɻɣ ɝȝɞʑ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴʲ ǼɄȝɻ ɴȝɇȯʳ ɴɣɝȳ ɝɣȯɇʟȩȝɻɇɣɞɴ ɻɣ exercise habits and intensity are necessary because of the many changes that are taking place in your body during pregnancy.

##### ƫȳɗɣʋ ȝɰȳ ȝ Ⱦȳʋ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿ ɝȝʑ ȿȝɇɞ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɝȝɇɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ ȝ ɴȝȾȳ ɗȳʊȳɗ ɣȾ ɭɄʑɴɇȩȝɗ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻʑ [58] :

- Minimizing morning sickness
- Back pain and swelling of the legs and feet
- Maintaining a healthy body weight
- ǵɻɰȳɞȿɻɄȳɞɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ Ȩɣɞȳɴʳ ɒɣɇɞɻɴ ȝɞȯ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴ
- Ǟȝɇɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ ʠȳʐɇȨɇɗɇɻʑ
- Improving your ability to do everyday activities
- Improving your heart health
- Controlling blood sugar levels, blood pressure and improving blood lipids (increasing levels of good cholesterol (HDL) and decreasing triglycerides levels)
- Ǳȳȯɿȩɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ɻʑɭȳ ̸ ȯɇȝȨȳɻȳɴʳ Ʉʑɭȳɰɻȳɞɴɇɣɞʳ ɒɣɇɞɻ ɣɰ Ȩɣɞȳ ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝɴʳ ɝɿɴȩɗȳ ɗɣɴɴʳ and some types of cancer
- Enhancing the function of your digestive system
- Improving your overall well-being and quality of life
- Lowering stress levels
- Reducing episodes of depression
- Improving breathing
- Improving immunity
- Enhancing sleep quality
- Facilitating postpartum weight loss and recovery
- Reducing the risk of infant obesity, while improving the cardiovascular system, nervous system development and brain development

#### 7.3. Recommendations and contraindications to exercise during pregnancy

The  general  recommendation  is  that  you  perform  a  cumulative  of  40-60  minutes  of  low  to moderate-intensity physical activity for at least 5 days/week. Vigorous-intensity activities are not  encouraged  during  pregnancy [58] .

![Picture 125](images/SRC013/picture-125.png)

Table 9. Exercise recommendations during pregnancy

| FITT                                                                                                               | Aerobic Exercise Program                                                                                                                           | Resistance Exercise Program   |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| ˹ ̻ ȯȝʑɴʿʋȳȳɕ If you were previously inactive, you should gradually increase the frequency to the recommended level | 2-3 days/ week                                                                                                                                     | Frequency                     |
| Low to Moderate                                                                                                    | reaching your planned repetition target, while still having the ability to perform 4                                                               | Intensity                     |
| Accumulate 40 - 60 minutes throughout the day                                                                      | 8-12 repetitions* per set of exercise 1-2 Sets of each exercise Moderate speed movements (6 seconds per repetition*) 2-3 minutes rest between sets | Time                          |
| Cardiovascular endurance activities                                                                                | 8-10 compound exercises that target all ɻɄȳ ɝȝɒɣɰ ɝɿɴȩɗȳ ȿɰɣɿɭɴ                                                                                    | Type                          |

If  you  regularly  engaged  in  vigorous  physical  activity,  or  were  physically  active  prior to  your  pregnancy ,  you  can  continue  being  active  at  this  intensity  level  throughout  your pregnancy. Still, you should coordinate your exercise regime with your healthcare specialist and seek clearance. Be responsible and do not aim for new records and exhausting exercise sessions. Ȓɣɿ ɝȝʑ ɞɣɻɇȩȳ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻʑ ɗȳʊȳɗɴ ȝɞȯ ʟɻɞȳɴɴ ɝȝʑ ȯȳȩɰȳȝɴȳ ȝɴ ʑɣɿɰ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɭɰɣȿɰȳɴɴȳɴʲ So, the best advice will be to always listen to your body and avoid some sorts of exercises altogether (see Box 15 for detailed tips on how to be careful while exercising).

### Box 15. Be careful while exercising

- Don't bump your belly! You want to avoid contact sports and risky physical activities such as martial arts (sparring), football, or horseback riding to reduce the risk of your baby belly getting hit.
- Avoid the extreme! For the upcoming 9 months skip your skiing vacation (above 2500 m altitude) and delay your scuba diving experience to another time. The change in air pressure might be harmful for your baby.
- Control your movements! The production of the hormone relaxin increases in preparation for giving birth [59] ʲ Ǌɻ ʋɇɗɗ ȝʜȳȩɻ ʑɣɿɰ ʠȳʐɇȨɇɗɇɻʑ ȝɞȯ ɴɻȝȨɇɗɇɻʑʲ Ǟɿɴȩɗȳɴ ȝɞȯ ɒɣɇɞɻɴ Ȩȳȩɣɝȳ ɗɣɣɴȳʳ ɴɣ ɇɻ ɇɴ ȝȯʊɇɴȝȨɗȳ ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ɴɿȯȯȳɞ ɝɣʊȳɝȳɞɻɴ ȝɞȯ ɯɿɇȩɕ ȯɇɰȳȩɻɇɣɞȝɗ changes. Engage in an extended warmup and cool down routine. This will decrease your ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ɇɞɒɿɰʑʲ
- Drink a lot of water! Always carry a water bottle with you and drink, before, during ȝɞȯ ȝȾɻȳɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳʷ Ǌɻ ɇɴ ȝȯʊɇɴȝȨɗȳ ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȳʐɻɰȳɝȳ Ʉɣɻ ȝɞȯ Ʉɿɝɇȯ ȳɞʊɇɰɣɞɝȳɞɻɴʲ The exercise itself does not lead to dangerous levels of heat, but you should avoid the hot summer outdoors.
- Posture Control! Over time, but usually around 16 weeks, you will notice a change in body posture, leading to an arching in your back. This might result in lower back pain. Staying physically active and strengthening your core can help. Be careful when strengthening your core at this time and avoid lying on your back. About 10% of expecting women experience low blood pressure while lying on their backs.

In case you had a sedentary lifestyle before pregnancy, you may wish to start by doing ɗɇȿɄɻ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳɴ Ⱦɣɰ ɴɄɣɰɻ ɭȳɰɇɣȯɴ ɣȾ ɻɇɝȳ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȳɞ ɝɣʊȳ ȿɰȝȯɿȝɗɗʑ ɇɞ ɻɇɝȳ ȝɞȯ ȳʜɣɰɻ ȝɴ ʑɣɿ Ⱦȳȳɗ ʟɻʲ  ƶʐȝɝɭɗȳɴ ɣȾ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳɴ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʳ ȳɴɭȳȩɇȝɗɗʑ Ⱦɣɰ Ȩȳȿɇɞɞȳɰɴʳ ȝɰȳ ʋȝɗɕɇɞȿʳ ɴɻȝɻɇɣɞȝɰʑ cycling, water aerobics (or aqua gym), swimming and Pilates.

Below are a few recommendations you may wish to consider regarding your physical activity during  pregnancy:

- ǊȾ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ȝ Ȩȳȿɇɞɞȳɰʳ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦȳʋ ʋȳȳɕɴʳ Ⱦɣȩɿɴ ɣɞ ɴɄɣʋɇɞȿ ɿɭ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿɰ ʋɣɰɕɣɿɻɴ ȝɞȯ gradually increase the exercise duration. You have plenty of time to work on your speed and distance once you established a routine. Start by walking 15 minutes every other day then increase the time by 5 minutes every week until you reach the recommended 40 minutes. Try to exercise on most of the days before you gradually increase the intensity.
- To bring the activity to a suitable intensity level, try the 'talk test' where you should still be able to talk while doing the activity. In case you are not able to maintain a conversation then you should reduce the pace at which you are exercising (for more details on the talk test, refer to Box 16 below).

#### Low Intensity

While engaging in light physical activity, you should be able to carry on a conversation with minimal to ɞɣ ȳʜɣɰɻʲ

![Picture 126](images/SRC013/picture-126.png)

##### Examples:

For most people the warmup, a recreational walk or a relaxed bike ride fall within this category.

#### Vigorous Intensity

While engaging in vigorousintensity physical activities, you will not be able to say more than a few words without pausing for a breath.

![Picture 127](images/SRC013/picture-127.png)

##### Examples:

Running, fast cycling, or interval training can be activities that raise the intensity to a vigorous level.

### Box 16. THE TALK TEST

#### Moderate Intensity

While engaging in moderateintensity activities,  breathing will be more audible, but you will still be able to hold a conversation.

![Picture 128](images/SRC013/picture-128.png)

##### Examples:

For most people noncompetitive exercises such ȝɴ Ȩɰɇɴɕ ʋȝɗɕɇɞȿʳ ɒɣȿȿɇɞȿʳ cycling, or swimming fall within this category.

- Limit single exercise sessions to a maximum of 60 minutes, to avoid overexertion (pushing yourself too hard), dehydration and loss of essential nutrients.
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɰȳɴɇɴɻȝɞȩȳ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳɴ ȝɴ ɻɄȳʑ Ʉȳɗɭ ɴɻɰȳɞȿɻɄȳɞ ɻɄȳ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴ ʋɄɇȩɄ ȝɰȳ ɞȳȳȯȳȯ ʋɄȳɞ giving  birth.  Furthermore,  women  who  regularly  engage  in  strength  training  recover quicker  after  giving  birth  and  are  well  prepared  for  baby  care  activities  such  as  lifting, carrying  and  stroller  pushing.
- Train your muscles 2-3 times a week, on non-consecutive days. It is usually recommended that pregnant women use light to moderate weights and aim for 8-12 repetitions and 1- 2  sets  per exercise. A slow movement speed is advisable: count to 6 while doing one repetition. Gradually increase the repetitions to reach the recommended target of 8-12 [58] . You can also gradually increase the resistance/weight if you easily exceed 12 ɰȳɭȳɻɇɻɇɣɞɴʲ ȋɇȩȳ ʊȳɰɴȝʳ ʑɣɿ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ȯȳȩɰȳȝɴȳ ɻɄȳ ɰȳɴɇɴɻȝɞȩȳʿʋȳɇȿɄɻ ɇȾ ɇɻ ɇɴ ɻɣɣ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻ for you to reach the minimum of 8 repetitions.
- ǵɻɰȳɞȿɻɄ ɻɰȝɇɞɇɞȿ ɇɴ ɞɣɻ ɗɇɝɇɻȳȯ ɻɣ ʟɻɞȳɴɴ ȩȳɞɻȳɰɴʵ ɿɴɇɞȿ ɴɻȝɇɰɴ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȩɣɞɴɇȯȳɰȳȯ ȝɴ a strengthening activity [60] ʳ  ȯȳɭȳɞȯɇɞȿ ɣɞ ʑɣɿɰ ʟɻɞȳɴɴ ɗȳʊȳɗ ȝɞȯ ɻɰɇɝȳɴɻȳɰʲ ǱȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ ǼȝȨɗȳ ̿ ȝȨɣʊȳ Ⱦɣɰ ɰȳɴɇɴɻȝɞȩȳ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴʲ ǼȝȨɗȳ ̷̶ Ȩȳɗɣʋ ɗɇɴɻɴ ɝȝɒɣɰ muscle groups and exercises on how to train them. These exercises are also called compound exercises (more than one muscle involved) and include movements such

as push-ups, pull-ups, or squats. Alternatively, you can work with resistance bands to ȿɰȝȯɿȝɗɗʑ ɇɞȩɰȳȝɴȳ ɻɄȳ ɇɝɭȝȩɻ ɣɰ ɝȝɕȳ ɿɴȳ ɣȾ ɴɻɰȳɞȿɻɄ ɻɰȝɇɞɇɞȿ ɝȝȩɄɇɞȳɴ ɇɞ ȝ ʟɻɞȳɴɴ center.  Machines  are  considered  a  safer  activity  than  using  free  weights  such  as dumbbells  and  barbells.

- Consult Box 15 above (Be careful).

##### Table 10. Examples of resistance exercises for pregnant women

|            | Free-Weights                                                      | Machine-Based                                                     | Body Weight                                    |
|------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| Chest      | Incline Bench Press                                               | Seated chest press                                                | Push-ups                                       |
| Back       | Bent over dumbbell rows                                           | Lat pulldown                                                      | Pull-up                                        |
| Shoulders  | Dumbbell lateral raise                                            | Cable lateral raise                                               | Arm Circles                                    |
| Biceps     | Dumbbell curls                                                    | Cable biceps pulls                                                | Reverse grip pull-ups                          |
| Triceps    | Dumbbell kick backs                                               | Press-downs                                                       | Dips                                           |
| Abdomen    | Weighted abdominal exercises are not recommended during pregnancy | Weighted abdominal exercises are not recommended during pregnancy | Prone planks, Crunches, side plank, leg raises |
| Quadriceps | Back squats                                                       | Leg extension                                                     | Body weight squats                             |
| Hamstrings | Dumbbell Deadlifts                                                | Leg curls                                                         | Hip-ups (bridging)                             |

- Avoid holding your breath while moving weights.
- Avoid momentum - every movement should be fully controlled.
- Continue training your abdominal muscles but exclude weighted abdominal exercises and the rotational abdominal machines.
- Avoid the strong stretches that are caused by overhead and behind the neck exercises, ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩȝɗɗʑ ȝȾɻȳɰ ɻɄȳ ̷̸ɻɄ ʋȳȳɕ ɣȾ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʲ
- Always avoid exercises that may place the baby belly at risk (such as martial arts, football, or horseback riding).
- ǊȾ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ɒɣɇɞɇɞȿ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ȩɗȝɴɴȳɴʳ ɝȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɇɞȾɣɰɝ ɻɄȳ ɇɞɴɻɰɿȩɻɣɰ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑʲ
- Reduce the inactive time throughout the day.
- ƶɞȩɣɿɰȝȿȳ Ⱦȝɝɇɗʑ ȝɞȯ Ⱦɰɇȳɞȯɴ ɻɣ ɒɣɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳ ɴȳɴɴɇɣɞɴ Ⱦɣɰ ɝɣɰȳ ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻʲ
- Make sure to exercise in a cool environment instead of a hot or humid environment. You should avoid exercising outdoors during the hot summer.
- Stay properly hydrated at all times.
- Exercise as tolerated and stop exercising if the following are experienced: abdominal pain, ȯɇʗʗɇɞȳɴɴʳ ɄȳȝȯȝȩɄȳʳ ʊȝȿɇɞȝɗ Ȩɗȳȳȯɇɞȿʳ ɣɰ ʠɿɇȯ ɗȳȝɕȝȿȳʲ ƫȳ ɰȳɴɭɣɞɴɇȨɗȳ ȝɞȯ ȯɣ ɞɣɻ ȝɇɝ Ⱦɣɰ ɞȳʋ ɰȳȩɣɰȯɴ ȝɞȯ ȳʐɄȝɿɴɻɇɞȿ ȳʐȳɰȩɇɴȳ ɴȳɴɴɇɣɞɴʲ ǖȳȳɭ ɇɞ ɝɇɞȯ ɻɄȝɻ ɻɄȳ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴ ȝɞȯ ɒɣɇɞɻɴ might be loose during the pregnancy phase.

Ơɴ ȳʐɭɗȝɇɞȳȯ ȝȨɣʊȳʳ ɭɄʑɴɇȩȝɗ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻʑ Ʉȝɴ ȝ ɞɿɝȨȳɰ ɣȾ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ independent from your pregnancy, it is important to always listen to your body. If you feel any discomfort before, during or after your exercise, it is recommended to stop your exercise and ɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɗɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰʲ Ǌɞ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ȩɣɗɿɝɞ ɣȾ ƫɣʐ ̷̽ʳ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɰȳȝȯ ȝȨɣɿɻ ɰȳȝɴɣɞɴ ɻɣ ɴɻɣɭ ȝɞʑ individual exercise session. These reasons are similar for every healthy adult but include some ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɇɻȳɝɴʲ

- Ǌɞ ɻɄȳ ɴȳȩɣɞȯ ȩɣɗɿɝɞʳ ʑɣɿ ʋɇɗɗ ʟɞȯ ɰȳɗȝɻɇʊȳ ȩɣɞɻɰȝɇɞȯɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȯɇɴȩɿɴɴȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ your doctor. Usually, upon your doctor's advice, you will still be able to participate in low to moderate-intensity physical activity.
- Only if you have signs or conditions that are listed in column 3, also known as absolute contraindications, you should not engage in any moderate to vigorous-intensity exercise. ǘɣʋ˅ɇɞɻȳɞɴɇɻʑ ɭɄʑɴɇȩȝɗ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻʑ ɝȝʑ ɴɻɇɗɗ Ȩȳ Ȩȳɞȳʟȩɇȝɗ ɿɭɣɞ ɻɄȳ ȝɭɭɰɣʊȝɗ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰʲ Box 17 presents a few considerations for exercising among pregnant women [58] .

![Picture 129](images/SRC013/picture-129.png)

It is recommended to consult with your doctor to assess your health condition and discuss the appropriate intensity and type of activity that suits you best.

#### 7.4. One more thing - A Special Strength Training for your Pelvic Floor

ǼɄȳ Ǯȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ɰȳȾȳɰɴ ɻɣ ɻɄȳ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴ ȝɰɣɿɞȯ ʑɣɿɰ Ȩɗȝȯȯȳɰʳ Ȩɣɻɻɣɝʳ ȝɞȯ ʊȝȿɇɞȝʲ Ǌɻ ɇɴ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ ɻɣ ɴɻɰȳɞȿɻɄȳɞ ɻɄȳ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ȯȝɇɗʑ ɻɣ ɰȳȯɿȩȳ ɻɄȳ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ ɿɰɇɞȝɰʑ ɇɞȩɣɞɻɇɞȳɞȩȳ ˉɇʲȳʲʳ ɗȳȝɕɇɞȿ ɿɰɇɞȳ Ȩʑ accident) [61] . Urinary incontinence is quite common during and after pregnancy.

- ǵɻȝɰɻ ʋɇɻɄ ʟɞȯɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴʲ Ȓɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɇɞɇɻɇȝɗɗʑ Ⱦȳȳɗ ɻɄȳɝ Ȩʑ ɻɰʑɇɞȿ ɻɣ ɴɻɣɭ ɻɄȳ ʠɣʋ ɣȾ ɿɰɇɞȳ ʋɄȳɞ ʑɣɿ ȿɣ ɻɣ ɻɄȳ ɻɣɇɗȳɻʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ ɇɻ ɇɴ ɞɣɻ ȝȯʊɇɴȝȨɗȳ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿ ɰȳȿɿɗȝɰɗʑ ɴɻɣɭ ɻɄȳ ʠɣʋ ɣȾ ɿɰɇɞȳ ɝɇȯɴɻɰȳȝɝ ȝɴ ɇɻ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ɄȝɰɝȾɿɗ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ Ȩɗȝȯȯȳɰʲ
- ƫȳȿɇɞɞȳɰɴ ɇȯȳȝɗɗʑ ɻɰȝɇɞ ɇɞ ȝ ɴɇɻɻɇɞȿ ɭɣɴɇɻɇɣɞ ȝɞȯ ɴɯɿȳȳʗȳ ɻɄȳ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴ ̷̶ ɻɣ ̷̻ times at a time. Avoid holding your breath or tightening your stomach, bottom, or thigh muscles at the same time.
- Ȓɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɇȝɭɄɰȝȿɝ ȝɰȳ ʋɣɰɕɇɞȿ ȝɴ ȝ ɻȳȝɝʲ Ǌɻ ɝɇȿɄɻ Ȩȳ ȳȝɴɇȳɰ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿ ɻɣ Ⱦȳȳɗ ȝɞȯ ȝȩɻɇʊȝɻȳ ʑɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ʋɄɇɗȳ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ȨɰȳȝɻɄɇɞȿ ȩȝɗɝɗʑʲ ƫɰȳȝɻɄȳ ɇɞ ȝɞȯ ɰȳɗȝʐ ˆ ȨɰȳȝɻɄȳ ɣɿɻ ȝɞȯ ȝȩɻɇʊȝɻȳ ʑɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰʲ

Ǥɞȩȳ ʑɣɿ ȿȝɇɞ ȩɣɞɻɰɣɗ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ɝɿɴȩɗȳɴʳ Ʉɣɗȯ ȝɞȯ ɴɯɿȳȳʗȳ Ⱦɣɰ ̹ ɴȳȩɣɞȯɴ ȳȝȩɄ ɻɇɝȳʲ And repeat the exercise at least twice a day. After a few weeks, you should start to notice ɇɝɭɰɣʊȳȯ ȝʋȝɰȳɞȳɴɴ ȝɞȯ ɴɻɰȳɞȿɻɄʲ Ȓɣɿ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɝȝɕȳ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ɻɰȝɇɞɇɞȿ ȝ ɄȝȨɇɻʲ Ǥɞȩȳ ʑɣɿ Ʉȝʊȳ Ⱦɿɗɗ ȩɣɞɻɰɣɗ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ɭȳɗʊɇȩ ʠɣɣɰ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɻɰȝɇɞ ȝɞʑʋɄȳɰȳ ȝɻ ȝɞʑ ɻɇɝȳ ʋɇɻɄɣɿɻ ɭȳɣɭɗȳ ɞɣɻɇȩɇɞȿ [62] .

![Picture 130](images/SRC013/picture-130.png)

![Picture 131](images/SRC013/picture-131.png)

food particles and acids that forms on the teeth and can lead to dental decay and gum disease). Gum disease in pregnant women may lead to premature birth (early birth) and low birth weight (very small baby). Thus you are highly encouraged to practice good oral hygiene habits [63, 64] :

- ·
- Floss your teeth once daily.
- Limit foods containing sweets as they may stick to your teeth and cause dental caries.
- Drink water or low-fat milk, while limiting sugar-sweetened beverages.
- Eat fruits rather than drinking fruit juices.
- Receive the necessary oral treatment before delivery if possible.
- The period between the 14th and the 20th week of pregnancy (2nd trimester) is the best time to receive any treatment (including dental X-rays). However, necessary treatments can  still  be  provided  throughout  pregnancy,  including  treatments  for  urgent  conditions requiring immediate care during the 1st trimester.
- Visit the dentist twice a year, or more if needed.

If you are experiencing morning sickness, including vomiting, some of the stomach acid will be left on your teeth. This acid could be harmful as it increases your risk of tooth erosion and dental decay. In this case, you are encouraged to follow the below recommendations [63, 64] :

- Eat small portions of nutritious meals/snacks throughout the day.
- Chew sugar free or Xylitol-containing gum after meals.
- Thoroughly brush your teeth and rinse with a mouthwash that you can buy at the pharmacy (you can also prepare a homemade mouthwash using a teaspoon of baking soda (sodium bicarbonate) in a cup of water can help).
- Refrain from brushing the teeth until 30 minutes after vomiting to prevent damage of tooth  structure.

![Picture 132](images/SRC013/picture-132.png)

### Emotional Health and Wellness

Ǌɻ  ɇɴ  ɒɿɴɻ  ȝɴ  ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ  ɻɣ  ɻȝɕȳ  ȩȝɰȳ  ɣȾ  ʑɣɿɰ  ɝȳɞɻȝɗ  ɄȳȝɗɻɄ  ȝɞȯ  ʋȳɗɗȨȳɇɞȿ  ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ȝɴ your physical health. If you are mentally healthy, you will be in the best position to manage the challenges of pregnancy and life with a new baby.

ǵɣɝȳ ʋɣɝȳɞ ȳʐɭȳɰɇȳɞȩȳ ɒɣʑ  ȝɞȯ  Ⱦɿɗʟɗɗɝȳɞɻ  ȯɿɰɇɞȿ  ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ  ȝɞȯ  ʋɄȳɞ  ȿɇʊɇɞȿ  ȨɇɰɻɄʳ  ʋɄɇɗȳ ɣɻɄȳɰɴ ȳʐɭȳɰɇȳɞȩȳ ȝɞʐɇȳɻʑʳ ȩɣɞȾɿɴɇɣɞʳ ɣɰ ɴȝȯɞȳɴɴʲ Ǟȳɞɻȝɗ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝɴ ȝʜȳȩɻ ȝ ȩɣɞɴɇȯȳɰȝȨɗȳ proportion of pregnant women during pregnancy and after delivery. These mental health issues may lead to poor health for the mother, father, and infant. While some women overcome their mental health problems, many develop chronic conditions. It is always advisable to get in contact ʋɇɻɄ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ʋɄȳɞ ȳʐɭȳɰɇȳɞȩɇɞȿ ȝɞʑ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋɇɞȿʴ ɴȝȯɞȳɴɴʳ ɗȝȩɕ ɣȾ ȳɞɒɣʑɝȳɞɻʳ ȩɰʑɇɞȿ episodes, worry, fear, being overwhelmed, anger, moodiness, , and trouble sleeping.

Box 18 below lists some strategies that can help you care for your emotional wellbeing.

### Box 18. Tips to help pregnant women care for their emotional wellbeing

- Connect with family and friends.
- Exercise regularly, when applicable (Refer to section 7).
- Ǯɗȝɞ ȳɞɒɣʑȝȨɗȳ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻɇȳɴʲ
- Ơȩȩȳɭɻ ɣʜȳɰɴ ɣȾ Ʉȳɗɭ Ⱦɰɣɝ Ⱦȝɝɇɗʑ ȝɞȯ Ⱦɰɇȳɞȯɴʲ
- ƶɞɒɣʑ ɴɻɰȳɻȩɄɇɞȿ ɴȳɴɴɇɣɞɴʲ
- Practice compassion and kindness with yourself and others.
- Involve your husband in your regular medical appointments so that he is acquainted ʋɇɻɄ ɻɄȳ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻɇȳɴ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ȿɣɇɞȿ ɻɄɰɣɿȿɄʵ ȝɴ ɴɿȩɄ Ʉȳ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻɇʊȳ ȝɞȯ ɝɣɰȳ understanding.
