### ǊǞǮǤǱǼƠǟǼ ǟǤǼƶ

ǊȾ ʑɣɿ ɴɿɴɭȳȩɻ ɻɄȝɻ ɴɣɝȳɻɄɇɞȿ ɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȯɇȳɻ ɝɇȿɄɻ Ȩȳ ȝʜȳȩɻɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɣɰ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ Ȩȳȩɣɝȳɴ Ⱦɿɴɴʑ ɣɰ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɴ ȝ ɰȝɴɄʳ ȯɇȝɰɰɄȳȝ ɣɰ ʋɄȳȳʗɇɞȿ ɴɣɣɞ ȝȾɻȳɰ ɞɿɰɴɇɞȿʳ ȩɣɞɴɿɗɻ ɻɄȳ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ˍ ̺̺ˎ .

### ̻ʲ̹ʲ     Ʋɇȝȿɞɣɴɇɴ ɣȾ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ

ǼɄȳ ȯɇȝȿɞɣɴɇɴ ɣȾ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ ɇɞ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ Ȩȳ ȯɣɞȳ Ȩʑ ȝ ȯɣȩɻɣɰʵ ʑɣɿ  ɴɄɣɿɗȯ  ɞɣɻ  ȯɇȝȿɞɣɴȳ  ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ  Ȩʑ  ʑɣɿɰɴȳɗȾʳ  ɻɣ  ȝʊɣɇȯ  ȝɞʑ ɿɞɞȳȩȳɴɴȝɰʑ ɰȳɴɻɰɇȩɻɇɣɞɴ ˍ̺̺ˎ ʲ  Ǌɞ  ɻɄȳ  ȩȝɴȳ ʋɄȳɰȳ ȝ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿʑ ȯɇȝȿɞɣɴɇɴ ɇɴ ȩɣɞʟɰɝȳȯʳ ɻɄȳ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ʋɇɗɗ ȩȝɰȳȾɿɗɗʑ Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋ ɿɭ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ȿɰɣʋɻɄ ȝɞȯ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɝȳɞɻʲ

### ƠǮǮƶǟƲǊȑ ̷ʴ ȌǇƠǼ Ǌǵ ǼǇƶ ƫƠƫȒ˅ǁǱǊƶǟƲǘȒ ǇǤǵǮǊǼƠǘ ǊǟǊǼǊƠǼǊȋƶ ˉƫǁǇǊˊʹ

ǼɄȳ  ƫȝȨʑ˅ǁɰɇȳɞȯɗʑ  Ǉɣɴɭɇɻȝɗ  Ǌɞɇɻɇȝɻɇʊȳ  ʋȝɴ  ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭȳȯ  Ȩʑ  ȀǟǊƬƶǁ  ȝɞȯ  ȌǇǤ  ɻɣ  ȝɴɴɇɴɻ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ  Ⱦȝȩɇɗɇɻɇȳɴ  ȝɰɣɿɞȯ  ɻɄȳ  ʋɣɰɗȯ  ɻɣ  ɇɝɭɗȳɝȳɞɻ  ɭɰȝȩɻɇȩȳɴ  ɻɄȝɻ  ɭɰɣɻȳȩɻʳ  ɭɰɣɝɣɻȳ  ȝɞȯ  ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ Ǌɻ ɇɴ ȝ ȿɗɣȨȝɗ ȳʜɣɰɻ ɻɣ ɇɝɭɰɣʊȳ ɝȝɻȳɰɞɇɻʑ ɴȳɰʊɇȩȳɴ ɴɣ ɻɄȝɻ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ȩȝɞ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɞȳʋȨɣɰɞɴ ȝɞȯ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɝ ɻɄȳ Ȩȳɴɻ ɴɻȝɰɻ ɇɞ ɗɇȾȳʲ ǼɄȳ ɇɞɇɻɇȝɻɇʊȳ Ʉȝɴ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȳȯ ȝ ɻɣɻȝɗ ɣȾ Ǽȳɞ ǵɻȳɭɴ ɻɄȝɻ Ʉɣɴɭɇɻȝɗɴ ȝɞȯ ɝȝɻȳɰɞɇɻʑ ʋȝɰȯɴ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ȝȯɣɭɻ ɻɣ ȳɞɴɿɰȳ ɻɄȝɻ ȝɗɗ ʋɣɝȳɞ ȝɞȯ ɞȳʋȨɣɰɞɴ ɰȳȩȳɇʊȳ  ȝȯȳɯɿȝɻȳ  ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻ  Ⱦɣɰ  ɇɞȾȝɞɻ  Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ  ǼɄȳɰȳ  ɇɴ  ɴɻɰɣɞȿ  ȳʊɇȯȳɞȩȳ  ɻɄȝɻ  Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋɇɞȿ  ɻɄȳ  Ǽ ȳɞ ǵɻȳɭɴ ʋɣɿɗȯ ȩɣɞɻɰɇȨɿɻȳ ɻɣ ȝ ɴɇȿɞɇʟȩȝɞɻ ɇɝɭɰɣʊȳɝȳɞɻ ɇɞ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɰȝɻȳɴ ȝɞȯ ɴɿȩȩȳɴɴʲ ǰȝɻȝɰ ɇɴ ȝɝɣɞȿ ɻɄȳ ȩɣɿɞɻɰɇȳɴ ɻɄȝɻ Ʉȝʊȳ ȝȯɣɭɻȳȯ ɻɄȳ ƫǁǇǊʳ ȝȯʊɣȩȝɻɇɞȿ Ⱦɣɰ ɇɻɴ ɇɝɭɗȳɝȳɞɻȝɻɇɣɞ ȝȩɰɣɴɴ ȝɗɗ  ɄȳȝɗɻɄȩȝɰȳ  ɇɞɴɻɇɻɿɻɇɣɞɴ  ɭɰɣʊɇȯɇɞȿ  ɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ  ȝɞȯ  ȩɄɇɗȯ  ɴȳɰʊɇȩȳɴʲ  ǼɄȳ  ȩɣɿɞɻɰʑ  Ʉȝɴ  ɻȝɕȳɞ  ɴɻȳɭɴ ɻɣʋȝɰȯɴ ɻɄȳ ȳɴɻȝȨɗɇɴɄɝȳɞɻ ɣȾ ȝ ȨȝȨʑ Ⱦɰɇȳɞȯɗʑ ȳɞʊɇɰɣɞɝȳɞɻ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ Ʉɣɴɭɇɻȝɗɴ ȝɞȯ ȩɗɇɞɇȩɴ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ǵɻȝɻȳ ɣȾ ǰȝɻȝɰ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ɭɰɣɝɣɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ȩɣɝɝɿɞɇɻʑ ˍ ̺̻ˎ .

### ǼɄȳ Ǽȳɞ ǵɻȳɭɴʴ

## Critical Management Procedures

- ̷ȝʲ    Ƭɣɝɭɗʑ Ⱦɿɗɗʑ ʋɇɻɄ ɻɄȳ Ǌɞɻȳɰɞȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ Ƭɣȯȳ ɣȾ Ǟȝɰɕȳɻɇɞȿ ɣȾ ƫɰȳȝɴɻɝɇɗɕ ǵɿȨɴɻɇɻɿɻȳɴ ȝɞȯ ɰȳɗȳʊȝɞɻ Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ ƠɴɴȳɝȨɗʑ ɰȳɴɣɗɿɻɇɣɞɴʲ
- ̷Ȩʲ    Ǉȝʊȳ ȝ ʋɰɇɻɻȳɞ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɭɣɗɇȩʑ ɻɄȝɻ ɇɴ ɰɣɿɻɇɞȳɗʑ ȩɣɝɝɿɞɇȩȝɻȳȯ ɻɣ ɴɻȝʜ ȝɞȯ ɭȝɰȳɞɻɴʲ
- ̷ȩʲ    ƶɴɻȝȨɗɇɴɄ ɣɞȿɣɇɞȿ ɝɣɞɇɻɣɰɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ȯȝɻȝ˅ɝȝɞȝȿȳɝȳɞɻ ɴʑɴɻȳɝɴʲ
- ̸ʲ     ƶɞɴɿɰȳ ɻɄȝɻ ɴɻȝʜ Ʉȝɴ ɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ɕɞɣʋɗȳȯȿȳʳ ȩɣɝɭȳɻȳɞȩȳʳ ȝɞȯ ɴɕɇɗɗɴ ɻɣ ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ

## Key Clinical Practices

- ̹ʲ     Ʋɇɴȩɿɴɴ ɻɄȳ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞȩȳ ȝɞȯ ɝȝɞȝȿȳɝȳɞɻ ɣȾ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ʋɇɻɄ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞɻ ʋɣɝȳɞ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȳɇɰ Ⱦȝɝɇɗɇȳɴʲ
- ̺ʲ     ǁȝȩɇɗɇɻȝɻȳ ɇɝɝȳȯɇȝɻȳ ȝɞȯ ɿɞɇɞɻȳɰɰɿɭɻȳȯ ɴɕɇɞ˅ɻɣ˅ɴɕɇɞ ȩɣɞɻȝȩɻ ȝɞȯ ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ɻɣ ɇɞɇɻɇȝɻȳ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɴ ɴɣɣɞ ȝɴ ɭɣɴɴɇȨɗȳ ȝȾɻȳɰ ȨɇɰɻɄʲ
- ̻ʲ     ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ɻɣ ɇɞɇɻɇȝɻȳ ȝɞȯ ɝȝɇɞɻȝɇɞ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ɝȝɞȝȿȳ ȩɣɝɝɣɞ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻɇȳɴʲ
- ̼ʲ     Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ ɭɰɣʊɇȯȳ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȯ ɞȳʋȨɣɰɞɴ ȝɞʑ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɣɰ ʠɿɇȯɴ ɣɻɄȳɰ ɻɄȝɞ Ȩɰȳȝɴɻɝɇɗɕʳ ɿɞɗȳɴɴ ɝȳȯɇȩȝɗɗʑ ɇɞȯɇȩȝɻȳȯʲ
- ̽ʲ     ƶɞȝȨɗȳ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ɻɣ ɰȳɝȝɇɞ ɻɣȿȳɻɄȳɰ ȝɞȯ ɻɣ ɭɰȝȩɻɇȩȳ ɰɣɣɝɇɞȿ˅ɇɞ ̸̺ Ʉɣɿɰɴ ȝ ȯȝʑʲ
- ̾ʲ     ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ɻɣ ɰȳȩɣȿɞɇʗȳ ȝɞȯ ɰȳɴɭɣɞȯ ɻɣ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ˔ ȩɿȳɴ Ⱦɣɰ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ
- ̿ʲ     Ƭɣɿɞɴȳɗ ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ɿɴȳ ȝɞȯ ɰɇɴɕɴ ɣȾ ɿɴɇɞȿ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ Ȩɣɻɻɗȳɴʳ ɻȳȝɻɴ ȝɞȯ ɭȝȩɇʟȳɰɴʲ
- ̷̶ʲ   Ƭɣɣɰȯɇɞȝɻȳ ȯɇɴȩɄȝɰȿȳ ɴɣ ɻɄȝɻ ɭȝɰȳɞɻɴ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ Ʉȝʊȳ ɻɇɝȳɗʑ ȝȩȩȳɴɴ ɻɣ ɣɞȿɣɇɞȿ ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻ ȝɞȯ ȩȝɰȳʲ

### ǱƶǁƶǱƶǟƬƶǵ

1. Ǟɇɞɇɴɻɰʑ ɣȾ ǇȳȝɗɻɄʲ ǰȝɻȝɰ Ʋɇȳɻȝɰʑ ǂɿɇȯȳɗɇɞȳɴʵ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǯɰɣɝɣɻɇɣɞ ȝɞȯ ǟɣɞ˅ȩɣɝɝɿɞɇȩȝȨɗȳ Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳɴ ǵȳȩɻɇɣɞʳ ǮɿȨɗɇȩ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ʋȳɭȝɰɻɝȳɞɻʴ ƲɣɄȝʳ ǰȝɻȝɰʳ ̸̶̷̻ʵ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿ ʋʋʋʲȾȝɣʲɣɰȿʿ̹ʿȝʗ̶̿̾ȳʿȝʗ̶̿̾ȳʲɭȯȾʲ
2. Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞ Ǳȳȿɇɣɞȝɗ Ǥʝȩȳ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ƶȝɴɻȳɰɞ Ǟȳȯɇɻȳɰɰȝɞȳȝɞʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȳɝɰɣʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɄȳȝɗɻɄ˅ɻɣɭɇȩɴʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿɇɞȯȳʐʲɄɻɝɗ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̶ Ơɭɰɇɗ ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
3. Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ ǊɞȾȝɞɻ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɞȿ ȩɄɇɗȯ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲ ʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɞȳʋɴ˅ɰɣɣɝʿȾȝȩɻ˅ɴɄȳȳɻɴʿȯȳɻȝɇɗʿɇɞȾȝɞɻ˅ȝɞȯ˅ʑɣɿɞȿ˅ȩɄɇɗȯ˅Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̸̸ ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
4. ̺ʲ ƫȳɰɞȝɰȯɣʳ Ǉʲʵ Ƭȳɴȝɰʳ ȋʲʵ Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ ǘɣɞȿ˅ɻȳɰɝ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ɣȾ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʴ ȝ  ɴʑɴɻȳɝȝɻɇȩ  ɰȳʊɇȳʋʵ  Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʴ  ǂȳɞȳʊȝʳ  ǵʋɇɻʗȳɰɗȝɞȯʳ  ̸̶̷̹ʵ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿȝɭɭɴʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɇɰɇɴʿȨɇɻɴɻɰȳȝɝʿɄȝɞȯɗȳʿ̷̶̼̼̻ʿ̷̽̿̿̾ʿ̸̷̶̶̺̻̻̹̿̽̾̿̽ˈȳɞȿʲ ɭȯȾʵɒɴȳɴɴɇɣɞɇȯ˵ƶƲƠ̼̿ǁ̶̶ƶ̼̼ƫƲ̶̶ǁƲ̷̷̼̾ƫƲǁ̶̸̼̻̺̻̿Ơʹɴȳɯɿȳɞȩȳ˵̷ʲ
5. ̻ʲ Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǤɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʿȀǟǊƬƶǁʲ  Ǌɞȯɇȩȝɻɣɰɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  ȝɴɴȳɴɴɇɞȿ  ɇɞȾȝɞɻ  ȝɞȯ  ʑɣɿɞȿ  ȩɄɇɗȯ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɭɰȝȩɻɇȩȳɴʴ ȯȳʟɞɇɻɇɣɞɴ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɴɿɰȳɝȳɞɻ ɝȳɻɄɣȯɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲ ʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɭɿȨɗɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴʿɇʿɇɻȳɝʿ̸̶̶̷̺̹̿̽̾̿̾̾̿  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̸̺  Ơɭɰɇɗ  ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
6. Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞ  Ǳȳȿɇɣɞȝɗ  Ǥʝȩȳ  Ⱦɣɰ  ɻɄȳ  ƶȝɴɻȳɰɞ  Ǟȳȯɇɻȳɰɰȝɞȳȝɞʲ  ƶʐȩɗɿɴɇʊȳɗʑ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯ Ⱦɣɰ ̼ ɝɣɞɻɄɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȳɝɰɣʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿɇɞȯȳʐʲɄɻɝɗ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ȑ̷̷  Ơɭɰɇɗ  ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
7. ̽ʲ Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɞȳʋɴ˅ ɰɣɣɝʿȾȝȩɻɴ˅ɇɞ˅ɭɇȩɻɿɰȳɴʿȯȳɻȝɇɗʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̼  Ơɭɰɇɗ  ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
8. ̾ʲ ȀǵƲƠ ˅ ȌǊƬ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻʲ Ǯɗɿȿȿȳȯ ȯɿȩɻɴʳ ɝȝɴɻɇɻɇɴ ȝɞȯʳ ɻɄɰɿɴɄʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋɇȩȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȾɞɴʲɿɴȯȝʲȿɣʊʿɭɗɿȿȿȳȯ˅ȯɿȩɻɴ˅ɝȝɴɻɇɻɇɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɻɄɰɿɴɄ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
9. ̿ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʴ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦȳʋ ȯȝʑɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲ ɞɄɴʲɿɕʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʿȨȝȨʑʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿɻɄȳ˅ʟɰɴɻ˅Ⱦȳʋ˅ ȯȝʑɴʿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
10. ȀǟǊƬƶǁʲ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɿɞɇȩȳȾʲɣɰȿʿɻɣɭɇȩɴʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
11. Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ  Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  Ȍȳȳɕ  ̸̶̸̶  Ǟȳɴɴȝȿȳʲ  ǔɣɇɞɻ  ɝȳɴɴȝȿȳʴ ȀǟǊƬƶǁ  ƶʐȳȩɿɻɇʊȳ  Ʋɇɰȳȩɻɣɰ  Ǉȳɞɰɇȳɻɻȝ  Ǉʲ  ǁɣɰȳ  ȝɞȯ  ȌǇǤ  Ʋɇɰȳȩɻɣɰ˅ǂȳɞȳɰȝɗ  Ǽȳȯɰɣɴ ƠȯɄȝɞɣɝ  ǂɄȳȨɰȳʑȳɴɿɴʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɞȳʋɴʿɇɻȳɝʿ̷̹˅̶̽˅̸̶̸̶˅ ʋɣɰɗȯ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ʋȳȳɕ˅̸̶̸̶˅ɝȳɴɴȝȿȳ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̷  Ơɭɰɇɗ  ̸̶̸̶ˊʲ

12. Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ ǊɞȾȝɞɻ ȝɞȯ ʑɣɿɞȿ ȩɄɇɗȯ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ Ǟɣȯȳɗ ƬɄȝɭɻȳɰ Ⱦɣɰ ɻȳʐɻȨɣɣɕɴ Ⱦɣɰ  ɝȳȯɇȩȝɗ  ɴɻɿȯȳɞɻɴ  ȝɞȯ  ȝɗɗɇȳȯ  ɄȳȝɗɻɄ  ɭɰɣȾȳɴɴɇɣɞȝɗɴʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲ ɇɞɻʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿɭɿȨɗɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴʿɇɞȾȝɞɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿ̸̷̺̻̺̺̿̽̾̿̿̽̿ʲɭȯȾ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̼ Ơɭɰɇɗ ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
13. ƶɇȯȳɗɝȝɞʳ Ơʲ Ǌʲʵ ǵȩɄȝɞɗȳɰʳ Ǳʲ ǔʲʵ ǔɣɄɞɴɻɣɞʳ Ǟʲʵ ǘȝɞȯȳɰɴʳ ǵʲʵ ǟɣȨɗȳʳ ǘʲʵ ǵʗɿȩɴʳ ǖʲʵ ȋɇȳɄɝȝɞɞʳ ǘʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ɻɄȳ ɿɴȳ ɣȾ Ʉɿɝȝɞ ɝɇɗɕʲ Ǯȳȯɇȝɻɰɇȩɴ ̸̶̷̸ʳ ̷̸̿ʳ ȳ̸̾̽˅ȳ̷̺̾ʲ
3. ̷̺ʲ ȀǟǊƬƶǁʲ Ǉɣʋ ɻɣ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿɴɇɻȳɴʲɿɞɇȩȳȾʲɣɰȿʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿ ʟɗȳɴʿƫɰɣȩɄɿɰȳˈɄɣʋˈɻɣˈȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯʲǮƲǁ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̿ Ơɭɰɇɗ ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ
4. ̷̻ʲ Ơɿɴɻɰȝɗɇȝɞ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ Ơɴɴɣȩɇȝɻɇɣɞʲ ǁɗȝɻ ȝɞȯ ɇɞʊȳɰɻȳȯ ɞɇɭɭɗȳɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿ ʋʋʋʲȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȝɴɞʲȝɿʿɰȳɴɣɿɰȩȳɴʿʠȝɻ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɇɞʊȳɰɻȳȯ˅ɞɇɭɭɗȳɴ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̶̹ ǟɣʊȳɝȨȳɰ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
16. Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ȩɣɿɞɴȳɗɗɇɞȿ  ɻɰȝɇɞȳɰ˔ɴ  ȿɿɇȯȳʵ  Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʴ ǂȳɞȳʊȝʳ ǵʋɇɻʗȳɰɗȝɞȯʳ ̷̹̿̿ʵ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿ ɭɿȨɗɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴʿɇʿɇɻȳɝʿȌǇǤ˅ƬƲǱ˅̹̿ʲ̹˅̻ʲ
6. ̷̽ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʴ ɇɴ ɝʑ ȨȝȨʑ ȿȳɻɻɇɞȿ ȳɞɣɿȿɄ ɝɇɗɕʹ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞɄɴʲɿɕʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʿȨȝȨʑʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝɴʿȳɞɣɿȿɄ˅ɝɇɗɕʿʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵ǵɇȿɞɴ̸̶̉ʑɣɿɰ̸̶̉ȨȝȨʑ̸̶̉ɇɴ̸̶̉ȿȳɻɻɇɞȿ̸̶̉ ȳɞɣɿȿɄ̸̶̉ɝɇɗɕ˞ɻȳʐɻ˵ǼɄȳʑ̸̶̉ɴȳȳɝ̸̶̉ȩȝɗɝ̸̶̉ȝɞȯ̸̶̉ɰȳɗȝʐȳȯʳȝɞȯ̸̶̉ɴȝɻɇɴʟȳȯ̸̶̉ ȝȾɻȳɰ̸̶̉ɝɣɴɻ̸̶̉Ⱦȳȳȯɴ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
7. ̷̾ʲ Ƭȳɞɻȳɰɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳ  Ƭɣɞɻɰɣɗ  ȝɞȯ  Ǯɰȳʊȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ  Ǉɣʋ  ɝɿȩɄ  ȝɞȯ  Ʉɣʋ  ɣȾɻȳɞ  ɻɣ  ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȩȯȩʲȿɣʊʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿɇɞȾȝɞɻȝɞȯɻɣȯȯɗȳɰɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿ Ʉɣʋ˅ɝɿȩɄ˅ȝɞȯ˅Ʉɣʋ˅ɣȾɻȳɞʲɄɻɝɗʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵Ǥʊȳɰ̸̶̉ɻɄȳ̸̶̉ʟɰɴɻ̸̶̉Ⱦȳʋ̸̶̉ʋȳȳɕɴʳɣȾ̸̶̉ ̸̶̺̉ɻɣ̸̶̸̶̻̉̉Ʉɣɿɰɴ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
8. ̷̿ʲ Ơȩȝȯȳɝʑ  ɣȾ  ǟɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ  ȝɞȯ  Ʋɇȳɻȳɻɇȩɴʲ  ǵɿɭɭɗȳɝȳɞɻɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȯ  ȨȝȨɇȳɴʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȳȝɻɰɇȿɄɻʲɣɰȿʿȾɣɣȯʿʊɇɻȝɝɇɞɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɴɿɭɭɗȳɝȳɞɻɴʿȯɇȳɻȝɰʑ˅ɴɿɭɭɗȳɝȳɞɻɴʿ ɴɿɭɭɗȳɝȳɞɻɴ˅Ⱦɣɰ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȯ˅ȨȝȨɇȳɴ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
20. Ƭȳɞɻȳɰɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳ  Ƭɣɞɻɰɣɗ  ȝɞȯ  Ǯɰȳʊȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ȝɞȯ  ɴɭȳȩɇȝɗ  ȩɇɰȩɿɝɴɻȝɞȩȳɴʴ ɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ ɣɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ ɇɗɗɞȳɴɴȳɴ ɣɰ ȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȩȯȩʲȿɣʊʿ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ɴɭȳȩɇȝɗ˅ȩɇɰȩɿɝɴɻȝɞȩȳɴʿɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ˅ɣɰ˅ɇɞȾȝɞɻ˅ɇɗɗɞȳɴɴȳɴʿɇɞȯȳʐʲɄɻɝɗ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̼  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
21. Ǳȝʑɝɣɞȯʳ ǔʲʵ  Ǟɣɰɰɣʋʳ  ǖʲ  ǖɰȝɿɴȳ  ȝɞȯ  ǞȝɄȝɞ˔ɴ  ǁɣɣȯ  ˞  ɻɄȳ  ǟɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ  Ƭȝɰȳ  Ǯɰɣȩȳɴɴʳ  ̷̻ɻɄ ƶȯɇɻɇɣɞ  ȳȯʵ  ƶɗɴȳʊɇȳɰʴ  ̸̶̸̶ʵ  ɭɭʲ

22. Ơɞɞȝ ƫɿɰȨɇȯȿȳ ˅ ǘȝ ǘȳȩɄȳ ǘȳȝȿɿȳ ǂƫʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ȝ ɝɣɻɄȳɰ˔ɴ ȯɇȳɻʴ ɝʑɻɄɴ ȝɞȯ Ⱦȝȩɻɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɗȝɗȳȩɄȳʲɣɰȿʲɿɕʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅ȝ˅ɝɣɻɄȳɰɴ˅ȯɇȳɻ˅ɝʑɻɄɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ Ⱦȝȩɻɴʿʾˈȳȯɞ̻ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̺ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
23. ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ  Ƭȳɞɻȳɰ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ƭɣɝɭɗȳɝȳɞɻȝɰʑ  ȝɞȯ  Ǌɞɻȳȿɰȝɻɇʊȳ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄʲ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ɇɞȾɣɰɝȝɻɇɣɞʴ  ȳɞȳɰȿʑ  ȯɰɇɞɕɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞȩȩɇɄʲɞɇɄʲȿɣʊʿɄȳȝɗɻɄʿȳɞȳɰȿʑ˅ȯɰɇɞɕɴʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵ǘȝɰȿȳ̸̶̉ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ̸̶̉ɣȾ̸̶̉ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ̸̶̉ɝȝʑʳȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɇɞȿ̸̶̉ȩȝɰȯɇɣʊȝɴȩɿɗȝɰ̸̶̉ȝɞȯ̸̶̉ ɞȳɰʊɣɿɴ̸̶̉ɴʑɴɻȳɝɴʲ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̿  ǔɿɗʑ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
3. ̸̺ʲ Ʋɰɿȿɴ ȝɞȯ ǘȝȩɻȝɻɇɣɞ ƲȝɻȝȨȝɴȳ ˉǘȝȩɻǞȳȯˊʲ Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞȩȨɇʲ ɞɗɝʲɞɇɄʲȿɣʊʿȨɣɣɕɴʿǟƫǖ̶̷̻̺̼̽ʿ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̺  ǔɿɗʑ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
4. ̸̻ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ Ǌɞɴɻɇɻɿɻȳɴ ɣȾ ǇȳȝɗɻɄʲ Ǟɣȯȳɰȝɻȳ ȯȝɇɗʑ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ ɝȝʑ ɗȳȝȯ ɻɣ  ɴɝȝɗɗȳɰ  ȨɇɰɻɄ  ɴɇʗȳʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞɇɄʲȿɣʊʿɞȳʋɴ˅ȳʊȳɞɻɴʿɞȳʋɴ˅ɰȳɗȳȝɴȳɴʿ ɝɣȯȳɰȝɻȳ˅ȯȝɇɗʑ˅ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ˅ɇɞɻȝɕȳ˅ȯɿɰɇɞȿ˅ɭɰȳȿɞȝɞȩʑ˅ɝȝʑ˅ɗȳȝȯ˅ɴɝȝɗɗȳɰ˅ȨɇɰɻɄ˅ɴɇʗȳ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ ̷̺ ǔɿɗʑ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
26. Ơɿɴɻɰȝɗɇȝɞ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ Ơɴɴɣȩɇȝɻɇɣɞʲ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ȩɣɞɴɿɝɭɻɇɣɞʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȝɴɞʲȝɿʿȨʟɞȾɣʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ˅ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ˅ȩɣɞɴɿɝɭɻɇɣɞ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̺ ǔɿɗʑ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
6. ̸̽ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ȝɞȯ  ȯɇȳɻʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞɄɴʲ ɿɕʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʿȨȝȨʑʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɗɇȾȳɴɻʑɗȳʿ ȯɇȳɻʿʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳ̸̶̉ȝɞȯ̸̶̉ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˞ɻȳʐɻ˵Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳ̸̶̉ɇɴ̸̶̉ȝ̸̶̉ ɴɻɇɝɿɗȝɞɻ̸̶̉ȝɞȯʳɝɿȿ̸̶̉ɣȾ̸̶̉ʟɗɻȳɰ̸̶̉ȩɣʜȳȳ̹̉Ở̸̶̷̶̺ɝȿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̸̹ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
7. ̸̾ʲ ƠɗȨȳɰɻȝ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳɴʲ  ǟɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ  ȿɿɇȯȳɗɇɞȳʴ  ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ  Ⱦɣɰ  ɻɄȳ  ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ɝɣɻɄȳɰʵ Ƭȝɞȝȯȝʳ ̸̶̷̾ʵ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȝɗȨȳɰɻȝɄȳȝɗɻɄɴȳɰʊɇȩȳɴʲȩȝʿȝɴɴȳɻɴʿɇɞȾɣʿ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿɇȾ˅ɞȾɴ˅ɞȿ˅ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰ˅ɻɄȳ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ɝɣɻɄȳɰʲɭȯȾʲ
8. ̸̿ʲ Ƭȳɞɻȳɰɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳ  Ƭɣɞɻɰɣɗ  ȝɞȯ  Ǯɰȳʊȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ  ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ȝɞȯ  ɴɭȳȩɇȝɗ  ȩɇɰȩɿɝɴɻȝɞȩȳɴʴ ȩɣɞɻɰȝɇɞȯɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴ ɻɣ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɣɰ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȳʐɭɰȳɴɴȳȯ Ȩɰȳȝɴɻ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɣ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȩȯȩʲȿɣʊʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ɴɭȳȩɇȝɗ˅ȩɇɰȩɿɝɴɻȝɞȩȳɴʿ ȩɣɞɻɰȝɇɞȯɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴ˅ɻɣ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲɄɻɝɗ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̷̼  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
30. Ȍɣɰɗȯ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ Ǟȝɻȳɰɞȝɗʳ ɞȳʋȨɣɰɞʳ ȩɄɇɗȯ ȝɞȯ ȝȯɣɗȳɴȩȳɞɻ ɄȳȝɗɻɄʴ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʳ ɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ȝɞȯ ȳʊȳɰʑȯȝʑ ɗɇʊɇɞȿʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɝȝɻȳɰɞȝɗˈȩɄɇɗȯˈ ȝȯɣɗȳɴȩȳɞɻʿɻɣɭɇȩɴʿȩɄɇɗȯʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿɄɇʊɇȾˈɯȝʿȿȳɞȳɰȝɗʿɯ̷̹ʿȳɞʿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̼ Ơɭɰɇɗ ̸̶̸̷ˊʲ

31. Ƭȳɞɻȳɰɴ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳ  Ƭɣɞɻɰɣɗ  ȝɞȯ  Ǯɰȳʊȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ  ǂɿɇȯȳɗɇɞȳɴ  ȝɞȯ  ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴʴ  Ǯɰɣɭȳɰ ɴɻɣɰȝȿȳ ȝɞȯ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȝɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ Ȩɰȳȝɴɻ ɝɇɗɕ ˅ Ⱦɰȳɯɿȳɞɻɗʑ ȝɴɕȳȯ ɯɿȳɴɻɇɣɞɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿ ʋʋʋʲȩȯȩʲȿɣʊʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȝɻɇɣɞɴʿȾȝɯʲɄɻɝɗʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵Ơɴ̸̶̉ɗɣɞȿ̸̶̉ȝɴ̸̶̉ ɻɄȳ̸̶̉ɻȳɝɭȳɰȝɻɿɰȳʳʋɇɻɄɇɞ̸̶̸̶̼̉̉ɝɣɞɻɄɴ̸̶̉ɇɴ̸̶̉ȨȳɴɻʲɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿɴȝ̷ɴ̹ʲɭȝɻɇȳɞɻɭɣɭʲ ȩɣɝʿȝɴɴȳɻɴʿȯɣȩɴʿ̸̶̶̻̿̿ʲɭȯȾ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̾ Ǟȝʑ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
32. ȀǵƲƠ ˅ ȌǊƬ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻʲ Ƭɣɝɝɣɞ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȩɄȝɗɗȳɞȿȳɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋɇȩȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȾɞɴʲɿɴȯȝʲȿɣʊʿȩɣɝɝɣɞ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȩɄȝɗɗȳɞȿȳɴ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
33. ȀǵƲƠ ˅ ȌǊƬ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻʲ Ƭɗɿɴɻȳɰ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ȿɰɣʋɻɄ ɴɭɿɰɻɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋɇȩȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȾɞɴʲɿɴȯȝʲȿɣʊʿȩɗɿɴɻȳɰ˅Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅ȿɰɣʋɻɄ˅ɴɭɿɰɻɴ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
4. ̹̺ʲ  ȀǵƲƠ ˅ ȌǊƬ ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ ǵɿɭɭɣɰɻʲ ƶɞȿɣɰȿȳɝȳɞɻʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿ ʋɇȩȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲȾɞɴʲɿɴȯȝʲȿɣʊʿȳɞȿɣɰȿȳɝȳɞɻ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
5. ̹̻ʲ ȀǟǊƬƶǁʲ  ̷̺ ɝʑɻɄɴ ȝȨɣɿɻ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɿɞɇȩȳȾʲɣɰȿʿ ɭȝɰȳɞɻɇɞȿʿȾɣɣȯ˅ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿ̷̺˅ɝʑɻɄɴ˅ȝȨɣɿɻ˅ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̸̹  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
36. Ǟȝʑɣȩɗɇɞɇȩʲ Ơɰȳ ɴȝȿȿɇɞȿ Ȩɰȳȝɴɻɴ ɇɞȳʊɇɻȝȨɗȳ ȝȾɻȳɰ Ȩɰȳȝɴɻ˅Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʹ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿ ʋʋʋʲɝȝʑɣȩɗɇɞɇȩʲɣɰȿʿɄȳȝɗɻɄʑ˅ɗɇȾȳɴɻʑɗȳʿʋɣɝȳɞɴ˅ɄȳȝɗɻɄʿȳʐɭȳɰɻ˅ȝɞɴʋȳɰɴʿɴȝȿȿɇɞȿ˅Ȩɰȳȝɴɻɴʿ Ⱦȝɯ˅̸̶̶̸̸̻̹̾ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̸̾ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
7. ̹̽ʲ ǟǇǵ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ ǵȩɣɻɗȝɞȯʲ ǁɣɰɝɿɗȝ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʴ Ʉɣʋ ɻɣ Ⱦȳȳȯ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɴȝȾȳɗʑʵ ̸̶̸̶ʵ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɄȳȝɗɻɄɴȩɣɻɗȝɞȯʲȩɣɝʿɿɭɗɣȝȯɴʿȯɣȩɿɝȳɞɻɴʿ̸̻̻̹˅ǁɣɰɝɿɗȝ̸̶̉ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ̸̶̉Ȩɣɣɕɗȳɻ˅ǔȝɞ̸̶̸̶˅ƶɞȿɗɇɴɄʲɭȯȾʲ
8. ̹̾ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ  ǂɿɇȯȳ  ɻɣ  Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ  Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿʴ  Ʉɣʋ  ɻɣ  ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳ  ɇɞȾȝɞɻ  Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ  ȝɞȯ ɴɻȳɰɇɗɇɴȳ  Ȩɣɻɻɗȳɴʵ  ǮɿȨɗɇȩ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ƶɞȿɗȝɞȯʴ  Ȁǖʳ  ̸̶̸̷ʵ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɿɞɇȩȳȾʲ ɣɰȿʲɿɕʿȨȝȨʑȾɰɇȳɞȯɗʑʿʋɭ˅ȩɣɞɻȳɞɻʿɿɭɗɣȝȯɴʿɴɇɻȳɴʿ̸ʿ̸̶̶̾ʿ̶̸ʿɴɻȝɰɻ̺ɗɇȾȳˈȿɿɇȯȳˈɻɣˈȨɣɻɻɗȳˈ˅ ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʲɭȯȾʲ
9. ̹̿ʲ Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʲ  Ǉɣʋ  ɻɣ  ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳ  Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ  Ⱦɣɰ  Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ˅Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ȝɻ  Ʉɣɝȳʵ Ʋȳɭȝɰɻɝȳɞɻ ɣȾ ǁɣɣȯ ǵȝȾȳɻʑʳ Șɣɣɞɣɴȳɴ ȝɞȯ ǁɣɣȯȨɣɰɞȳ Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳɴ ˉȌǇǤˊʳ ȝɞȯ ǁƠǤʴ ̸̶̶̽ʵ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿȾɣɣȯɴȝȾȳɻʑʿɭɿȨɗɇȩȝɻɇɣɞɴʿɝɇȩɰɣʿǮǊǁˈƫɣɻɻɗȳˈȳɞʲɭȯȾʲ
10. ̶̺ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ ǇȳȝɗɻɄ ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ ǁɣɰɝɿɗȝ ɝɇɗɕʴ ȩɣɝɝɣɞ ɯɿȳɴɻɇɣɞɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲ ɞɄɴʲɿɕʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʿȨȝȨʑʿȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȨɣɻɻɗȳ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȾɣɰɝɿɗȝ˅ɝɇɗɕ˅ ɯɿȳɴɻɇɣɞɴʿ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̷̽ Ǟȝʑ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ

- ̷̺ʲ Ƭȳɞɻȳɰɴ Ⱦɣɰ Ʋɇɴȳȝɴȳ Ƭɣɞɻɰɣɗ ȝɞȯ Ǯɰȳʊȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ ǊɞȾȝɞɻ ȝɞȯ ɻɣȯȯɗȳɰ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʴ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ Ⱦɰɣɝ ȝ Ȩɣɻɻɗȳʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȩȯȩʲȿɣʊʿɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿɇɞȾȝɞɻȝɞȯɻɣȯȯɗȳɰɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞʿȨɣɻɻɗȳ˅ ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿɇɞȯȳʐʲɄɻɝɗʾʴ˽ʴɻȳʐɻ˵Ʋɣ̸̶̉ɞɣɻ̸̶̉ɭɰɣɭ̸̶̉ɣɰ̸̶̉ɗȳȝʊȳʳɻɄȝɞ̸̶̉Ʉȳ̸̶̉ɣɰ̸̶̉ ɴɄȳ̸̶̉ɞȳȳȯɴʲ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽ ǞȝɰȩɄ ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
- ̸̺ʲ ǟȝɻɇɣɞȝɗ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǵȳɰʊɇȩȳʲ  ǁɣɣȯ  ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ  ɇɞ  ȨȝȨɇȳɴ  ȝɞȯ  ʑɣɿɞȿ  ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲɞɄɴʲɿɕʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴʿȨȝȨʑʿʋȳȝɞɇɞȿ˅ȝɞȯ˅ȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʿȾɣɣȯ˅ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ˅ɇɞ˅ȨȝȨɇȳɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ ʑɣɿɞȿ˅ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞʿ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
- ̺̹ʲ ǔɣɄɞɴ Ǉɣɭɕɇɞɴ  Ǟȳȯɇȩɇɞȳʲ  ǁɣɣȯ  ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ ɇɞ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞʲ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  Ʉɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲ ɄɣɭɕɇɞɴɝȳȯɇȩɇɞȳʲɣɰȿʿɄȳȝɗɻɄʿȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ȯɇɴȳȝɴȳɴʿȾɣɣȯ˅ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ˅ɇɞ˅ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ ɣɞ ̽  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
- ̺̺ʲ Ơȩȝȯȳɝʑ ɣȾ ǟɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ ȝɞȯ Ʋɇȳɻȳɻɇȩɴʲ Ǳȳȯɿȩɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ɰɇɴɕ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴʲ ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿʋʋʋʲȳȝɻɰɇȿɄɻʲɣɰȿʿɄȳȝɗɻɄʿȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ˅ȝɞȯ˅ɇɞɻɣɗȳɰȝɞȩȳɴʿȾɣɣȯ˅ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴʿɰȳȯɿȩɇɞȿ˅ɻɄȳ˅ ɰɇɴɕ˅ɣȾ˅Ⱦɣɣȯ˅ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ  ˉȝȩȩȳɴɴȳȯ  ɣɞ  ̽  ǞȝɰȩɄ  ̸̶̸̸ˊʲ
- ̺̻ʲ Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  ǤɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞʿȀǟǊƬƶǁʲ  Ǌɝɭɗȳɝȳɞɻȝɻɇɣɞ  ȿɿɇȯȝɞȩȳʴ  ɭɰɣɻȳȩɻɇɞȿʳ  ɭɰɣɝɣɻɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ  ɴɿɭɭɣɰɻɇɞȿ  ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ  ɇɞ  Ⱦȝȩɇɗɇɻɇȳɴ  ɭɰɣʊɇȯɇɞȿ  ɝȝɻȳɰɞɇɻʑ  ȝɞȯ  ɞȳʋȨɣɰɞ  ɴȳɰʊɇȩȳɴʴ ɻɄȳ  ɰȳʊɇɴȳȯ  ȨȝȨʑ˅Ⱦɰɇȳɞȯɗʑ  Ʉɣɴɭɇɻȝɗ  ɇɞɇɻɇȝɻɇʊȳʵ  Ȍɣɰɗȯ  ǇȳȝɗɻɄ  Ǥɰȿȝɞɇʗȝɻɇɣɞ  ȝɞȯ  ȀǟǊƬƶǁʴ ǂȳɞȳʊȝʳ  ǵʋɇɻʗȳɰɗȝɞȯʳ  ̸̶̷̾ʵ  ƠʊȝɇɗȝȨɗȳ  ɣɞɗɇɞȳʴ  ɄɻɻɭɴʴʿʿȝɭɭɴʲʋɄɣʲɇɞɻʿɇɰɇɴʿȨɇɻɴɻɰȳȝɝʿɄȝɞȯ ɗȳʿ̷̶̼̼̻ʿ̸̸̺̹̽̿ʿ̸̷̷̶̺̻̹̿̽̾̿̾̽˅ȳɞȿʲɭȯȾʹɴȳɯɿȳɞȩȳ˵̷̿˞ɇɴƠɗɗɣʋȳȯ˵ʑʲ

![Picture 240](images/SRC013/picture-240.png)

![Picture 241](images/SRC013/picture-241.png)

At around six months of age, your baby will need to consume healthy and nutritious foods, in addition to breastmilk, to meet his/her energy and nutrient needs. Therefore, at six months, solid foods, such as vegetables, fruits, infant cereals, and mashed meat, should be introduced to complement your child's diet while maintaining breastfeeding for up to two years and beyond [1] .

ǼɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻʋɣ ʑȳȝɰɴ ɣȾ ȝɞʑ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ɗɇȾȳ ȝɰȳ ȩɣɞɴɇȯȳɰȳȯ ɭȝɰɻ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ 1000 days of life, and is a critical period for your child's growth and development for his/her future health. It is also the period when malnutrition may start to develop in many children [2] , which can have ɇɝɝȳȯɇȝɻȳ ȝɞȯ ɗɣɞȿ˅ɻȳɰɝ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ȳʜȳȩɻɴʲ Ǟȝɗɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ ȳȝɰɗʑ ɇɞ ɗɇȾȳ can lead to delayed physical and mental development, decreased intellectual performance, and poor health later on during adolescence and adulthood. Once a child reaches two ʑȳȝɰɴ ɣȾ ȝȿȳʳ ɇɻ Ȩȳȩɣɝȳɴ ȳʐɻɰȳɝȳɗʑ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻ ɻɣ ɰȳʊȳɰɴȳ ɻɄȳ ȳʜȳȩɻɴ ɣȾ ɝȝɗɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞ [3] .

'The transition from exclusive breastfeeding to family foods, referred to as complementary feeding, typically covers the period from 6 to 18 - 24 months of age.'

-World Health Organization (WHO) [4]

![Picture 242](images/SRC013/picture-242.png)

## Assessment of the  Child's Growth

It is important that the doctor routinely assesses the growth of your child. Growth is, in fact, an important indicator of the child's overall health, development, and nutritional status. the doctor ʋɇɗɗ  ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩȝɗɗʑ  ɝȳȝɴɿɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ʋȳɇȿɄɻʳ ɗȳɞȿɻɄʳ ȝɞȯ Ʉȳȝȯ ȩɇɰȩɿɝȾȳɰȳɞȩȳʲ ǼɄȳ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ʋɇɗɗ ɗȝɻȳɰ ȯɰȝʋ ɻɄȳɴȳ ɝȳȝɴɿɰȳɝȳɞɻɴ ɣɞ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ȿɰɣʋɻɄ ȩɄȝɰɻɴ ɻɄȝɻ ɻȝɕȳ ɇɞɻɣ ȩɣɞɴɇȯȳɰȝɻɇɣɞ ɻɄȳ ȳʐȝȩɻ age of your child [5-7] .

In some instances, these measurements may reveal certain growth-related problems, such as:

- The child has a low weight for his/her age (underweight or severely underweight): This may result from the child being too thin or too short for his/her age. It may also be the result of poor nutrition or certain illnesses. Underweight children are more vulnerable to diseases and may experience delays in their development.
- The child is short for his/her age (stunted or severely stunted): If your child's height is below the normal range for his/her age (a condition referred to as stunting), this may be the result of long-term malnutrition or illness. It has consequences on the child's physical development and is often accompanied by poor mental development.
- The  child  has  lost  weight  (wasted  or  severely  wasted):  This  may  occur  because  of  poor nutrition or illness. Wasted children have a higher risk of contracting diseases and illnesses.
- The child is overweight or obese: Infants and young children can become overweight or obese Ⱦɣɰ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ɰȳȝɴɣɞɴʲ ǼɄȳ ɝɣɴɻ Ⱦɰȳɯɿȳɞɻ ȩȝɿɴȳ ɇɴ ɣʊȳɰȾȳȳȯɇɞȿʳ ɿɞɄȳȝɗɻɄʑ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɭɰȝȩɻɇȩȳɴʳ genetic factors (i.e., running in the family), or a combination of all these factors. In rare cases, obesity  in  children  may  result  from  a  medical  condition  diagnosed  by  the  doctor.  Being overweight and obese early in life can increase the risk of obesity and chronic diseases later in life.
- The child has a larger-than-normal or smaller-than-normal head circumference: This helps in assessing brain size as an indicator of possible developmental or nutritional problems.

![Picture 243](images/SRC013/picture-243.png)

![Picture 244](images/SRC013/picture-244.png)

For optimal growth and development, the World Health Organization (WHO) and United Nations International Children's Emergency Fund (UNICEF) recommend continued breastfeeding for up to two years and beyond while introducing adequate complementary foods (solid and soft foods) at six months of age.

ǼɄȳ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɣȾ ȩɣɞɻɇɞɿȳȯ ȨɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯɇɞȿ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ȝɰȳ ȝɴ Ⱦɣɗɗɣʋɴʴ [8- 10]

- Breastmilk provides your baby with important nutrients (but make sure to introduce solid foods in addition to breastmilk at six months of age).
- Breastmilk  strengthens  your  child's  immunity;  as  long  as  you  breastfeed  your  baby,  the antibodies and cells in your breastmilk will continue to enhance your baby's immune system.

In addition, breastfeeding reduces your risk of certain illnesses, such as the risk of developing ovarian cancer, breast cancer, high blood pressure, heart disease, type 2 diabetes and rheumatoid arthritis.

![Picture 245](images/SRC013/picture-245.png)

## Dietary Recommendations

Adequate child growth depends on several factors, including appropriate energy and nutrient intake. Starting complementary feeding is a must at six months since milk alone will not meet all ɻɄȳ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ɞȳȳȯɴ ȝɻ ɻɄɇɴ ȝȿȳʲ ǼɄȳɰȳȾɣɰȳʳ ɝȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɣʜȳɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯʳ ȿɰȝȯɿȝɗɗʑʳ ȝ ʊȝɰɇȳɻʑ of nutrient-dense foods from the following general food groups:

- Breastmilk (or infant formula milk in certain conditions)

### · Vegetables:

- Vitamin A rich vegetables such as pumpkin, carrots, sweet red peppers, squash, and dark green leafy vegetables.
- Other vegetables such as broccoli, zucchini and cucumbers. Try to choose vegetables ɣȾ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ȩɣɗɣɰɴʳ ʠȝʊɣɰɴ ȝɞȯ ɻȳʐɻɿɰȳɴ ɻɣ ȳɞɴɿɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ɰȳȩȳɇʊȳɴ ȝɗɗ ɻɄȳ ȳɴɴȳɞɻɇȝɗ vitamins and minerals.

### · Fruits:

- Vitamin A rich fruits such as ripe mangoes and ripe papayas.
- ǤɻɄȳɰ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ Ȩȝɞȝɞȝɴʳ ɭȳȝɰɴ ȝɞȯ ȝɭɭɗȳɴʲ Ǽ ɰʑ ɻɣ ȩɄɣɣɴȳ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴ ɣȾ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ȩɣɗɣɰɴʳ ʠȝʊɣɰɴ ȝɞȯ ɻȳʐɻɿɰȳɴ ɻɣ ȳɞɴɿɰȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ɰȳȩȳɇʊȳɴ ȝɗɗ ɻɄȳ ȳɴɴȳɞɻɇȝɗ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞɴ ȝɞȯ ɝɇɞȳɰȝɗɴʲ
- Ƭȳɰȳȝɗɴ ȝɞȯ ɴɻȝɰȩɄʑ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳɴʴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴʳ ɰɇȩȳʳ ɭȝɴɻȝʳ ɴʋȳȳɻ ɭɣɻȝɻɣʳ and potatoes.
- Legumes: such as beans and lentils.
- Dairy products: such as yogurt, labneh and cheese.
- ǁɇɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ɝȳȝɻ ȝɞȯ ȝɗɻȳɰɞȝɻɇʊȳɴʴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʟɴɄʳ ȩɄɇȩɕȳɞʳ ɝȳȝɻ ˉȳʲȿʲʳ ȨȳȳȾ ȝɞȯ ȿɣȝɻˊʳ ȝɞȯ eggs.

Section 6 provides information on the texture (consistency) ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȿɇʊȳɞ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ȝɻ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ȝȿȳɴʲ

Section 12 provides details on what foods to avoid to prevent choking and tips on how to prepare these foods.

![Picture 246](images/SRC013/picture-246.png)

![Picture 247](images/SRC013/picture-247.png)

ƫȳɴɇȯȳɴ ȝȿȳʳ ɻɄȳɰȳ ȝɰȳ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɴɇȿɞɴ ɻɣ ɗɣɣɕ Ⱦɣɰ ȩɣɞȩȳɰɞɇɞȿ ʋɄȳɻɄȳɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɇɴ ɰȳȝȯʑ ɻɣ ɴɻȝɰɻ complementary feeding [11] :

- Your baby can stay in a sitting position with their head held steady with no support
- Your baby has full coordination between their eyes, hands, and mouth by locating the food and attempting to pick it up to place in their mouth.
- Your baby can properly swallow their food and not spit it out
- Your baby seems hungry earlier than usual
- Your baby shows interest in food when others are eating
- Your baby can let you know if they do not want to eat by turning their head away from the food or leaning back
- Your baby's weight has doubled compared to their birth weight.

![Picture 248](images/SRC013/picture-248.png)

![Picture 249](images/SRC013/picture-249.png)

## How to Start the Complementary Feeding (Weaning) Process?

As previously mentioned, complementary feeding should begin at six months of age; however, the weaning process could take days, weeks, or months depending on your baby's growth and  development [12] .  Y ou  can  begin  by  slowly  decreasing  how  often  or  how  long  you  are breastfeeding and/or formula feeding each day.  Begin with substituting one breastfeed with complementary feed, and once your baby is accustomed to this, you can substitute another feed, and so on. Remember that the weaning process should be gradual, and the pace is up to you and your baby [12] .

![Picture 250](images/SRC013/picture-250.png)

![Picture 251](images/SRC013/picture-251.png)

It  is  recommended  to  gradually  thicken  food  consistency  as  the  baby  ages,  while  paying attention  to  your  baby's  abilities.  Infants  can  usually  eat  puréed,  mashed  and  soft/semi-solid Ⱦɣɣȯɴ Ȩȳȿɇɞɞɇɞȿ ȝɻ ɴɇʐ ɝɣɞɻɄɴ ɣȾ ȝȿȳʲ ƫʑ ȳɇȿɄɻ ɝɣɞɻɄɴʳ ɝɣɴɻ ȨȝȨɇȳɴ ȩȝɞ ȝɗɴɣ ȳȝɻ ˑʟɞȿȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ˒ (i.e.,  foods  and snacks that the baby can grasp and eat alone).

By the age of 12 months, most children can consume the same types of foods as the rest of the family (while making sure that these are nutritious foods) [4, 13] . Refer to section 12 to learn more about the risk of choking and how to avoid it, and to section 14 for examples of nutritious foods and tips on preparing foods for your baby.

![Picture 252](images/SRC013/picture-252.png)

![Picture 253](images/SRC013/picture-253.png)

### ȌɄȝɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ Ȩȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩȳȯ ɻɣ ɝʑ ȨȝȨʑʹ

ǼɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩȳȯ ɻɣ ȨȝȨɇȳɴ ʊȝɰʑ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɣɞȳ ȩɿɗɻɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɻɄȳ ɣɻɄȳɰ ȝɞȯ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɣɞȳ Ⱦȝɝɇɗʑ ɻɣ ɻɄȳ ɣɻɄȳɰʲ ǇȳȝɗɻɄʑ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɄȳ ȳɞɻɇɰȳ Ⱦȝɝɇɗʑ ȳȝɻɴ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ȝɗʋȝʑɴ Ȩȳ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ȩɄɣɇȩȳʳ Ȩɿɻ ɇɻ ɇɴ ȩɰɿȩɇȝɗ to keep them plain (i.e., no added salt, sugar, or strong spices).

Ǳȳȿȝɰȯɇɞȿ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȿɰɣɿɭɴʳ ɻɄȳɰȳ ɇɴ ɞɣ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɣɰȯȳɰ ɻɣ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩȳ ɣɞȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȿɰɣɿɭ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ȝɞɣɻɄȳɰʲ However, many experts agree that you should start with foods that contain iron, since it  is needed for many areas of the baby's development [11] ʲ Ǟȳȝɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʟɴɄʳ ȩɄɇȩɕȳɞʳ ɻɿɰɕȳʑʳ ȝɞȯ ȨȳȳȾ ȝɰȳ ȳʐȩȳɗɗȳɞɻ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ ɣȾ ɇɰɣɞ ȝɞȯ ɄɇȿɄ˅ɯɿȝɗɇɻʑ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ˉʟɴɄ ɝȝʑ ȩȝɿɴȳ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȩ ɰȳȝȩɻɇɣɞɴ ɇɞ ɴɣɝȳ ȨȝȨɇȳɴʲ ǱȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ ɴȳȩɻɇɣɞ ̷̽ Ⱦɣɰ ɝɣɰȳ ɇɞȾɣɰɝȝɻɇɣɞˊʲ Ǌɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ (such as rice and oatmeal), vegetables, and fruits are also good sources of iron and other vital minerals and vitamins.

It is very important that you introduce one single-ingredient food to your baby at a time. For example, introduce peaches alone rather than peach-yogurt, which has more than one ingredient. Introducing a single new food at a time, at 3-5 days intervals, will allow you to  identify any adverse reaction, allergic response or intolerances that your baby may have to certain foods [11] .

### 6-8 months

At around six months of age, you can introduce strained or puréed foods to your baby's diet (see ƫɣʐ ̷ Ⱦɣɰ ȳʐȝɝɭɗȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɗɴˊʲ Ǽɣ ɭɰɣɝɣɻȳ ɄȳȝɗɻɄʑ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɝȳɞɻʳ ɿɴȳ ȝ ɴɭɣɣɞ ɻɣ ɣʜȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʵ ȯɣ ɞɣɻ ȩɣɝȨɇɞȳ ɻɄȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ʋɇɻɄ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ ɇɞ ȝ Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ ȝɞȯ ȯɣ ɞɣɻ ȿɇʊȳ ɇɻ ɻɣ your baby directly from a squeezable pouch.

Some dietitians recommend introducing vegetables before fruits. This is because the sweetness of fruits will make vegetables less ȝɭɭȳȝɗɇɞȿ ɇȾ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴ ȝɰȳ ɣʜȳɰȳȯ ʟɰɴɻʲ

'Your baby needs more energy and nutrients now than at any other time in their life.' -UNICEF [14]

### ƫɣʐ ̷ʲ ƶʐȝɝɭɗȳ ɣȾ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɗɴ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ

### ƶʐȝɝɭɗȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɣ Ȩȳ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩȳȯ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ [11] :

- Well-cooked  mashed  vegetables,  puréed  meat,  well-cooked  mashed  legumes  (e.g., beans, lentils, peas (peeled), rice, mashed potatoes, and whole-fat dairy products (such as  yogurt)
- Soft,  diced,  or  mashed  fruits  such  as  bananas  ,  apples  (puréed  after  boiling),  ripe mangos,  avocados,  and  melons
- Ǌɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ȨȝȨʑ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ
- All foods should be natural without the addition of salt, sugar, or spices

Introduce a single new food at a time, at 3-5 day-intervals. This approach will allow you to identify any adverse reaction, allergic response or intolerances that your baby may have to ȩȳɰɻȝɇɞ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʲ ƠȾɻȳɰ ɻɄȝɻʳ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɴɻȝɰɻ ɝɇʐɇɞȿ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ɇɞȿɰȳȯɇȳɞɻɴ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ˔ɴ ɝȳȝɗɴʲ

### Examples   of nutritious, suitable, and easy to prepare meals for your baby (6-8 months old):

- Puréed: potatoes + carrots + peas, mashed with fork (without salt)
- Puréed: potatoes + carrots + peas, mashed with fork + boiled chicken
- Puréed: potatoes + carrots + peas, mashed with fork + part of boiled egg
- Pumped breastmilk or formula milk + mashed boiled rice (without salt)
- Mashed lentil soup: rice + mashed lentils + potatoes + carrots
- Mashed: boiled rice + spinach, mulukhiya (jute leaves), beans, or basil (without salt)
- Puréed: Apples (boiled, yellow, or green, or red), ripe
- Mashed bananas and avocado

![Picture 254](images/SRC013/picture-254.png)

ƶʐȝɝɭɗȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȝɰȳ ȿɣɣȯ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ ɣȾ ɇɰɣɞ ȝɰȳ ɭɿɰȴȳȯ ɝȳȝɻɴʳ ʊȳȿȳɻȝȨɗȳɴ ȝɞȯ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴʲ Ǌɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ  ȨȝȨʑ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ ȝɰȳ ɣɻɄȳɰ ȿɣɣȯ ɴɣɿɰȩȳɴ ɣȾ ɇɰɣɞ ɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ȯɇȳɻʲ Ǟȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ʑɣɿ add enough breast milk or formula to the infant cereal (do not use cow's milk) for a relatively thin consistency so that it is easy for your baby to swallow. Just 2 feedings a day, a couple of spoonfuls, is all your baby needs [11] .

When introducing store-bought infant cereals, check the food label to ensure that the cereal is a single-ingredient product and does not contain other added ingredients such as cow's milk, ʑɣȿɿɰɻʳ ȝȯȯȳȯ Ⱦɰɿɇɻʳ ʠȝʊɣɰɇɞȿɴʳ ȝɞȯʿɣɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝʲ ǼɄɇɴ ʋɇɗɗ ɰȳȯɿȩȳ ɻɄȳ ɗɇɕȳɗɇɄɣɣȯ ɣȾ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȩ reactions  to  the  cereals  (See  section  17  on  food  allergies  and  section  14  on  tips  related  to preparing foods for your baby).

### How much food should I give my baby?

- Complementary  feeding  should  be  introduced  at  six  months,  however  most  of  your baby's daily calories will still come from breastmilk (or formula) at this age. Once you start introducing complementary feeding, your baby may only be eating one meal per day along with  breastmilk  (or  formula).  This  is  completely  normal;  start  slowly  and  progressively increase the number of meals daily.
- Eventually, you can give 3 meals per day to your 6-8 months old baby, with an amount close to 2-3 tablespoons of food per meal [16] , while maintaining breastfeeding (or formula Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿˊʲ Ȓɣɿ ɝȝʑ ȝɗɴɣ ɣʜȳɰ ɄɇɝʿɄȳɰ ̷ˆ̸ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɿɴ ɴɞȝȩɕɴ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ Ⱦɰɿɇɻɴˊʳ ȯȳɭȳɞȯɇɞȿ ɣɞ his/her  appetite.
- Observe your child for signs of hunger or satiety (see section 8) [16] .
- If  you  are  formula  feeding,  do  not  exceed  more  than  950  mL  (32  oz.)  in  24  hours [11] . Overfeeding  can  cause  vomiting,  diarrhea,  or  excessive  weight  gain.

An example of choices to include in a one-day menu is provided in Box 2 [17] .

## Box 2. Example of choices to include in a one-day menu (while continuing breastmilk or formula feeding)

| Mealtimes   | Sample Meals                                                                  |
|-------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Breakfast   | Ǌɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ȨɰȳȝɕȾȝɴɻ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴ Strawberries or blueberries, mashed           |
| Lunch       | Boiled chicken Boiled chickpeas, mashed                                       |
| Snack       | Ripe pear, peeled and mashed                                                  |
| Dinner      | Ground beef or well-cooked mashed lentils Boiled rice Boiled broccoli, mashed |

### 9-12 months:

- Ơɻ ɻɄɇɴ ȝȿȳʳ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȩȝɞ ɴɻȝɰɻ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɄɇɝɴȳɗȾʿɄȳɰɴȳɗȾʳ ɴɣ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɴɻȝɰɻ ɣʜȳɰɇɞȿ ʟɞȿȳɰ foods in small amounts. Your baby will show signs that they are ready to eat on their own by trying to grab the food or the spoon with their hands.
- Ơɻ ɻɄɇɴ ȝȿȳʳ ʑɣɿ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɣʜȳɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ̹˅̺ ɝȳȝɗɴʿȯȝʑ ȝɞȯ ̷ ɻɣ ̸ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɿɴ ɴɞȝȩɕɴʿȯȝʑ ˉɴɿȩɄ as fruits) [16] . Per meal, your baby can consume an amount of food equivalent to ½ cup (i.e., approximately 125 mL) [16] .
- ǼɄȳ ȳȝɴɇȳɴɻ ʋȝʑ ɻɣ ɴɻȝɰɻ ʟɞȿȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɇɴ ȝɗɴɣ ɻɄȳ ɝȳɴɴɇȳɴɻʷ Ǯɿɻ ȝ ɗɇɻɻɗȳ ɣȾ ʋɄȝɻȳʊȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯ ʑɣɿ Ʉȝʊȳ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳȯ ɣɞɻɣ ɻɄȳ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɻɰȝʑ ɣɰ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɄɇȿɄȩɄȝɇɰ ȝɞȯ ɗȳɻ ɻɄȳɝ ȯɇȿ ɇɞʷ Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ȝɗȝɰɝȳȯ ɇȾ ȝɗɝɣɴɻ ȳʊȳɰʑɻɄɇɞȿ ɇɴ ɴɭɇɗɗȳȯ ɣɞ ɻɄȳ ʠɣɣɰ ɣɰ ɻɄȳɝɴȳɗʊȳɴʳ ȝɞȯ ɇȾ ʊȳɰʑ ɗɇɻɻɗȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ Ʉȝɴ made it to their mouth. Your baby is learning, and he/she will soon be able to get the skills ɻɣ ɴȳɗȾ˅Ⱦȳȳȯʲ ƫɣʐ ̹ ɴɄɣʋɴ ɻɄȳ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɣȾ ɗȳɻɻɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɴȳɗȾ˅Ⱦȳȳȯ [18] .

![Picture 255](images/SRC013/picture-255.png)

### ƫɣʐ ̹ʲ ƫȳɞȳʟɻɴ ȝɴɴɣȩɇȝɻȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ɗȳɻɻɇɞȿ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɴȳɗȾ˅Ⱦȳȳȯ

- Allowing your child to feed themselves is the best technique to allow them to experience their senses such as taste, texture and smell.
- Nurturing independence (giving them a little control  over  when  they  take  a  bite,  how much they put in their mouth, and when they are done eating).
- Enhancing grasping and coordination skills.
- Allowing them to be aware of their bodies (knowing where their mouth is, how to bend ɻɄȳɇɰ ʟɞȿȳɰɴ ȝɞȯ ȳɗȨɣʋɴ ʋɄȳɞ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɝɴȳɗʊȳɴˊʲ
- Helping in oral motor development (how wide they need to open their mouth, close their ɗɇɭɴ ɻɣ ȿȳɻ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɣʜ ɻɄȳ ɴɭɣɣɞʳ ȝɞȯ ɗɇȩɕ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɗɇɭɴ ɻɣ ȩɗȳȝɞ ɻɄȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɴɿɰɰɣɿɞȯɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɝɣɿɻɄˊʲ

### 12-24 months:

- Ơɻ ɻɄɇɴ ȝȿȳʳ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɇɴ ɰȳȝȯʑ ɻɣ ȳȝɻ ɻɄȳ ɴȝɝȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȝɴ ɻɄȳ Ⱦȝɝɇɗʑʲ Ǥʜȳɰ ɝȳȝɗɴ ̹˅̺ ɻɇɝȳɴ per day at 12-24 months of age, with additional nutritious snacks (such as a piece of fruit), 1- 2 times per day [16] .
- Per  meal,  your  child  can  consume  an  amount  close  to  ¾    cup,  i.e.  around  190  mL [16] . Appendix 1 provides information on the recommended number of servings from each food group,  and  examples  of  servings.

IMPORTANT NOTE

Children do not need to eat chocolate or sweets to feel ȳɞȳɰȿȳɻɇȩʷ ǼɄȳʑ ȩȝɞ ȿȳɻ ȝɗɗ ɻɄȳ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ they need from a healthy and varied diet that includes food and beverages from the six food groups (refer to Appendix 1).

![Picture 256](images/SRC013/picture-256.png)

Feed your child at his or her own comfort and observe signs of hunger and satiety (feeling of fullness). Below are hunger and satiety cues that your child may display (Box 4) [19] .

|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Hunger cues                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Satiety cues                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| • Moves head towards spoon/food, bottle, or nipple • Smiles during feeding to indicate they want more • Points out or reaches for food • Gets excited when he/she sees food • Expresses with words or sounds the ȯȳɴɇɰȳ Ⱦɣɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ | • Turns head away from spoon/food, bottle, or nipple • Spits food out of their mouth • Shakes head to say no more • Clenches mouth, closes and refuses to open • Plays with the food, spoon, or plate |

![Picture 257](images/SRC013/picture-257.png)

![Picture 258](images/SRC013/picture-258.png)

Children need adequate intakes of nutrients and vitamins to help boost their immune system and protect them against infectious germs. However, there are no magical foods or supplements that will boost your child's immune system [20] . The best advice for supporting your child's immunity is ɞɣɻ ɻɣ Ⱦɣȩɿɴ ɣɞ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻɴʳ Ȩɿɻ ɰȝɻɄȳɰ ɻɣ ɗɣɣɕ ȝɻ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɣʊȳɰȝɗɗ ȯɇȳɻȝɰʑ ɇɞɻȝɕȳ ȝɞȯ ɴɻɰɇʊȳ Ⱦɣɰ a varied and balanced diet consisting of food and beverages from the six food groups.  Prioritize nutrient-rich foods such as vegetables and fruits that supply an abundant amount of antioxidants, vitamins, and minerals. Make sure to limit their consumption of processed foods, snacks, and foods high in sugar, salt, and unhealthy fats. Consult Appendix 1 for details pertinent to dietary recommendations for your child.

![Picture 259](images/SRC013/picture-259.png)

![Picture 260](images/SRC013/picture-260.png)

Some children go through a phase of refusing certain types of food, especially  when trying ɻɄȳɴȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻɇɝȳʲ ǼɄȳɴȳ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ ȝɰȳ ɕɞɣʋɞ ȝɴ ˑɭɇȩɕʑ ȳȝɻȳɰɴ˒ʲ Ǯɇȩɕʑ ȳȝɻɇɞȿ ɻʑɭɇȩȝɗɗʑ occurs among young children and is often perceived as a stressful and frustrating experience for parents. Picky eating rarely causes serious nutritional, medical or growth problems for the child, and it is a phase that most children grow out of [21] ʲ  ǵɣɝȳ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ Ʉȝʊȳ ɝɣɰȳ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻ ȳȝɻɇɞȿ habits, and they can be considered as 'extreme picky eaters.' Professionals may consider this as a feeding disorder, and you will need the help of a health professional to help your child grow out of ɇɻʲ ǼɄȳ ɴȳȩɻɇɣɞ Ȩȳɗɣʋ ȳʐɭɗȝɇɞɴ ɻɄȳ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞȩȳ Ȩȳɻʋȳȳɞ ɭɇȩɕʑ ȳȝɻȳɰɴ ȝɞȯ ȳʐɻɰȳɝȳ ɭɇȩɕʑ ȳȝɻȳɰɴ [21] .

## Picky eaters &amp; extreme picky eaters

Extreme picky eating can last for a longer time as compared to picky eating. Extreme picky eaters can grow out of it over months or years; however, this usually needs to be done with the help of a health professional [21] . Extreme picky eating is usually more common in children with social communication disorders [21] .

Although being a picky eater is usually harmless, being an extreme picky eater can cause serious ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȿɰɣʋɻɄ ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝɴʳ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴʳ ȯȳɄʑȯɰȝɻɇɣɞ ȝɞȯ ɣɻɄȳɰ ȩɣɞȯɇɻɇɣɞɴ [21] . Table 1 provides you with a direct comparison between the two behaviors.

![Picture 261](images/SRC013/picture-261.png)

![Picture 262](images/SRC013/picture-262.png)

| ɿɞȯȳɰ ʟʊȳ ʑȳȝɰɴ                       | Picky eating                                                                                                                                                                                           | Extreme picky eating                                                                                                                                           |
|---------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| How common is it?                     | • Very common in children. • Ơʜȳȩɻɴ ̷ʿ̹ ɣȾ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ ȝȿȳȯ ̷˅̻ ʑȳȝɰɴʲ                                                                                                                                        | • Less common. • More common in children with social communication disorders.                                                                                  |
| Health/Growth consequences            | • No health/growth consequences or only minor ones.                                                                                                                                                    | • Moderate to severe health/growth consequences. • However, in some cases, there is no health/growth consequences or only minor ones.                          |
| Impact on parents                     | • Can be very stressful for parents.                                                                                                                                                                   | • Usually very stressful for parents.                                                                                                                          |
| Do children grow out of it?           | • Usually, children grow out of it within a period of weeks to months.                                                                                                                                 | • Can take a longer time (months or years) for children to grow out of it. • Management requires the help of a health professional.                            |
| Eating habits                         | • They eat a range of food items, with a preference for some food items from each food group. • Some days, they may only eat very little or have preferences for ȝ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɞȝɰɰɣʋ ɰȝɞȿȳ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɻʑɭȳɴʲ | • They eat a limited range of food ɇɻȳɝɴʳ ɿɴɿȝɗɗʑ ɗȳɴɴ ɻɄȝɞ ̸̶ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ types. • They often exclude some food groups altogether.                                 |
| Feelings towards new food items       | • Picky eaters are upset when new food items are introduced and their Ⱦȝʊɣɰɇɻȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɇɴ ɞɣɻ ɣʜȳɰȳȯʲ                                                                                                     | • Extreme picky eaters are upset when new food items are introduced and when their favorite food is not ɣʜȳɰȳȯ ȝɞȯ ɿɴɿȝɗɗʑ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɰȳȝȩɻɇɣɞ ȩȝɞ be more extreme. |
| Hiding food in other food items       | • You can sometimes hide the refused food item in other foods that the child likes.                                                                                                                    | • ǼɄɇɴ ɇɴ ɝɣɰȳ ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻ ɻɣ Ȩȳ ȯɣɞȳ because the child can detect it.                                                                                             |
| Would they eat ɣʜȳɰȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɇȾ hungry? | • They would eventually eat the ɣʜȳɰȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯʳ ȝɞȯ ʋɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ ɴɻȝɰʊȳ themselves.                                                                                                                          | • ǼɄȳʑ ʋɇɗɗ ɞɣɻ ȳȝɻ ɻɄȳ ɣʜȳɰȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯ usually, and they may be at risk of being ill from starving themselves[21].                                                |

## When to seek professional help?

Do not get frustrated if your child is a picky eater. Just provide your child with healthy food choices and try your best to help your child grow out of this phase. Most picky eaters remain healthy, and their eating habits tend to gradually improve as they age [22] .  If  your child's picky ȳȝɻɇɞȿ ɇɴ ɞɣɻ ȝʜȳȩɻɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɄȳȝɗɻɄ ɣɰ ȿɰɣʋɻɄʳ ɻɄȳɰȳ ɇɴ ɞɣ ɞȳȳȯ ɻɣ Ȩȳ ȩɣɞȩȳɰɞȳȯʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ ʋɄȳɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ȳȝɻɇɞȿ ɄȝȨɇɻɴ ȝɰȳ ȝʜȳȩɻɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɄȳȝɗɻɄʳ  ȿɰɣʋɻɄʳ ɣɰ ȝɰȳ ɴɻɰȳɴɴɇɞȿ ʑɣɿ ȝɴ ȝ ɭȝɰȳɞɻʳ ʑɣɿ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɴȳȳɕ ɭɰɣȾȳɴɴɇɣɞȝɗ Ʉȳɗɭ ɻɣ ʟɞȯ ɻɄȳ ɝɣɴɻ ɴɿɇɻȝȨɗȳ ȝɭɭɰɣȝȩɄ ɻɣ ɣʊȳɰȩɣɝȳ ɻɄɇɴ ɭɰɣȨɗȳɝ [21] .

Box 5 provides some useful steps to follow if your child is a picky eater [21-23] .

![Picture 263](images/SRC013/picture-263.png)

![Picture 264](images/SRC013/picture-264.png)

![Picture 265](images/SRC013/picture-265.png)

![Picture 266](images/SRC013/picture-266.png)

Parents tend to get worried when their child eats very little, refuses to eat a meal or refuses to eat healthy foods like fruits and vegetables [24] ʲ ǼɄɇɴ ʋɣɰɰʑ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ɴɇȿɞɇʟȩȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰ ɴɣɝȳ ɭȝɰȳɞɻɴʳ especially if the child is underweight or not gaining weight adequately. For others, unconsumed meals can be a source of frustration, especially when the parents do not like to waste food that has been prepared, or when they believe that children have to 'clean their plates' [24] . As a result, parents may force their child to eat their entire meal.

The child may indeed eat a bit more when forced to eat. However, studies have shown that the act of forcing the child to eat can cause long-term problems, which are summarized below:

- Disliking or avoiding certain foods. This can result from a negative experience of being Ⱦɣɰȩȳȯ ɻɣ ȳȝɻ ȝ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ Ⱦɣɣȯʲ ƬɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ ȝɰȳ ȝȨɗȳ ɻɣ ɝȝɕȳ ɯɿɇȩɕ ȝɴɴɣȩɇȝɻɇɣɞɴ Ȩȳɻʋȳȳɞ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ and unpleasant experiences that may accompany them [24] .
- Disturbing  the  child's  ability  to  respond  to  their  internal  feelings  of  hunger  and fullness. This means that the child would not listen to their body, so food intake becomes determined  by  factors  other  than  what  the  body  requires.  Instead,  the  child  learns  to continue eating, even when they feel full, stopping only when the plate is empty [24] .
- Development of overeating and overweight. As explained above, forcing the child to eat can disturb the child's ability to learn appropriate appetite control. This can eventually lead to overeating and the development of overweight and obesity [24] .

Except in rare cases, children are usually extremely good at knowing when they are full and ʋɄȳɞ ɻɄȳʑ ȝɰȳ Ʉɿɞȿɰʑʲ ǼɄȳɰȳȾɣɰȳʳ ɇɻ ɇɴ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿ ɻɰɿɴɻ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ȝɞȯ Ȩȳ ȩɣɞʟȯȳɞɻ ɻɄȝɻ they will eat when feeling hungry. It is also important to remember that children naturally tend ɻɣ ɰȳɒȳȩɻ ɞȳʋ Ⱦɣɣȯʳ ʋɄɇȩɄ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ɝȳɻ ʋɇɻɄ ɭɰȳɴɴɿɰȳʲ Ǌɞɴɻȳȝȯʳ ȩɣɞɻɇɞɿȳ ɣʜȳɰɇɞȿ ɞȳʋ Ⱦɣɣȯ and accept that children may refuse to eat it, as this is a normal part of their development. Also remember that the stomachs of young children are smaller than adults' and you may be serving too much food that your child cannot consume.

![Picture 267](images/SRC013/picture-267.png)

## What are the choking hazards for 6-12 months old babies?

Young children are at a risk of food-related choking. Even if they started developing teeth, this ȯɣȳɴ ɞɣɻ ɝȳȝɞ ɻɄȳʑ ȩȝɞ Ʉȝɞȯɗȳ ȝɗɗ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʲ Ǽɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȩɄɣɕɇɞȿʳ ȯɣ ɞɣɻ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɴȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯʴ

- ǵɝȝɗɗʳ ʟɰɝ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʴ ɞɿɻɴʳ ɴȳȳȯɴʳ ɭɣɭȩɣɰɞʳ ɭȳȝɴʳ ȯɰʑ ʠȝɕȳ ȩȳɰȳȝɗʳ ȩɄɇɭɴʳ ɭɰȳɻʗȳɗɴʳ ȩɄɿɞɕɴ ɣȾ ɰȝʋ vegetables, whole cherry tomatoes, raw apple slices, raw pear slices, whole kernels of corn, and whole olives. (Note: carrots and corn, can be cooked and then diced).
- Slippery  foods:  including  whole  small  fruits,  such  as  grapes,  berries  and  cherries,  large pieces of meat, poultry and cheese, hot dogs, and hard candy such as lollipops, jellybeans, and cough drops. (Note: meat, poultry and other protein foods should be well-cooked and then cut lengthwise or chopped up into smaller pieces (less than 0.5 cm in size). Grapes should be cut into quarters.)
- Sticky foods: ȩɄɿɞɕʑ ɭȳȝɞɿɻ Ȩɿɻɻȳɰʳ ȿɿɝʳ ɻȝʜʑʳ ȿɿɝɝʑ ȩȝɞȯɇȳɴʳ ȩȝɰȝɝȳɗɴʳ ɝȝɰɴɄɝȝɗɗɣʋɴʳ jellybeans, dried fruits, and fruit leathers. (Note: smooth nut butters should be spread in a thin layer on a food, such as bread; they should not be given straight from a spoon or a ʟɞȿȳɰʲˊ
- Fruits with seeds or stones: whole fruits with stones inside such as cherries, plum, etc.
- Foods that can form crumbs in your baby's mouth include bread, hard cookies/biscuits.
- Cow's milk: Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ ȿɇʊȳ ȝɞʑ ȩɣʋ˔ɴ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ʑȳȝɰ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳʲ Ȓɣɿɞȿ infants  cannot  digest  cow's  milk.
- Honey: Honey should never be given to babies under the age of one year, as there is a risk of infant botulism (food poisoning).
- Raw or runny eggs: Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ ȿɇʊȳ ɰɿɞɞʑ ȳȿȿɴ ɣɰ ɰȝʋ ȳȿȿɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ year of life. Runny eggs can contain bacteria such as salmonella that cause food poisoning. Ȓɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɴȝȾȳɗʑ ɣʜȳɰ ʋȳɗɗ˅ȩɣɣɕȳȯ ȳȿȿɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȝȾɻȳɰ ɴɇʐ ɝɣɞɻɄɴ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɴȩɰȝɝȨɗȳȯʳ poached, boiled, or fried).
- Camel milk: Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ ȿɇʊȳ ȩȝɝȳɗ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ʑȳȝɰ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳ
- Goat milk: Ʋɣ ɞɣɻ ȿɇʊȳ ȾɰȳɴɄ ȿɣȝɻ ɝɇɗɕ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ʑȳȝɰ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳʲ Ȓɣɿɞȿ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ȩȝɞɞɣɻ ȯɇȿȳɴɻ ȾɰȳɴɄ ȿɣȝɻ ɝɇɗɕʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ ɝɣȯɇʟȳȯ ȿɣȝɻ ɝɇɗɕ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝɴ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ given to your baby if recommended by the doctor.
- Sugary drinks or sweet foods: ƫȝȨɇȳɴ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ɣʜȳɰȳȯ ɴɿȿȝɰʑ ȯɰɇɞɕɴ ɣɰ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʳ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ candies, carbonated soda, or energy drinks.
- Salt: T ry to avoid puréeing adult foods and feeding them to your child as they may contain large amounts of salt. Your baby's kidneys are not yet fully developed to cope with large amounts of salt, and the longer you wait to introduce it into their diet, the better chance you have of not encouraging a liking for it.
- Ǽȳȝ ɣɰ ȩɣʜȳȳʴ Culturally speaking, the older generations have the misconception that if ʑɣɿ ȿɇʊȳ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȩɣʜȳȳ ˉȳɴɭȳȩɇȝɗɗʑ ƠɰȝȨɇȩ ȩɣʜȳȳˊ ɻɄȳʑ ʋɇɗɗ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭ ɻɄȳɇɰ ɴɭȳȳȩɄ ȝɻ ȝɞ ȳȝɰɗʑ ȝȿȳʲ ǼɄɇɴ ɇɴ ɞɣɻ ȩɣɰɰȳȩɻʲ Ƭɣʜȳȳ ȝɞȯ ɻȳȝ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ȿɇʊȳɞ ȝɴ ɻɄȳɴȳ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ ɝȝʑ overstimulate your baby and may also prevent the baby's body from absorbing iron from their  food.

![Picture 268](images/SRC013/picture-268.png)

![Picture 269](images/SRC013/picture-269.png)

![Picture 270](images/SRC013/picture-270.png)

![Picture 271](images/SRC013/picture-271.png)

- Low-fat foods (especially dairy products): Low-calorie cheeses, yogurts or spreads should not be given to babies. Always feed your baby the full-fat varieties as their body needs it.
- Foods that can lead to choking: Foods that may stick to the roof of the mouth and foods ʋɇɻɄ ɴɕɇɞɴ ɣɰ ɰɇɞȯɴ ȩȝɞ ȩȝɿɴȳ ȩɄɣɕɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ɣʜȳɰȳȯ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɞȿ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ˉɰȳȾȳɰ ɻɣ section 12 for more information on the risk of choking).

Beyond six months of age, there is no reason to delay the introduction of common food allergens ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȳȿȿɴʳ ɣɰ ʟɴɄˊʲ Ǥɞȩȳ ʑɣɿ ȯɣʳ ɇɻ ɇɴ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ ɻɣ ȩɣɞɻɇɞɿȳ ɻɣ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɴȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ regularly and monitor if any signs of an allergic reaction occur. If you have concerns, please speak to the doctor.

![Picture 272](images/SRC013/picture-272.png)

![Picture 273](images/SRC013/picture-273.png)

Recommendation 8 of the Qatar Dietary Guidelines (QDG), which is 'Take care of your family,' heavily focuses on the following:

'Build and model healthy patterns for your family'

- Keep regular hours for meals.
- Eat at least one meal together with your family every day.
- Be a role model for your children when it comes to healthy eating and physical activity.

ǼɄȳɰȳ ɇɴ ɞɣ ɴɇɞȿɗȳ ʋȝʑ ɻɣ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɣɰ ʟɞȿȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ Ⱦɣɰ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑʲ ǊȾ ʑɣɿ Ʉȝʊȳ ȝ Ⱦȝʊɣɰɇɻȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɣɰ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ Ⱦɣɣȯ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȝɻɇɣɞ ɻȳȩɄɞɇɯɿȳʳ ɿɴȳ ɇɻ Ȩʑ ȝɗɗ ɝȳȝɞɴʷ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ ɒɿɴɻ ɗɇɕȳ ɻɄȳ ǰƲǂ recommends for healthy  adults,  the  same  recommendations  can  be  given  here;  always  limit sugar, salt and unhealthy fats/oils when preparing your baby's meals and adopt healthier cooking methods such as boiling, steaming, baking and grilling. Do not add sugar, salt, and spices to the child's food before 12 months of age.

The following section presents examples of nutritious foods to introduce to your baby's diet as well as the cooking/preparation method that will best preserve the foods' nutritive value. The information is presented per food group.

![Picture 274](images/SRC013/picture-274.png)

### VEGETABLES

Broccoli

![Picture 275](images/SRC013/picture-275.png)

Zucchini

Bell Peppers / capsicum (red, yellow, orange or

green)

Cherry tomatoes

![Picture 276](images/SRC013/picture-276.png)

![Picture 277](images/SRC013/picture-277.png)

![Picture 278](images/SRC013/picture-278.png)

This vegetable is high in vitamin C, vitamin K, calcium, ɭɣɻȝɴɴɇɿɝ ȝɞȯ ɴɣɗɿȨɗȳ ʟȨȳɰʲ ǼɄȳ ʟȨȳɰ ʋɇɗɗ Ʉȳɗɭ ɗɣɣɴȳɞ ɻɄȳ baby's bowels, making it easier for them to pass stool. Gently steam broccoli for 5 minutes or roast them in the oven with a little bit of olive oil for 12-20 minutes or until they are soft and tender. You can serve them puréed, by placing them in a blender and adding water if necessary to achieve a smooth consistency. You can also serve them chopped once your child starts self-feeding.

Ƭɣɞɻȝɇɞɴ ɞɣ Ⱦȝɻ ȝɞȯ ɇɴ ɄɇȿɄ ɇɞ ʋȝɻȳɰ ȝɞȯ ʟȨȳɰʲ Ǌɻ ȝɗɴɣ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɴ ɴɇȿɞɇʟȩȝɞɻ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ȝɞɻɇɣʐɇȯȝɞɻɴʳ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞɴ ƫ̼ʳ ɰɇȨɣʠȝʊɇɞʳ folate, vitamin C, vitamin K and minerals, like potassium ȝɞȯ ɝȝɞȿȝɞȳɴȳʲ Ǥɞȳ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ ɝȝɒɣɰ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɣȾ ɇɞȩɣɰɭɣɰȝɻɇɞȿ this veggie into your baby's diet is that it can help improve digestion and reduce the incidence of constipation. Gently steam or boil for 2-4 minutes and chop in small cubes or thin strips. Another way to cook them is to slice them in round coin shapes and sauté them in a pan with a little bit of olive oil until they are soft and tender.

Make sure the only peppers your baby is eating are the mild and sweet peppers (i.e., not the hot ones). Peppers are rich ɇɞ ȝɞɻɇɣʐɇȯȝɞɻɴʳ ʟȨȳɰʳ ȝɞȯ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ Ƭ ˉ̷ ȩɿɭ ɣȾ ɰȳȯ ɭȳɭɭȳɰɴ contains more vitamin C than an orange).

- How you prepare them for your baby depends on the stage of development he/she is in. If your baby is still being spoon-fed, bell peppers are delicious when puréed and super easy to prepare. Just steam them for a few minutes to soften them up and throw them in the blender.
- If your baby has reached the stage where they can ȿɰȝɴɭ ʟɞȿȳɰ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʳ ʑɣɿ ȩȝɞ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɝ ɰȝʋ Ȩȳɗɗ peppers (if they have teeth) in long slices, or slightly steamed if they cannot chew properly.

These are an excellent source of lycopene, vitamins A and C, and a good source of vitamin K, vitamin E and potassium. Serve them raw but cut into halves, quarters, or eighths (depending on how well your baby can chew to avoid chances of choking).

### CEREALS &amp; STARCHY VEGETABLES

Cereals and starchy vegetables provide your baby with a major source of energy (calories) and represent an essential part of a healthy diet to ensure your child's normal growth and development. Cereals and starchy vegetables are excellent sources of complex ȩȝɰȨɣɄʑȯɰȝɻȳɴʳ ʟȨȳɰʳ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞʳ ȝɞȯ ȝ ʋɇȯȳ ɰȝɞȿȳ ɣȾ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞɴ ȝɞȯ ɝɇɞȳɰȝɗɴʲ

The initial foods introduced within this food group are infant cereals and starchy vegetables such as potatoes and peas. You can mix the infant cereal with your breastmilk, water, or formula (if you were already formula feeding your infant). Make sure the cereal is of thin consistency to allow for easy swallowing. As your baby gets older and develops more motor skills, you can increase the thickness.

### LEGUMES

Legumes represent an important food group, and their consumption should be encouraged daily as ɭȳɰ ɻɄȳ ǰȝɻȝɰ Ʋɇȳɻȝɰʑ ǂɿɇȯȳɗɇɞȳɴʲ ǵɇɝɇɗȝɰ ɻɣ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɻʳ ɗȳȿɿɝȳɴ ȝɰȳ ɰɇȩɄ ɇɞ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞʳ ɇɰɣɞʳ and zinc, which makes them a good substitute for these animal foods. They are also an excellent ɴɣɿɰȩȳ ɣȾ ɴɣɗɿȨɗȳ ʟȨȳɰʳ ʋɄɇȩɄ ɇɴ ɇɝɭɣɰɻȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ɝȝɻɿɰȝɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ȿȝɴɻɰɣɇɞɻȳɴɻɇɞȝɗ ɻɰȝȩɻʲ Legumes include but are not limited to chickpeas (hummus and nakhi), and fava beans (bajela and foul mudammes).

### MILK, DAIRY PRODUCTS &amp; ALTERNATIVES

Human milk (or infant formula in certain situations) should be the only type of milk given to infants and young children. Cow's milk as well as goat and camel milk should be avoided until 12 months of age, as young infants cannot digest it. The high concentration of protein and minerals in those milk types can stress your baby's kidneys and cause anemia, fever, or diarrhea. You should also limit giving these ȝɞɇɝȝɗ ɝɇɗɕɴ ɻɣ ʑɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ȯɿɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ʑȳȝɰ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳ ˉɝɣȯɇʟȳȯ ȿɣȝɻ ɝɇɗɕ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝɴ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȿɇʊȳɞ to your baby if recommended by the medical practitioner).

ǘɇɝɇɻɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ȩɣʋ˔ɴ ɝɇɗɕ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ʑȳȝɰ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳ ȯɣȳɴ ɞɣɻ ɞȳȩȳɴɴȝɰɇɗʑ ɝȳȝɞ ɻɄȝɻ ʑɣɿ cannot introduce other dairy products in your child's diet. Hard cheeses, cottage cheese and yogurt can be given to your baby as a protein source but ensure to observe them closely for any reaction after introducing these foods.

![Picture 287](images/SRC013/picture-287.png)

### FISH, POULTRY, MEAT &amp; ALTERNATIVES

Fish, poultry, and meat are excellent sources of protein and essential minerals and should be introduced into your baby's diet after six months of age. As your baby reaches six months of age, iron stores begin to decrease which is why iron and zinc found in protein-rich foods such as meat become crucial.

Iron and Zinc Iron and zinc are essential nutrients to combat the ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɝȳɞɻ ɣȾ ɇɰɣɞ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩʑ ȝɞȯ ɇɰɣɞ˅ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩʑ ȝɞȳɝɇȝʲ ǼɄȳɴȳ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ Ʉȝʊȳ ȝ ɗɣɞȿ˅ɻȳɰɝ ȳʜȳȩɻ ɣɞ ɞȳɿɰɣ˅ developmental behavior. Therefore, proper complementary feeding should include foods rich in iron and zinc to help support the production of red blood cells, to build a strong immunity and foster normal brain development.

![Picture 288](images/SRC013/picture-288.png)

ǖȳȳɭ ɇɞ ɝɇɞȯ ɻɣ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩȳ ɻɄȳ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞ ɴɣɿɰȩȳ ɣɞȳ ȝɻ ȝ ɻɇɝȳʳ ʋȝɇɻɇɞȿ ̹˅̻ ȯȝʑɴ Ȩȳɻʋȳȳɞ ȳȝȩɄ food before introducing a new one, to make sure that your baby did not develop any reaction to these Ⱦɣɣȯɴʲ ƫȳɗɣʋ ȝɰȳ ɴɣɝȳ ɭɰȝȩɻɇȩȝɗ ɻɇɭɴ Ⱦɣɰ ɻɄȳ ɭɰȳɭȝɰȝɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑ ȝɞȯ ɝȳȝɻʴ

- Ǳȳɝɣʊȳ Ⱦȝɻʳ ɴɕɇɞ ȝɞȯ Ȩɣɞȳ Ⱦɰɣɝ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑ ɣɰ ɝȳȝɻ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ȩɣɣɕɇɞȿʲ ƫȳ ȳʐɻɰȳɝȳɗʑ ȩȝɿɻɇɣɿɴ ɻɣ ɰȳɝɣʊȳ ȝɗɗ Ȩɣɞȳɴ ȳɴɭȳȩɇȝɗɗʑ ɻɄȳ ɴɝȝɗɗ ɣɞȳɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ Ⱦɣɿɞȯ ɇɞ ʟɴɄʲ
- Broil, boil, roast or bake these foods and limit frying and deep frying.
- Thoroughly cook these foods to kill any bacteria.
- Once cooked, cut up these foods and purée them to the desired consistency.
- Use a separate blender for your baby's foods, or make sure the blender is thoroughly cleaned before using it to prepare your baby's foods.
- As your baby's feeding skills mature, you no longer need to purée these foods, you can start ɴȳɰʊɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɝ ʟɞȳɗʑ ȩɄɣɭɭȳȯʲ
- ǘɇɝɇɻ ɝɇʐɇɞȿ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞɴʵ ȝɗʋȝʑɴ ɴȳɰʊȳ ɻɄȳɝ ɴȳɭȝɰȝɻȳɗʑ ˉȳɴɭȳȩɇȝɗɗʑ ʋɄȳɞ ʑɣɿ ȝɰȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩɇɞȿ them).

More on Fish Fish is healthy for your child, and it is recommended that ʑɣɿ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɝ ʟɴɄ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɻʋɣ ɻɇɝȳɴ ɭȳɰ ʋȳȳɕʲ Ǉɣʋȳʊȳɰʳ Ȩȳ ȩȝɰȳȾɿɗ ȝɴ ɻɣ ɻɄȳ ɻʑɭȳɴ ɣȾ ʟɴɄ ʑɣɿ ɣʜȳɰ ɴɇɞȩȳ ɴɣɝȳ ɗȝɰȿȳ ʟɴɄ ɝȝʑ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ɄɇȿɄ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑ ɣɰ ɣɻɄȳɰ ȩɣɞɻȝɝɇɞȝɞɻɴʲ Ǌɞ ȿȳɞȳɰȝɗʳ ɣʜȳɰ ɗɣʋ˅ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ seafood (such as anchovies, Spanish mackerel (also known as 'khanad' in Qatar) salmon, sardine, oysters, white ʟɴɄ ȝɞȯ ɻɿɞȝ ˉȩȝɞɞȳȯʳ ɗɇȿɄɻˊʲ ǘɇɝɇɻ ʟɴɄ ɻɄȝɻ ɝȝʑ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ɄɇȿɄ ɗȳʊȳɗɴ ɣȾ ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑ ȝɞȯ ȩɣɞɻȝɝɇɞȝɞɻɴʳ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɻɇɗȳʟɴɄʳ ɴʋɣɰȯʟɴɄ ȝɞȯ ɕɇɞȿ ɝȝȩɕȳɰȳɗʳ ɴɇɞȩȳ ɝȳɰȩɿɰʑ ɝȝʑ ɞȳȿȝɻɇʊȳɗʑ ȝʜȳȩɻ ɻɄȳ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭɝȳɞɻ ɣȾ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ [28] .

Sweetened Beverages Any beverage with high sugar content, such as carbonated ɴɣȾɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɴʳ Ⱦɰɿɇɻ ɒɿɇȩȳɴʳ ɇȩȳȯ ɻȳȝɴʳ ʠȝʊɣɰȳȯ ɝɇɗɕʳ ȳɻȩʲʳ ȝɰȳ ɞɣɻ recommended for children. Consumption of these types of beverages can cause tooth decay and may contribute to being overweight and obese.

Herbal Teas and Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȝɻȳȯ Beverages

The Gulf and Middle Eastern cultures rely heavily on the ȩɣɞɴɿɝɭɻɇɣɞ ɣȾ ɄȳɰȨȝɗ ɻȳȝɴ ȝɞȯ ɻɰȝȯɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȝɻȳȯ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴʲ Ǟȝɞʑ ɭȝɰȳɞɻɴ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɴȳ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ ɻɣ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ believing that they would help with digestion and relaxation; ɴɣɝȳ ɻɰȝȯɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȩɿɴɻɣɝɴ ȝɗɴɣ ȩɗȝɇɝ ɻɄȝɻ ƠɰȝȨɇȩ ȩɣʜȳȳ ɝȝʑ allow the infant to speak at an early age. More research needs to be conducted on the safety of herbal teas and their impact on infants' health and development. Thus, parents should consult a doctor before giving their baby any herbal tea.

Ơɞʑ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ˉɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȩɣʜȳȳʳ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ drinks or carbonated soft drinks) should not be given to ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ɣɰ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞʲ Ƭȝʜȳɇɞȳ ȩȝɞʳ ɇɞ Ⱦȝȩɻʳ ɣʊȳɰɴɻɇɝɿɗȝɻȳ your baby, leading to fussiness and disturbance of sleep. Similarly, tea and cocoa products contain a substance that is ɴɇɝɇɗȝɰ ɻɣ ȩȝʜȳɇɞȳ ȝɞȯ ȝɰȳ ɞɣɻ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯȳȯ Ⱦɣɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ɣɰ children.

![Picture 291](images/SRC013/picture-291.png)

![Picture 292](images/SRC013/picture-292.png)

![Picture 293](images/SRC013/picture-293.png)

![Picture 294](images/SRC013/picture-294.png)

Feeding  practices  in  infancy  may  increase  the  risk  of  early  childhood  caries,  which  are  also known as baby bottle caries. Babies derive comfort from sucking on the bottle, and this may help  them  relax  and  fall  asleep.  However,  you  should  not  give  a  bottle  of  formula,  juice  or any other sweetened beverages to calm your baby or at bedtime since this will lead to teeth demineralization  and,  thus,  tooth  decay [34,  35] .

The American Academy of Pediatric Dentistry and the American Academy of Pediatrics have provided recommendations to prevent early childhood caries; [30, 35] :

- Limit frequent consumption of liquids and solid foods that contain sugar. In particular, avoid ɣʜȳɰɇɞȿ ɴɿȿȝɰ˅ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ Ȩȳʊȳɰȝȿȳɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ȩȝɰȨɣɞȝɻȳȯ ɴɣȾɻ ȯɰɇɞɕɴʳ ɒɿɇȩȳɴʳ ɴʋȳȳɻȳɞȳȯ ɻȳȝʳ and sweetened milk to your baby.
- Ȓɣɿɰ ȨȝȨʑ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ ɴɗȳȳɭ ʋɇɻɄ ȝ Ȩɣɻɻɗȳ ʟɗɗȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ɝɇɗɕ ɣɰ ȝɞʑ ɗɇɯɿɇȯ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞɇɞȿ ɴɿȿȝɰɴʲ
- Your baby should be weaned from the bottle at 12-18 months of age.
- At the age of 12 months, you should be taking your baby to see a dentist. Talk to the ȯȳɞɻɇɴɻ ȝȨɣɿɻ ɻɄȳ ɞȳȳȯ ɻɣ ɭɿɻ ʠɿɣɰɇȯȳ ʊȝɰɞɇɴɄ ɣɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ɻȳȳɻɄ ɰɇȿɄɻ ȝȾɻȳɰ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻɣɣɻɄ emerges.
- Use a gentle brush or a clean, soft cloth to wipe emerging baby teeth and promote good ɣɰȝɗ Ʉʑȿɇȳɞȳʲ ǼɄɇɴ ȩȝɞ Ȩȳ ȯɣɞȳ ɻʋɇȩȳ ȝ ȯȝʑʳ ɇʲȳʲʳ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ɝɣɰɞɇɞȿ ȝȾɻȳɰ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ Ⱦȳȳȯɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ right before bed.

![Picture 295](images/SRC013/picture-295.png)

![Picture 296](images/SRC013/picture-296.png)

Always consult with the doctor before giving your baby any supplements. In most instances, a balanced and diverse diet will meet your child's needs for the various nutrients. Thus, once your ȨȝȨʑ ɇɴ ɻɣɗȳɰȝɻɇɞȿ ȝɞȯ ȝȩȩȳɭɻɇɞȿ ɴɣɗɇȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʳ ɝȝɕȳ ɴɿɰȳ ɻɣ ɣʜȳɰ ɻɄȳɝ ȝ ʊȝɰɇȳɻʑ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ Ⱦɰɣɝ ȝɗɗ the 6 food groups in order to meet their nutritional needs.

- Vitamin D: This vitamin is crucial for healthy bones. The American Academy of Pediatrics recommends  that  all  breastfed  infants  (whether  exclusively  or  partially  breastfed),  and Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ˅Ⱦȳȯ ɇɞȾȝɞɻɴ ʋɄɣ ȩɣɞɴɿɝȳ ɗȳɴɴ ɻɄȝɞ ̶̻̿ ɝǘ ˉ̸̹ ʠɿɇȯ ɣʗˊ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ ɭȳɰ ȯȝʑʳ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ take vitamin D supplements. When your baby starts complementary feeding, you can add the vitamin D drops to puréed food or porridge [36] .
- Iron: Ơɴ ʑɣɿɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ ɴɻȝɰɻɴ ɻɣ ȳȝɻ ɝɣɰȳ ɴɣɗɇȯ Ⱦɣɣȯʳ ɣʜȳɰɇɞȿ ɻɄȳɝ ɇɰɣɞ˅ɰɇȩɄ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ɇɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ ȩȳɰȳȝɗɴʳ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ ɝȳȝɻ ɣɰ Ȩȳȝɞɴ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɻʋɇȩȳ ɭȳɰ ȯȝʑ ʋɇɗɗ Ʉȳɗɭ them meet iron requirements. Speak to the doctor about iron supplements and how long you  should  continue  iron  supplementation  after  your  baby  starts  eating  iron-containing Ⱦɣɣȯɴʲ ǊɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ ɇɴ ȿȳɞȳɰȝɗɗʑ ɇɰɣɞ˅Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯʳ ɴɣ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ˅Ⱦȳȯ ȨȝȨɇȳɴ ɰȝɰȳɗʑ ɞȳȳȯ ȝɞ ɇɰɣɞ supplement [36] .
- Vitamin B12: ȋɇɻȝɝɇɞ ƫ̷̸ ɇɴ ɣɞɗʑ Ⱦɣɿɞȯ ɇɞ ȝɞɇɝȝɗ˅Ȩȝɴȳȯ ɭɰɣȯɿȩɻɴ ɴɿȩɄ ȝɴ ʟɴɄʳ ɭɣɿɗɻɰʑʳ meat, eggs and dairy. Most children do not have any problem with this nutrient. However, for vegan moms who are breastfeeding their baby and who plan to introduce only plantbased  foods  into  their  child's  diet,  there  will  be  a  need  for  vitamin  B12  supplements. ȋȳȿȳɻȝɰɇȝɞ ȨȝȨɇȳɴ ʋɄɣ ȝɰȳ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ˅Ⱦȳȯ ɝȝʑ ȿȳɻ ɻɄȳɇɰ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞ ƫ̷̸ Ⱦɰɣɝ ȝ ɴɭȳȩɇȝɗ Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ formula, which is most often soy-based [36] .
- Other vitamins: ƫȝȨɇȳɴ ʋɄɣ ɻȝɕȳ ɝɣɰȳ ɻɄȝɞ ̶̶̻ ɝǘ ˉ̷̼˅̷̽ ʠɿɇȯ ɣʗˊ ɣȾ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰɝɿɗȝ ɭȳɰ day should not be given any other vitamin supplements. This is because infant formula is Ⱦɣɰɻɇʟȳȯ ʋɇɻɄ ɝȝɞʑ ʊɇɻȝɝɇɞɴ [37] .

![Picture 297](images/SRC013/picture-297.png)

![Picture 298](images/SRC013/picture-298.png)

## What is a food allergy?

It is an abnormal body response to a certain food or beverage [38] .

## How can I reduce the risk of my child having a food allergy?

You cannot prevent your child from developing a certain food allergy, but studies have shown that following the below recommendations can prevent or delay food allergies in infants:

- ƫɰȳȝɴɻȾȳȳȯ ʑɣɿɰ ɇɞȾȝɞɻ Ⱦɣɰ ȝɻ ɗȳȝɴɻ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɴɇʐ ɝɣɞɻɄɴʲ
- Do  not  begin  complementary  feeding  before  six  months  of  age [38] (unless  medically prescribed  by  your  healthcare  provider).

## Allergies to infant formula:

Breastmilk is the best milk for your baby. If for any reason the baby is switched to cow's milkbased infant formula, and you found out that the baby is allergic to it then consult the doctor or dietitian for advice on other options such as soy milk. If the infant was also found to be allergic to soy milk, then a special hypoallergenic formula is usually recommended.

There is no evidence that soy or goat-based formula will reduce the risk of developing allergic diseases in healthy infants.

## What are the most common allergens in the diet?

When infants are introduced to complementary feeding, some may develop allergies to certain foods. Around 90% of all food allergies are caused by the following types of foods [38, 39] :

- Animal-based milk such as cow's milk
- Eggs
- Peanuts
- Soy
- Tree nuts
- Fish
- ǵɄȳɗɗʟɴɄ ˉȩɰɿɴɻȝȩȳȝɞɴ ȝɞȯ ɝɣɗɗɿɴȩɴˊ
- Wheat
- Seeds

![Picture 299](images/SRC013/picture-299.png)

When introducing foods to the baby, especially those foods that are known to cause allergic reactions (as listed above), make sure to introduce each type of food, one at a time, and in small amounts, so you will be able to notice any reactions or symptoms in your baby [39] . Do not be scared to introduce these types of foods to your child. In fact, there is no need to limit any of ɻɄȳɴȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴʳ ɿɞɗȳɴɴ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ɇɴ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȩʲ Ƭɿɻɻɇɞȿ ɣʜ ȝ ɝȝɒɣɰ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȿɰɣɿɭ ȩȝɞ ɗȳȝȯ ɻɣ ɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴʳ ɴɣ ȝɗʋȝʑɴ ȩɣɞɴɿɗɻ ʋɇɻɄ ɻɄȳ ȯɣȩɻɣɰ ȨȳȾɣɰȳ ȳɗɇɝɇɞȝɻɇɞȿ ȝɞʑ Ⱦɣɣȯ Ⱦɰɣɝ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ diet [39] .

Some individuals can have allergies for food additives including colors and preservatives, but allergic reactions from ordinary food items are usually more common [39] .

## What are the symptoms of food allergies?

An allergic reaction can begin within minutes to an hour after ingesting the food or beverage that ɻɄȳ ȩɄɇɗȯ ɇɴ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȩ ɻɣʲ ƶȝȩɄ ȩɄɇɗȯ ɝȝʑ ȳʐɭȳɰɇȳɞȩȳ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿʑ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻɗʑ ȝɞȯ ɝɇȿɄɻ Ʉȝʊȳ ɣɞȳ ɣɰ more symptoms. The most common symptoms of food allergy are [38] :

- Diarrhea
- Vomiting
- Cough
- Swelling
- Dry and itchy skin (Eczema)
- Itching or swelling of the lips, tongue, or mouth
- Itching or tightness in the throat
- Skin rashes
- Sore, red and/or itchy eyes
- Runny or blocked nose
- Lowered blood pressure
- Stomach cramps and pain
- Red itchy bumps on the skin (Hives)
- Trouble breathing or shortness of breath
- Wheezing (coarse sound when breathing)

![Picture 300](images/SRC013/picture-300.png)

In  some  cases,  severe  allergic  reaction  may  occur,  known  as  'anaphylaxis';  this  can  be  lifethreating [39,  40] ʳ  ȝɞȯ  ɇɴ  ɿɴɿȝɗɗʑ  ɝȝɞɇȾȳɴɻȳȯ  Ȩʑ  ȨɰȳȝɻɄɇɞȿ  ȯɇʝȩɿɗɻɇȳɴ  ȝɞȯ  Ⱦȝȩȳ  ɴʋȳɗɗɇɞȿʲ  ǊȾ  ɴɿȩɄ ɴʑɝɭɻɣɝɴ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭʳ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ ʋɇɗɗ ɞȳȳȯ ɇɝɝȳȯɇȝɻȳ ɝȳȯɇȩȝɗ ȝɻɻȳɞɻɇɣɞʲ Ǽɰȳȳ ɞɿɻɴʳ ɭȳȝɞɿɻɴʳ ʟɴɄ ȝɞȯ ɴɄȳɗɗʟɴɄ ɿɴɿȝɗɗʑ ȩȝɿɴȳ ɻɄȳ ɝɣɴɻ ɴȳʊȳɰȳ ɰȳȝȩɻɇɣɞɴ ȩɣɝɭȝɰȳȯ ɻɣ ɣɻɄȳɰ ȩɣɝɝɣɞ ȝɗɗȳɰȿȳɞɴ [38] . Take care when introducing new foods and closely observe whether your child develops any allergic  reaction  to  a  newly  introduced  food.

## How do we diagnose a food allergy?

A diagnosis should be done by a doctor. You should not make the diagnosis yourself to limit any unnecessary dietary restrictions. In case a food allergy is diagnosed, you must have a dietary plan to replace the eliminated food items, and you also need to have a plan in case of emergency [41]. If your infant/child develops any of the typical allergy-related symptoms after eating any type of food or beverage, you should immediately contact the doctor.

![Picture 301](images/SRC013/picture-301.png)

## Nutritional concerns in infants and children with food allergies

Ǟɣɴɻ ȩɄɇɗȯɰȳɞ ȯȳʊȳɗɣɭ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɻʋɣ ʑȳȝɰɴ ɣȾ ɗɇȾȳʳ ʋɄɇȩɄ ɇɴ ȝ ȩɰɿȩɇȝɗ ȿɰɣʋɻɄ ɭȳɰɇɣȯʲ Therefore,  it  is  important  to  keep  in  mind  that  eliminating  a  certain  food  group  (because  of ȝɞ ȝɗɗȳɰȿʑˊ ʋɇɻɄɣɿɻ ɰȳɭɗȝȩɇɞȿ ɇɻ ʋɇɻɄ ɻɄȳ ɰɇȿɄɻ ȝɗɻȳɰɞȝɻɇʊȳ ȩȝɞ ȩȝɿɴȳ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ ȝɞȯ growth problems in your child [42] .

For example, milk, eggs and soy are good sources of fat and protein. Eliminating these food items Ȩȳȩȝɿɴȳ ɣȾ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ ɝɇȿɄɻ ɗȳȝȯ ɻɣ ɇɞɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ ɭɰɣɻȳɇɞ ȝɞȯ Ⱦȝɻ ɇɞ ɻɄȳ ȯɇȳɻ ɇȾ ɻɄȳʑ are not replaced by other good sources [42] .

- Ʋɇȳɻɴ ʋɇɻɄ ɇɞɴɿʝȩɇȳɞɻ ȝɝɣɿɞɻɴ ɣȾ Ⱦȝɻ ȯɣ ɞɣɻ ɿɴɿȝɗɗʑ ȩɣɞɻȝɇɞ ȝȯȳɯɿȝɻȳ ȳɞȳɰȿʑ ˉȩȝɗɣɰɇȳɴˊ ȝɞȯ certain vitamins, which can lead to poor growth.
- Diets that are low in protein may also lead to protein malnutrition and hence poor growth [42] .

Another example is wheat. This cereal provides the body with carbohydrates, which are known to be an important source of energy for your child's body, and particularly the brain. Wheat also contains important vitamins and minerals. So if the child is allergic to wheat, other alternative ɴɄɣɿɗȯ Ȩȳ ɇɞȩɗɿȯȳȯ ɇɞ ʑɣɿɰ ȩɄɇɗȯ˔ɴ ȯɇȳɻ ɻɣ ɗɇɝɇɻ ȝɞʑ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ [42] .

Another potential challenge is that children that have one or more food allergies might experience some dietary behavior problems more than other children. For example, they may develop 'food aversion' (i.e., refusing certain types of food) or a state of anxiety about food, which again can lead to inadequate food intake [42] .

This is why it is very important that the doctor monitors the growth of infants and children with food allergies [42] . It is also important that the doctor or dietitian provide the right alternatives to ɰȳɭɗȝȩȳ ɻɄȳ ȳɗɇɝɇɞȝɻȳȯ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ȝɞȯ ɭɰȳʊȳɞɻ ɞɿɻɰɇɻɇɣɞȝɗ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ [42] .  The doctor may sometimes prescribe supplements when needed [42] .

## What should I do if my child was diagnosed with a food allergy?

ǼɄȳɰȳ ɇɴ ɞɣ ȩɿɰȳ Ⱦɣɰ Ⱦɣɣȯ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴʵ ɻɄȳ ʟɰɴɻ ɴɻȳɭ ɻɄȝɻ ɝɿɴɻ Ȩȳ ȯɣɞȳ ɇɴ ɻɣ ȩɣɝɭɗȳɻȳɗʑ ȝʊɣɇȯ ɻɄȳ food or beverage that causes the allergic reaction [38, 40, 41, 43] . It is therefore important to get the help of a dietitian to plan an adequate, healthy and balanced diet for your child, to avoid any ɝɇȩɰɣɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ɣɰ ɝȝȩɰɣɞɿɻɰɇȳɞɻ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ ȩȝɿɴȳȯ Ȩʑ ȳɗɇɝɇɞȝɻɇɞȿ ȩȳɰɻȝɇɞ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ [43] .  Below are some practical tips that can help you in managing your child's food allergy:

- Check with your dietitian and doctor to  identify food alternatives or nutritional supplements ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȯȳʟȩɇȳɞȩɇȳɴ [38] .
- Ơɗʋȝʑɴ ɰȳȝȯ  Ⱦɣɣȯ  ɗȝȨȳɗɴ  ȝɞȯ  ɻɄȳ  ɗɇɴɻ  ɣȾ  ɇɞȿɰȳȯɇȳɞɻɴ  ȨȳȾɣɰȳ  ɣʜȳɰɇɞȿ  ʑɣɿɰ  ȩɄɇɗȯ  ȝɞʑ  ɞȳʋ item [41] .
- Educate your family (at home) and teachers (in the nursery) about your child's allergies and what to do in case of an emergency [41] .

![Picture 302](images/SRC013/picture-302.png)

- If  the doctor has prescribed any medications in case of an allergic reaction, always keep those medications at hand [38] .
- ƶȝɰɗʑ  ȝɞȯ  ɯɿɇȩɕ  ɇȯȳɞɻɇʟȩȝɻɇɣɞ  ɣȾ  ɻɄȳ  ɴɇȿɞɴ  ȝɞȯ  ɴʑɝɭɻɣɝɴ  ȩȝɞ  ɭɰȳʊȳɞɻ  ɝɣɰȳ  ɴȳɰɇɣɿɴ complications  caused  by  food  allergies [40] .

ǵɣɝȳ ȯɣȩɻɣɰɴ ɝȝʑ ɰȳȩɣɝɝȳɞȯ ɰȳɇɞɻɰɣȯɿȩɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ɴɭȳȩɇʟȩ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɄȝɻ Ʉȝʊȳ ȩȝɿɴȳȯ ɻɄȳ ȝɗɗȳɰȿɇȳɴ after a certain amount of time to evaluate whether the child has outgrown the allergy. Some allergies may in fact be outgrown with time, and the foods may end up being tolerated after reaching the age of three or four years old. This must be done under the doctor's supervision [38] .

## Tips when dining out of the house:

As a parent of a child with one or more food allergies, eating out of the house can be challenging. The following tips can help you:

- Check the menu online before going to the restaurant.
- Read and/or ask about the ingredients before ordering any dish.
- Let the server be aware of your child's allergy and ensure there is no cross-contamination when preparing your child's dish.
- ǘɇɝɇɻʳ ɇȾ ɭɣɴɴɇȨɗȳʳ Ȩɿʜȳɻ˅ɴɻʑɗȳ ɰȳɴɻȝɿɰȝɞɻɴ ɻɣ ȝʊɣɇȯ ȝɞʑ ȩɰɣɴɴ˅ȩɣɞɻȝɝɇɞȝɻɇɣɞ ɻɄȝɻ ȩȝɞ Ʉȝɭɭȳɞ Ⱦɰɣɝ ɿɴɇɞȿ ɻɄȳ ɴȝɝȳ ɿɻȳɞɴɇɗɴ Ⱦɣɰ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ ȯɇɴɄȳɴʲ
- ǘɇɝɇɻ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɄȝɻ ȝɰȳ ȩɣɣɕȳȯ ɇɞ ɣɇɗʳ ȝɴ ɻɄȳʑ ɝȝʑ ɿɴȳ ɻɄȳ ɴȝɝȳ ɣɇɗ ɻɣ Ⱦɰʑ ɴȳʊȳɰȝɗ ȯɇʜȳɰȳɞɻ dishes [38] .

![Picture 303](images/SRC013/picture-303.png)

## Food allergy card:

Having a food allergy card can help your child and especially help the people around them (if you ȝɰȳ ɞɣɻ ȝɰɣɿɞȯˊ Ȩȳ ȝʋȝɰȳ ɣȾ ɻɄȳ Ⱦɣɣȯɴ ɻɄȝɻ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ ɞɣɻ Ȩȳ ɣʜȳɰȳȯʲ ǼɄȳ ȩȝɰȯ ɴɄɣɿɗȯ Ȩȳ ʋɇɻɄ ɻɄȳ child at all times, including at the nursery, when the child is visiting a friend, at a party and/or in a restaurant. Inform any adult in charge that the child has this card, such as the teacher at the nursery or the parents of the friend that your child is visiting [38].

The food allergy card should contain the following information:

- The name of the child
- Food items your child is allergic to
- What to do in case of emergency
- Parent's name and phone number

This card can be easily done at home (below is the card template).

![Picture 304](images/SRC013/picture-304.png)

## Food Safety Considerations

Complementary feeding (i.e., solid and soft foods) should be introduced at six months of age. Babies have a higher risk of food poisoning due to their immature immune systems. Therefore, it is crucial to practice good hygiene and proper food handling to avoid any cases of food poisoning. Keep  these  simple  vital  tips  in  mind  to  ensure  that  you  and  your  baby  will  have  a  fruitful experience  when  introducing  solid  and  soft  foods [4] .

- Always wash your hands thoroughly before preparing the food and before feeding your baby.
- Always wash your baby's hands before feeding as they will uncontrollably want to feed themselves.
- Always use clean utensils and surfaces when preparing food and when feeding your baby.
- Always ensure that food is cooked thoroughly.
- Always store food safely in airtight containers and appropriate temperatures.

By paying close attention to hygienic practices, you can lower the incidence of gastrointestinal illnesses such as diarrhea. Refer to Appendix 2.

![Picture 305](images/SRC013/picture-305.png)

![Picture 306](images/SRC013/picture-306.png)

## Physical Activity Recommendations for Infants and Young Children

It is important for the development of your child to have some form of physical activity. This can be achieved in various ways:

### For infants (&lt;12 months) [44, 45] :

An exercise regimen for infants is impractical: infants do not follow instructions. However, it is crucial to facilitate some form of physical activity daily.

Interact often with your baby and provide opportunities for 'tummy time'.

- Tummy time is when you place your baby on their stomach while they are awake, and only when supervised.
- Tummy time can help develop strength in your baby's neck, arms and back.
- You can start your baby's tummy time 'training' as soon as you leave the hospital. During ɻɄȳ ʊȳɰʑ ʟɰɴɻ ȯȝʑɴ ȝɞȯ ʋȳȳɕɴ ȝɇɝ Ⱦɣɰ ̹˅̺ ɴɄɣɰɻ ȯȝɇɗʑ ɴȳɴɴɇɣɞɴʲ Ơȩȩɿɝɿɗȝɻȳ ȝ ɝȝʐɇɝɿɝ ɣȾ 10-15 minutes per day. As your baby grows and gains strength you should extend the time gradually.
- Initiate tummy time when your baby is energetic following a nap or a diaper change.
- Create a safe environment such as a playmat or clean towel. You might want to add some toys to stimulate your baby's attention.
- Once your baby starts enjoying this position gradually increase the session frequency and duration throughout the day. If your baby is not able to crawl yet, aim for a minimum of 30 minutes per day in several 'tummy time' sessions.
- As good as tummy time is for your baby, never put your baby to sleep on their stomach. ǵɗȳȳɭɇɞȿ  ɣɞ  ɻɄȳ  ɴɻɣɝȝȩɄ  ɇɴ  ȝ  ɴɇȿɞɇʟȩȝɞɻ  ɰɇɴɕ  Ⱦȝȩɻɣɰ  Ⱦɣɰ  ɴɿȯȯȳɞ  ɇɞȾȝɞɻ  ȯȳȝɻɄ  ɴʑɞȯɰɣɝȳ (SIDS).

For a healthy development, avoid 'locking up' your child in prams, strollers, or highchairs for more than 60 minutes. Your baby develops daily and needs to start exploring their surroundings.

Make sure to allow some opportunities for:

- Floor-based play.
- Reaching out and grabbing objects.
- Crawling.

![Picture 307](images/SRC013/picture-307.png)

### For toddlers (1-2 years) [44-46] :

Toddlers this age should engage in at least 3 hours of physical activity throughout the day (not all at once). This should be achieved through fun activities that promote exploration and discovery. Below are some tips for you and your toddler:

- Include  a  wider  variety  of  physical  activity  options  through  active  play  (e.g.,  standing, rolling,  playing,  and  moving  around).
- When the child starts walking, encourage them to walk more, and move around the house.
- When the child can balance well, encourage them to take part in activities such as running, jumping, climbing, swimming, bouncing, catching, kicking, ball games etc.

### ȌɄȝɻ ȝɰȳ ɻɄȳ Ȩȳɞȳʟɻɴ ɣȾ ɭɄʑɴɇȩȝɗ ȝȩɻɇʊɇɻʑ Ⱦɣɰ ɝʑ ȩɄɇɗȯʹ [44, 45]

### Physical activity helps infants and toddlers to:

- Develop locomotor and movement skills
- Develop strong bones and muscles
- Maintain a healthy weight
- Improve social and intellectual skills
- Adopting physical activity as a habit early in life

### Safety tips [44] :

- Activities should be based on physical maturity rather than chronological age to reduce the risk of injury, because each child grows at their own pace.
- Frequency, intensity, and time should gradually progress as the child develops.
- Supervise your child to prevent at home-accidents.

### Limiting sedentary behavior (sitting) [44, 45] :

Reducing  sedentary  behavior  (sitting  or  restrained)  during  your  child's  waking  hours  is recommended  to  support  healthy  growth  and  development.

- Do not allow any screen time for children under the age of two years.
- Do not restrain your child for more than one hour at a time (i.e., in a highchair or stroller).
- Integrate active fun activities in the child's everyday routines.

## APPENDIX 1: CHILD'S DAILY RECOMMENDATIONS FROM THE DIFFERENT FOOD GROUPS
